  Option7.Name = "optDesigner"

  Arial, 1, 9, 6, 15, 12, 32, 3, 0
  Tahoma, 0, 9, 5, 14, 12, 29, 2, 0
  Comic Sans MS, 3, 8, 7, 15, 12, 37, 3, 0
  Verdana, 3, 8, 6, 13, 11, 25, 2, 0

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE calcpreco
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE calcpreco
Local Custo, Moec, Venda, Moev, Fator, fPeso, Ideal

Do Case
	Case (ThisForm.TpCalcp = 3)
		ThisForm.CalcPreMoe

	Case (ThisForm.TpCalcp = 6)
		ThisForm.CalcPreCPM

	Otherwise
		Select crSigPrCpo

		ThisForm.TotalGrupocv
		ThisForm.TotalGrupo
		Thisform.TotalPlan

		oPagC = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgComposicao

		Custo  = crSigCdPro.Pcuss
		FPeso  = crSigCdPro.PesoMs * crSigCdPro.Fcustos
		Fator  = crSigCdPro.Margems
		Feitio = crSigCdPro.Pftios
		FeitioC= CrSigCdPro.Pftiocs
		cFtioV = CrSigCdPro.cftios
		nPeso  = crSigCdPro.PesoMs

		pGru   = crSigCdPro.CGrus
		ThisForm.poDataMgr.Requery('crSigCdGrp')
		Go Top In crSigCdGrp
		ThisForm.OrdGrade = Int(Val(Substr(crSigCdGrp.CfgGerGprs, 6, 1)))

		If CrSigCdGrp.MarkAplics <> 0 And CrSigCdGrp.MoeMrkaps <> ' ' And CrSigCdGrp.TpCalcPs <> 2
			Replace Moevs With CrSigCdGrp.MoeMrkaps In CrSigCdPro
		Endif

		ThisForm.Podatamgr.Cursorquery('SigPrFti','CrFtio','Cods',cFtioV)

		ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdMoe', 'crMoe', 'CMoes', crSigCdPro.Moecs)
		Go Top In crMoe
		If Not Empty(crMoe.Moeqs)
			m.Moedas = crMoe.Moeqs
			_Qtdeqs = Iif(crMoe.Qtdeqs=0, 1, crMoe.Qtdeqs)
		Else
			m.Moedas = crSigCdPro.Moecs
			_Qtdeqs = 1
		ENDIF

		Moec = fBuscarCotacao(m.Moedas, DateTime(), ThisForm.poDataMgr) * _qtdeqs
		
		ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdMoe', 'crMoe', 'CMoes', crSigCdPro.Moepcs)
		Go Top In crMoe
		If Not Empty(crMoe.Moeqs)
			m.Moedas = crMoe.Moeqs
			_Qtdeqs = Iif(crMoe.Qtdeqs=0, 1, crMoe.Qtdeqs)
		Else
			m.Moedas = crSigCdPro.Moepcs
			_Qtdeqs = 1
		EndIf
		Moep  = fBuscarCotacao(m.Moedas, DateTime(), ThisForm.poDataMgr) * _qtdeqs

		ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdMoe', 'crMoe', 'CMoes', crSigCdPro.Moevs)
		Go Top In crMoe
		If Not Empty(crMoe.Moeqs)
			m.Moedas = crMoe.Moeqs
			_Qtdeqs = Iif(crMoe.Qtdeqs=0, 1, crMoe.Qtdeqs)
		Else
			m.Moedas = crSigCdPro.Moevs
			_Qtdeqs = 1
		EndIf
		Moev = fBuscarCotacao(m.Moedas,DateTime(), ThisForm.poDataMgr) * _qtdeqs

		ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdMoe', 'crMoe', 'CMoes', crSigCdPro.MoeCusfs)
		Go Top In crMoe
		If Not Empty(crMoe.Moeqs)
			m.Moedas = crMoe.Moeqs
			_Qtdeqs = Iif(crMoe.Qtdeqs=0, 1, crMoe.Qtdeqs)
		Else
			m.Moedas = crSigCdPro.Moecusfs
			_Qtdeqs = 1
		EndIf

		IF ThisForm.TpCalcp = 7		&& mena - 03/08/2017 - calcula preco pela cotaçăo digitada
			Moecf = crSigcdpro.cotaCalcp
		ELSE
			Moecf = fBuscarCotacao(m.Moedas, DateTime(), ThisForm.poDataMgr) * _qtdeqs
		ENDIF

		ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdMoe', 'crMoe', 'CMoes', crSigCdPro.Moedas)
		Go Top In crMoe
		If Not Empty(crMoe.Moeqs)
			m.Moedas = crMoe.Moeqs
			_Qtdeqs = Iif(crMoe.Qtdeqs=0, 1, crMoe.Qtdeqs)
		Else
			m.Moedas = crSigCdPro.Moedas
			_Qtdeqs = 1
		EndIf
		Moeda = fBuscarCotacao(m.Moedas,DateTime(), ThisForm.poDataMgr) * _qtdeqs

		ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdMoe', 'crMoe', 'CMoes', crSigCdPro.Mftios)
		Go Top In crMoe
		If Not Empty(crMoe.Moeqs)
			m.Moedas = crMoe.Moeqs
			_Qtdeqs = Iif(crMoe.Qtdeqs=0, 1, crMoe.Qtdeqs)
		Else
			m.Moedas = crSigCdPro.Mftios
			_Qtdeqs = 1
		EndIf

		IF ThisForm.TpCalcp = 7		&& mena - 03/08/2017 - calcula preco pela cotaçăo digitada
			Moeft = crSigcdpro.cotaCalcp
		ELSE
			Moeft = fBuscarCotacao(m.Moedas,DateTime(), ThisForm.poDataMgr) * _qtdeqs
		ENDIF

		If (crSigCdPro.mftios <> crSigCdPro.MoeCusFs)
			Feitio = Feitio * Moeft / Moecf
		EndIf

		If (crSigCdPro.Moepcs <> crSigCdPro.MoeCusFs)
			FeitioC = FeitioC * Moep / Moecf
		EndIf

		If Not Empty(crSigCdGrp.CodCols)
			Custof = crSigCdPro.Fcustos
		Else
			If (crSigCdPro.Moecs <> crSigCdPro.MoeCusFs)
				Custof = Custo * Moec / Moecf
			Else
				Custof = Custo
			EndIf
			Custof = Custof + FeitioC
				
			If (crSigCdPaC.CalcCusts = 2) and ThisForm.TpCalcp <> 7		&& se = 7 năo faz esse calculo && Năo Usar o Peso No Cálculo do Custo
				If (crSigCdPro.Moepcs <> crSigCdPro.moecusfs)
					Custof = Custof * Iif(crSigCdPro.Fcustos = 0, 1, crSigCdPro.Fcustos * Moep / Moecf)
				Else
					Custof = Custof * Iif(crSigCdPro.Fcustos = 0, 1, crSigCdPro.Fcustos)
				EndIf
			Else
				If (crSigCdPro.Moepcs <> crSigCdPro.moecusfs)
					Custof = Custof + (FPeso * Moep / Moecf )
				Else
					Custof = Custof + FPeso
				EndIf
			EndIf
		EndIf
		
		If Custof <> 0
			Custof=ThisForm.Variacaocusto(Custof)
		EndIf 
		
		If Custof <> 0
			oPagC.getcustof.Value = Custof
		Endif

		If Not Empty(cFtioV) And CrFtio.Acrescs = 0 And CrFtio.Valors = 0 And CrFtio.tpftios <> 3
			fator = 0
		Endif

		If (crSigCdPro.MoeCusFs <> crSigCdPro.Moedas)
			Ideal = (Custof + Feitio) * Moecf / Moeda * Iif(Fator=0,1,Fator)
		Else
			Ideal = (Custof + Feitio ) * Iif(Fator=0,1,Fator)
		EndIf

		If Not Empty(cFtioV) And CrFtio.Acrescs = 0 And CrFtio.Valors = 0 And (CrFtio.TpFtios <> 3 Or oPagC.GetMargem.Value = 0 )
			oPagC.GetMargem.Value = Iif(CustoF = 0, 0 , Round(Ideal / Custof,6))
			oPagC.Getmargem.Refresh
		Endif

		With oPagC.getPvideal
			Go Top In crSigCdPam
			.Value = Ideal
			.Refresh
		EndWith

		If CrSigCdGrp.TpCalcPs = 4 && Custo * Feitio
			IdealCv = custo * CrSigCdPro.MarkupA
		Else
			IdealCv = oPagC.getPvideal.Value
		EndIf

		* Arredondamento do Preço Ideal
		If Not Eof('crSigCdGrp') And crSigCdGrp.Arredcs <> 0 And CrSigCdGrp.TpCalcPs <> 2

			_FatArred = crSigCdGrp.Arredcs
			_Soma = _FatArred
			Do While (_Soma < IdealCv)
				_Soma = _Soma + _FatArred
			Enddo
			IdealCv = _Soma

			Idealcv = fArredondamento(Idealcv, ThisForm.poDataMgr)

		EndIf

		oPagC.getPvideal.Value = IdealCv
		oPagC.getPvideal.Refresh

		If (CrSigCdGrp.MarkAplics <> 0 And CrSigCdGrp.MoeMrkaps <> ' ' And CrSigCdGrp.TpCalcPs <> 2) or (CrSigCdPro.MarkupA <> 0 and CrSigCdGrp.TpCalcPs = 4)
			If CrSigCdGrp.TpCalcPs = 4 && Custo * Feitio
				oPagC.GetPven.Value = custo * CrSigCdPro.MarkupA
			Else
				oPagC.GetPven.Value = IdealCv * CrSigCdGrp.MarkAplics
			EndIf

			If crSigCdGrp.Arredcs <> 0

				Pvenda = oPagC.getPven.Value
				
				_FatArred = crSigCdGrp.Arredcs
				_Soma = _FatArred
				Do While (_Soma < pVenda)
					_Soma = _Soma + _FatArred
				Enddo
				pVenda = _Soma
				oPagC.GetPven.Value = pVenda
			EndIf
		EndIf
		
		If Type([CrSigCdGrp.VendPeso])=[N] And CrSigCdGrp.VendPeso = 1 And Not Empty(crSigCdPro.CodFinP)
			ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery([SigCdFip],[LocalCdFip],[Cods], crSigCdPro.CodFinP)
			If Not Used([LocalCdFip])
				=MessageBox([Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!], 16, [Falha na Conexăo (CursorQuery - LocalCdFip)])
				Return .f.
			EndIf
			If Type([LocalCdFip.VendPeso])=[N] And LocalCdFip.VendPeso = 1
				oPagC.GetPven.Value = nPeso
			EndIf 
		EndIf 
		
		* Calcular o Markup Aplicado
		oPagC.getMarkupA.Value = Iif(oPagC.GetCustoF.Value=0,0,Round((oPagC.getPVen.Value * Moev) / (oPagC.getCustoF.Value * Moecf), 3))
		oPagC.getMarkupA.Refresh
EndCase

Select crSigCdPro
* Fim *********************************************************************************

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE totalgrupo
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE totalgrupo
Private pPro, pDat, pHor

Zap In TotGrupo
Zap In TotGrupo2

pPro = Iif(Empty(crSigCdPro.CPros), Replicate(Chr(254), 14), crSigCdPro.CPros)

If ThisForm.Tipo2
	pDat = Iif(Empty(crSigCdPro.DataAlts), fDtoSQL({}), crSigCdPro.DataAlts)
	pHor = crSigCdPro.HoraAlts

	Select Cgrus, Moeds, pCompos, Qtds From crSigPrCp2 into cursor crtmp

	Select crTmp
	Scan
		Select TotGrupo
		Set Order To GruMoe
		Seek crTmp.Cgrus + crTmp.Moeds
		If Eof()
			Valgr = (CrTmp.Qtds * crTmp.Pcompos)
			Insert Into TotGrupo (Grupo, ValGrupo, Moeda) Values (crTmp.Cgrus, Valgr, crTmp.Moeds)
		Else
			Replace ValGrupo With ValGrupo + (crTmp.Qtds * crTmp.Pcompos) IN totgrupo
		EndIf

		Select TotGrupo2
		Set Order To GruMoe
		Seek crTmp.Cgrus + crTmp.Moeds
		If Eof()
			Valgr = (CrTmp.Qtds * crTmp.Pcompos)
			Insert Into TotGrupo2 (Grupo, ValGrupo, Moeda) Values (crTmp.Cgrus, Valgr, crTmp.Moeds)
		Else
			Replace ValGrupo With ValGrupo + (crTmp.Qtds * crTmp.Pcompos) IN totgrupo2
		EndIf
	EndScan
Else
	If ThisForm.TemTipos And ThisForm.TempTipos
		Select Cgrus, Moeds, pCompos, Iif(chkInstalas=2, Pesos, Qtds) as Qtds ;
		  From crSigPrCpo Where TpCalcCus = 1 into cursor crtmp
	Else
		Select Cgrus, Moeds, pCompos, Iif(chkInstalas=2, Pesos, Qtds) as Qtds ;
		  From crSigPrCpo Into cursor crtmp
	EndIf
	
	Select crTmp
	Scan
		ThisForm.Podatamgr.cursorquery('SigCdGrp','TmpGru','Cgrus',CrTmp.Cgrus,[cvestims])
		Select TotGrupo
		Set Order To GruMoe
		Seek crTmp.Cgrus + crTmp.Moeds
		If Eof()
			Valgr = (crTmp.Qtds * crTmp.pCompos)
			Insert Into TotGrupo (Grupo, ValGrupo, Moeda, Estimado ) Values ;
					(crTmp.Cgrus, Valgr, crTmp.Moeds, TmpGru.cvestims )
		Else
			Replace ValGrupo With ValGrupo + (crTmp.Qtds * crTmp.pCompos) IN totgrupo
		EndIf
	EndScan
	
	If ThisForm.TemTipos And ThisForm.TempTipos
		Select Cgrus, Moeds, pCompos, Iif(chkInstalas=2, Pesos, Qtds) as Qtds ;
		  From crSigPrCpo ;
		 Where ((TpCalcCus = 1) And Tipos = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgCusto.cmbTipos.Value) ;
		  Into cursor crtmp
	Else
		Select Cgrus, Moeds, pCompos, Iif(chkInstalas=2, Pesos, Qtds) as Qtds From crSigPrCpo Into cursor crtmp
	EndIf

	Select crTmp
	Scan
		ThisForm.Podatamgr.cursorquery('SigCdGrp','TmpGru','Cgrus',CrTmp.Cgrus,[cvestims])
		Select TotGrupo2
		Set Order To GruMoe
		Seek crTmp.Cgrus + crTmp.Moeds
		If Eof()
			Valgr = (crTmp.Qtds * crTmp.pCompos)
			Insert Into TotGrupo2 (Grupo, ValGrupo, Moeda, Estimado ) Values ;
					(crTmp.Cgrus, Valgr, crTmp.Moeds, TmpGru.cvestims )
		Else
			Replace ValGrupo With ValGrupo + (crTmp.Qtds * crTmp.pCompos) IN TotGrupo2
		EndIf
	EndScan

	Select TotGrupo
	Locate For Estimado = 1
	If Not Eof()
		If crSigCdPro.Moedas = ' ' And InList(ThisForm.PcEscolha,'INSERIR','ALTERAR')
			Replace Moedas with MoeCs in CrSigCdPro
		EndIf

		ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdMoe', 'crMoe', 'CMoes', crSigCdPro.Moedas)
		Go Top In crMoe
		If Not Empty(crMoe.Moeqs)
			m.Moedas = crMoe.Moeqs
			_Qtdeqs = Iif(crMoe.Qtdeqs=0, 1, crMoe.Qtdeqs)
		Else
			m.Moedas = crSigCdPro.Moedas
			_Qtdeqs = 1
		EndIf
		_Moeda  = fBuscarCotacao(m.Moedas, DateTime(), ThisForm.poDataMgr) * _qtdeqs

		_VlrT = 0
		Scan
			If Estimado = 1
				If TotGrupo.Moeda <> crSigCdPro.Moedas
					ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdMoe', 'crMoe', 'CMoes', TotGrupo.Moeda)
					Go Top In crMoe
					If Not Empty(crMoe.Moeqs)
						m.Moedas = crMoe.Moeqs
						_Qtdeqs = Iif(crMoe.Qtdeqs=0, 1, crMoe.Qtdeqs)
					Else
						m.Moedas = TotGrupo.Moeda
						_Qtdeqs = 1
					EndIf
					Moeg  = fBuscarCotacao(m.Moedas, DateTime(), ThisForm.poDataMgr) * _qtdeqs

					_vlrT = _vlrt + (TotGrupo.ValGrupo * MoeG / _Moeda)
				Else
					_vlrt = _vlrt + TotGrupo.ValGrupo
				EndIf
			EndIf
		EndScan
		If InList(ThisForm.PcEscolha,'INSERIR','ALTERAR')
			Replace Valors With _vlrt in crSigCdPro
		Endif
	Endif

	Select TotGrupo2
	Locate For Estimado = 1
	If Not Eof()
		If crSigCdPro.Moedas = ' ' And InList(ThisForm.PcEscolha,'INSERIR','ALTERAR')
			Replace Moedas with MoeCs in CrSigCdPro
		EndIf

		ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdMoe', 'crMoe', 'CMoes', crSigCdPro.Moedas)
		Go Top In crMoe
		If Not Empty(crMoe.Moeqs)
			m.Moedas = crMoe.Moeqs
			_Qtdeqs = Iif(crMoe.Qtdeqs=0, 1, crMoe.Qtdeqs)
		Else
			m.Moedas = crSigCdPro.Moedas
			_Qtdeqs = 1
		EndIf
		Moedac  = fBuscarCotacao(m.Moedas, DateTime(), ThisForm.poDataMgr) * _qtdeqs

		_VlrT = 0
		Scan
			If Estimado = 1
				If TotGrupo2.Moeda <> crSigCdPro.Moedas
					ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdMoe', 'crMoe', 'CMoes', TotGrupo2.Moeda)
					Go Top In crMoe
					If Not Empty(crMoe.Moeqs)
						m.Moedas = crMoe.Moeqs
						_Qtdeqs = Iif(crMoe.Qtdeqs=0, 1, crMoe.Qtdeqs)
					Else
						m.Moedas = TotGrupo2.Moeda
						_Qtdeqs = 1
					EndIf
					Moeg  = fBuscarCotacao(m.Moedas, DateTime(), ThisForm.poDataMgr) * _qtdeqs

					_vlrT = _vlrt + (TotGrupo2.ValGrupo * MoeG / Moedac)
				Else
					_vlrt = _vlrt + TotGrupo2.ValGrupo
				EndIf
			EndIf
		EndScan
		If InList(ThisForm.PcEscolha,'INSERIR','ALTERAR')
			Replace Valors With _vlrt in crSigCdPro
		Endif
	EndIf
EndIf
SELECT CrSigPrCpo
ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgComposicao.GradeGrupo.Refresh
ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgCusto.gradeGRUPO2.Refresh
* Fim *********************************************************************************
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE impetiqueta
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE impetiqueta
ThisForm.Tipo 	    = 'CADASTRO'
ThisForm.Produto    = crSigCdPro.CPros
ThisForm.Op_Escolha = ThisForm.pcEscolha

lcQuery = [Select * ] + ;
		    [From SigOpEtq ] + ;
		   [Where Cpros = '] + Padr(ThisForm.Produto, 14) + [' And ] + ;
		    	 [Not Grupos = '] + Space(10) + [' And ] + ;
		    	 [Not Contas = '] + Space(10) + [']

If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'TmpEti') < 1)
	=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (ImpEtiqueta - 1)')
	Return 0
EndIf

If (RecCount('TmpEti') > 0)
	Do Form SigOpIpE With ThisForm, ThisForm.AlterouoProduto

	ThisForm.poDatamgr.CursorQuery('SigCdPro', 'crTmp', 'CPros', ThisForm.Produto)
	Go Top In crTmp
	Update crSigCdPro Set ImpEtiqs = crTmp.ImpEtiqs Where CPros = ThisForm.Produto
	Use In crTmp
Else
	=MessageBox('Este Produto Năo Possui Etiquetas Ativas!!!', 48, '')
EndIf
* Fim *********************************************************************************
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE auxmontadescs
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE auxmontadescs
Private pGru, pSGr

Select crSigCdPro
pGru = crSigCdPro.CGrus
pSGr = crSigCdPro.SGrus

Select crSigCdPrd
Go Top In crSigCdPrd
Locate For CGrus = pGru
If Not Eof([crSigCdPrd])
	ThisForm.MontaDescrs
	
	Return .t.
EndIf

Go Top In crSigCdPam
lnGrD = 0

If Not Empty(pGru)
	ThisForm.poDataMgr.Requery('crSigCdGrp')
	ThisForm.poDataMgr.Requery('crSigCdPsg')
	ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdCli', 'crSigCdCli', 'IClis', crSigCdPro.IFors, 'Rclis', 'Rclis')
	ThisForm.OrdGrade = Int(Val(Substr(crSigCdGrp.CfgGerGprs, 6, 1)))

	Go Top In crSigCdGrp
	Go Top In crSigCdPsg
	
	lnGrD = Nvl(crSigCdGrp.MontaGrDs,0)
EndIf

lcDescr = []

If Not InList(lnGrD, 0, 5)
	* 1 - Composiçăo
	* 2 - Grupo + Composiçăo
	* 3 - SubGrupo + Composiçăo
	* 4 - Grupo + SubGrupo + Composiçăo
	* 5 - Manual
	* 6 - Grupo + Fornecedor (4 Dig.) + Ref.Forneedor
	* 7 - Grupo + Cor + Composiçăo
	* 8 - Grupo + Pedras + Ouro
	* 9 - Grupo + Pedras
	*11 - Grupo + SubGrupo + Classificaçăo
	Do Case
		Case (lnGrD = 1) && Composiçăo
			pGru = ''

		Case (lnGrD = 2) && Grupo + Composiçăo
			pGru = Alltrim(Iif(Eof('crSigCdGrp'), '', crSigCdGrp.DGrus))

		Case (lnGrD = 3) && SubGrupo + Composiçăo
			pGru = Alltrim(Iif(Not Eof('crSigCdPsg'), crSigCdPsg.Descricaos, Iif(Eof('crSigCdGrp'), '', crSigCdGrp.DGrus)))
			
		Case (lnGrD = 4) && Grupo + SubGrupo + Composiçăo
			pGru = Alltrim(Iif(Eof('crSigCdGrp'), '', Alltrim(crSigCdGrp.DGrus)) + ' ' + Iif(Eof('crSigCdPsg'), '', Alltrim(crSigCdPsg.Descricaos)))

		Case (lnGrD = 6) && Grupo + Fornecedor (4 digitos) + Referencia Fornecedor
			pGru = Alltrim(Iif(Eof('crSigCdGrp'), '', Alltrim(crSigCdGrp.DGrus)) + ' ' +;
					Iif(Eof('crSigCdCli'), '', Alltrim(Left(Alltrim(crSigCdCli.Rclis), 4))) + ' ' +;
					Alltrim(crSigCdPro.reffs))

		Case (lnGrD = 7) && Grupo + Cor + Composiçăo
			lcQuery = [Select Descs ] + ;
					    [From SigCdCor ] + ;
					   [Where Cods = '] + crSigCdPro.CodCors + [']

			If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, [LocalCor]) < 1)
				=MessageBox([Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!], 16, [Falha na Conexăo (LocalCor)])
				Return 0
			EndIf
			Go Top In LocalCor
			pGru = Alltrim(Iif(Eof('crSigCdGrp'), '', Alltrim(crSigCdGrp.DGrus)) + ' ' + Iif(Eof('LocalCor'), '', Alltrim(LocalCor.Descs)))

		Case (lnGrD = 11)
			Select * ;
			  From crSigCdCls ;
			 Where CGrus In (crSigCdPro.CGrus, Space(3)) ;
			 Order By Cods ;
			  Into Cursor LocalClas ReadWrite
			Select LocalClas
			Index On Cods Tag Cods	  

			Select LocalClas
			Go Top In LocalClas
			Locate For Cods = Padr(crSigCdPro.cClass, 3)
		
			lcfina = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.getCodFinP.Value
			pGru = Alltrim(Iif(Eof('crSigCdGrp'), '', Alltrim(crSigCdGrp.DGrus)) + ' ' + Iif(Eof('crSigCdPsg'), '', Alltrim(crSigCdPsg.Descricaos)) + ;
				' ' + Iif(Eof('LocalClas'), '', Alltrim(LocalClas.Descs)) + ' ' + Alltrim(lcfina))
				
	EndCase

	If Not Inlist(lnGrD, 8, 9) && Grupo + Pedras + Ouro / Grupo + Pedras
		lcDescr = fGerarDescrs(pGru, crSigCdPro.CPros, 3, ThisForm.poDataMgr, .f., .t.)
	EndIf
	
	If (lcDescr = Chr(254))
		Return .f.
	EndIf

	If Empty(lcDescr)
		lcDescr = [PRODUTO SEM COMPOSIÇĂO]
	EndIf
	
	If InList(lnGrD, 8, 9) && Grupo + Pedras + Ouro / Grupo + Pedras
		Replace DPros      With lcDescr, ;
				ObsCompras With lcDescr In crSigCdPro
		
		Replace DPro3s With lcDescr In crSigCdPro
	Else
		Replace DPros   With Subs(lcDescr, 01, 40) In crSigCdPro

		Replace DPro3s With Subs(lcDescr, 41, Len(Alltrim(lcDescr)) - 40) In crSigCdPro
	EndIf
EndIf

If Inlist(lnGrD, 8, 9) && Grupo + Pedras + Ouro / Grupo + Pedras
	Replace ObsCompras With lcDescr In crSigCdPro
EndIf

If InList(crSigCdGrp.DscCompras, 2, 3) && 0/1-Nenhum; 2-Portuguęs; 3-Inglęs
	lcDgs = Alltrim(Iif(IsEmpty(crSigCdPro.DescFis), Iif(IsEmpty(crSigCdPro.DPro3s), crSigCdPro.DPros, crSigCdPro.DPro3s), crSigCdPro.DescFis))

	If (crSigCdGrp.DscCompras = 3) And Not Empty(lcDgs) && Descriçăo Em Inglęs
		Select crSigCdDic
		Scan
			If Not Empty(lcDgs)
				lcDgs = Strtran(lcDgs, Alltrim(crSigCdDic.Expressao), Alltrim(crSigCdDic.Traducao))
			EndIf
		EndScan
	EndIf

	Replace DscCompras With lcDgs In crSigCdPro
EndIf

Return .t.
* Fim *********************************************************************************
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE mostracompos
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE mostracompos
LParameters pGru

* Checando Se o Grupo é o Grupo De Matéria Prima, Para Exibir ou Ocultar os
* Campos de Composiçăo Relativos a Matéria Prima (por Richard - 17/05/2002)

With ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgComposicao.cntMtPrima
	.getCompos.Enabled 	   = .f.
	.lblDigiMaxs.Visible   = .f.
	.getDigiMaxs.Visible   = .f.
	.lblOrdCompos.Visible  = .f.
	.getOrdCompos.Visible  = .f.
	.lblMontaDescs.Visible = .f.
	.cmbMontaDescs.Visible = .f.
	.lblCasas.Visible 	   = .f.
	.getCasas.Visible 	   = .f.

	ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdGrp', 'crTmp', 'CGrus', pGru)
	Go Top In crTmp
	
	If Not Empty(pGru) And Not Eof('crTmp') And InList(crTmp.MtPrimas, 1, 2)
		.getCompos.Enabled 	   = .t.
		.lblDigiMaxs.Visible   = .t.
		.getDigiMaxs.Visible   = .t.
		.getDigiMaxs.Enabled   = .t.
		.lblOrdCompos.Visible  = .t.
		.getOrdCompos.Visible  = .t.
		.getOrdCompos.Enabled  = .t.
		.lblMontaDescs.Visible = .t.
		.cmbMontaDescs.Visible = .t.
		.cmbMontaDescs.Enabled = .t.
		.lblCasas.Visible  	   = .t.
		.getCasas.Visible      = .t.
		.getCasas.Enabled      = .t.

		.getCompos.Value	 = Iif(Empty(crSigCdPro.Compos),     crTmp.Compos, 	 crSigCdPro.Compos)
		.cmbMontaDescs.Value = Iif(Empty(crSigCdPro.MontaDescs), crTmp.MontaDescs, crSigCdPro.MontaDescs)
		.getDigiMaxs.Value 	 = Iif(Empty(crSigCdPro.DigiMaxs),   crTmp.DigiMaxs,   crSigCdPro.DigiMaxs)
		.getOrdCompos.Value  = Iif(Empty(crSigCdPro.OrdCompos),  crTmp.OrdCompos,  crSigCdPro.OrdCompos)
		.getCasas.Value 	 = Iif(Empty(crSigCdPro.Casas), 	   crTmp.Casas, 	 crSigCdPro.Casas)

		.getCompos.Enabled 	   = Iif(.getCompos.Enabled, 	 Empty(crTmp.Compos), 	  .getCompos.Enabled)
		.cmbMontaDescs.Enabled = Iif(.cmbMontaDescs.Enabled, Empty(crTmp.MontaDescs), .cmbMontaDescs.Enabled)
		.getDigiMaxs.Enabled   = Iif(.getDigiMaxs.Enabled,   Empty(crTmp.DigiMaxs),   .getDigiMaxs.Enabled)
		.getOrdCompos.Enabled  = Iif(.getOrdCompos.Enabled,  Empty(crTmp.OrdCompos),  .getOrdCompos.Enabled)
		.getCasas.Enabled	   = Iif(.getCasas.Enabled, 	 Empty(crTmp.Casas), 	  .getCasas.Enabled)
	EndIf 
	Use In crTmp
EndWith
* Fim *********************************************************************************
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE totalgrupocv
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE totalgrupocv
Private pPro, pDat, pHor

Zap In TotGruCv

pPro = Iif(Empty(crSigPrCpo.CPros), Replicate(Chr(254), 14), crSigPrCpo.CPros)

If ThisForm.Tipo2
	pDat = Iif(Empty(crSigPrCpo.DataAlts), fDtoSQL({}), crSigPrCpo.DataAlts)
	pHor = crSigPrCpo.HoraAlts

	Select Cgrus, Moeds, VlrCvs, QtdCvs From crSigPrCp2 Into cursor CrTmp

	Select crTmp
	Scan
		Select TotGrucv
		Set Order To GruMoe
		Seek crTmp.Cgrus + crTmp.Moeds
		If Eof()
			Valgr = (crTmp.VlrCvs * crTmp.Qtdcvs)
			Insert Into TotGrucv (Grupo, ValGrupo, Moeda) Values (crTmp.Cgrus, Valgr, crTmp.Moeds)
		Else
			Replace ValGrupo With ValGrupo + (crTmp.VlrCvs * crTmp.QtdCvs) IN totgrucv
		EndIf
	EndScan
Else
	Select Cgrus, Moeds, VlrCvs, QtdCvs, pCompos, Iif(chkInstalas=2, Pesos, Qtds) as Qtds ;
	  From crSigPrCpo Where TpCalcCus = 1 Into cursor crtmp

	Select crTmp
	Scan
		Select TotGrucv
		Set Order To GruMoe
		Seek crTmp.CGrus + crTmp.Moeds
		If Eof()
			Valgr = (crTmp.VlrCvs * crTmp.QtdCvs)
			Insert Into TotGrucv (Grupo, ValGrupo, Moeda) Values (crTmp.Cgrus, Valgr, crTmp.Moeds)
		Else
			Replace ValGrupo With ValGrupo + (crTmp.VlrCvs * crTmp.QtdCvs) IN totgrucv
		EndIf
	EndScan
EndIf
SELECT CrSigPrCpo

ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgCusto.gradeGRUPO2.Refresh 
* Fim *********************************************************************************
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE sqldados
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE sqldados
Private pPro, pGru, pSgr, pDtI, pDtF, pDtA, pHrA, pUsA, pStI, pStF

pGru = Padr(ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntFiltros.getCgru.Value, 3)
pDtI = fDtoSQL(ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntFiltros.getDtIni.Value)
pDtF = fDtoSQL(ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntFiltros.getDtFim.Value, '23:59:59')
pStI = Iif(ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntFiltros.optFilSituas.Value = 3, 2, 1)
pStF = Iif(ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntFiltros.optFilSituas.Value = 2, 1, 2)

Do Case
	Case Empty(pGru)
		ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntMensagem.Top = ThisForm.TopMensa
		=MessageBox('Selecione Um Grupo de Produto Válido!!!', 0+48, 'Atençăo!!!')
		ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntFiltros.getCgru.SetFocus
		Return 0

	Case Empty(ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntFiltros.getDtIni.Value)
		ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntMensagem.Top = ThisForm.TopMensa
		=MessageBox('Selecione Uma Data Inicial Válida!!!', 0+48, 'Atençăo!!!')
		ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntFiltros.getDtIni.SetFocus
		Return 0

	Case Empty(ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntFiltros.getDtFim.Value)
		ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntMensagem.Top = ThisForm.TopMensa
		=MessageBox('Selecione Uma Data Final Válida!!!', 0+48, 'Atençăo!!!')
		ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntFiltros.getDtFim.SetFocus
		Return 0

	Case (ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntFiltros.getDtIni.Value > ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntFiltros.getDtFim.Value)
		ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntMensagem.Top = ThisForm.TopMensa
		=MessageBox('Selecione Uma Data Inicial Menor ou Igual a Final!!!', 0+48, 'Atençăo!!!')
		ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntFiltros.getDtIni.SetFocus
		Return 0
EndCase

ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.Grade.RecordSource = ''
ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.cntQtMin.grdQtMin.RecordSource = ''
ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgComposicao.grdCompo.RecordSource = ''
ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgCusto.grdCompo.RecordSource = ''
ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgComposicao.grdSubCp.RecordSource = ''
ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.PgDadosFaseP.GradFase.RecordSource = ''
ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.PgDadosFaseP.grdMatrizes.RecordSource = ''
ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.PgDadosConsP.GrdCons.RecordSource  = ''
ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.PgDadosConsP.GrDTemp.RecordSource  = ''
ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDadosFiscais.grdCmv.RecordSource = ''
ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDesigner.grdDesigner.RecordSource = ''
ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDesigner.grdArquivos.RecordSource = ''

ThisForm.poDataMgr.Requery('crListaPro')
Go Bottom In crListaPro

pPro = Iif(Empty(crListaPro.CPros), Replicate(Chr(254), 14), crListaPro.CPros)
pSgr = crListaPro.SGrus

If ThisForm.Tipo2
	pDtA = Iif(Empty(crListaPro.DataAlts), fDtoSQL({}), crListaPro.DataAlts)
	pHrA = crListaPro.HoraAlts
	pUsA = crListaPro.UsuaAlts
EndIf

With ThisForm.poDataMgr
	.Requery('crSigPrCpo')
	.Requery('crSigPrMdl')
	.Requery('crSigCdPrf')
	.Requery('crSigPrMtz')
	.Requery('crSigPrPmi')
	.Requery('crSigCdMin')
	.Requery('crSigCdGrp')
	.Requery('crSigCdPsg')
	.Requery('crSigPrCrr')
	.Requery('crSigPrTar')
	.Requery('crSigPrArq')

	If ThisForm.Tipo2
		.Requery('crSigCdPrc')
		.Requery('crSigPrCp2')
		.Requery('crSigPrMdc')
		.Requery('crSigCdPfc')
		.Requery('crSigPrMt2')
		.Requery('crSigSubC2')
		.Requery('crSigPrTa2')
		.Requery('crSigPrCa2')
	EndIf
EndWith
ThisForm.OrdGrade = Int(Val(Substr(crSigCdGrp.CfgGerGprs, 6, 1)))

Select crSigCdPrf
Index On Produtos + Str(Ordem2, 3) Tag Linhas

Select crSigPrCpo
ThisForm.LimpaFilCompo
Update crSigPrCpo Set Etiqs = [N] Where Not Etiqs = [S]
Select crSigSubCp
ThisForm.LimpaFilCompo
Update crSigSubCp Set Etiqs = [N] Where Not Etiqs = [S]

Select crSigPrCpo
Scan
	If Not ThisForm.CarregaInstal(crSigPrCpo.Mats)
		Return .f.
	EndIf
EndScan
Go Top In crSigPrCpo

ThisForm.RetiraNulls

ThisForm.MontaGrades

Zap In crProcurar

Select crListaPro
If ThisForm.Tipo2
	Index On CPros  + Dtos(DataAlts) + HoraAlts Tag CPros
	Index On DPros  + Dtos(DataAlts) + HoraAlts Tag DPros
	Index On DPro2s + Dtos(DataAlts) + HoraAlts Tag DPro2s
	Index On Dtos(DataAlts) + HoraAlts + CPros  Tag Reffs
	Index On UsuaAlts + Dtos(DataAlts) + HoraAlts + CPros Tag UsuaAlts
Else
	Index On CPros  Tag CPros
	Index On DPros  Tag DPros
	Index On DPro2s Tag DPro2s
	If CrSigCdPac.lstPrors = 2
		Index on Compos Tag Reffs
	Else
		Index On Reffs Tag Reffs
	Endif
EndIf
Index On cIdChaves Tag cIdChaves
Go Top

If Not Empty(pGru) And Not Empty(pDtI) And Not Empty(pDtF)
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.Enabled = .t.
	ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.Grade.Enabled = .t.
	ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.Grupo_op.Enabled = .t.
	ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cmdAcabado.Enabled = .t.
EndIf

ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntMensagem.Top = ThisForm.TopMensa
ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.lblProdutos.Caption = 'Produtos Selecionados : ' + Alltrim(Str(Reccount('crListaPro')))

ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.Grade.Refresh
* Fim **************************************************************************************
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE retiranulls
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE retiranulls
Select crSigPrCpo
ThisForm.LimpaFilCompo
Replace All DtMovs    With Ctod('') For IsNull(DtMovs)
Replace All DataTrans With Ctod('') For IsNull(DataTrans)

Select crSigSubCp
ThisForm.LimpaFilCompo
Replace All DtMovs    With Ctod('') For IsNull(DtMovs)
Replace All DataTrans With Ctod('') For IsNull(DataTrans)

Select crSigCdPrc
Replace All DataAlts  With Ctod('') For IsNull(DataAlts)
Replace All DtComps   With Ctod('') For IsNull(DtComps)
Replace All Datas     With Ctod('') For IsNull(Datas)
Replace All DataTrans With Ctod('') For IsNull(DataTrans)
Replace All DtFilms   With Ctod('') For IsNull(DtFilms)
Replace All DtIncs    With Ctod('') For IsNull(DtIncs)
Replace All DescFis   With '' For IsNull(DescFis)
Replace All FigJpgs   With '' For IsNull(FigJpgs)

Select crSigPrCp2
Replace All DataAlts  With Ctod('') For IsNull(DataAlts)
Replace All DataTrans With Ctod('') For IsNull(DataTrans)

Select crSigSubC2
Replace All DataAlts  With Ctod('') For IsNull(DataAlts)
Replace All DataTrans With Ctod('') For IsNull(DataTrans)

Select crSigCdPrf
Replace All FigProcs With '' For IsNull(FigProcs)
Replace All Obs      With '' For IsNull(Obs)

Select crSigCdPfc
Replace All DataAlts With Ctod('') For IsNull(DataAlts)
Replace All DtFins   With Ctod('') For IsNull(DtFins)
Replace All DtInis   With Ctod('') For IsNull(DtInis)
Replace All FigProcs With '' For IsNull(FigProcs)
Replace All Obs      With '' For IsNull(Obs)

Select crSigPrMt2
Replace All DataAlts With Ctod('') For IsNull(DataAlts)

Select crSigPrMdc
Replace All ModDtFin With Ctod('') For IsNull(ModDtFin)
Replace All ModDtIni With Ctod('') For IsNull(ModDtIni)
Replace All DataAlts With Ctod('') For IsNull(DataAlts)

Select crSigCdGrp
Replace All DataTrans With Ctod('') For IsNull(DataTrans)

Select crSigPrTam
Replace All DataAlts  With Ctod('') For IsNull(DataAlts)
Replace All DataTrans With Ctod('') For IsNull(DataTrans)

Select crSigPrTa2
Replace All DataAlts  With Ctod('') For IsNull(DataAlts)
Replace All DataTrans With Ctod('') For IsNull(DataTrans)

Select crSigPrCa2
Replace All DataAlts  With Ctod('') For IsNull(DataAlts)

Select crSigPrTar
Replace All DtFims    With Ctod('') For IsNull(DtFims)
Replace All ObsTars   With '' For IsNull(ObsTars)

Select crSigCdPro
* Fim *********************************************************************************
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE preparadados
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE preparadados
Lparameters pGpr

Private pPro

If Not InList(Lastkey(), 5, 19, 27, 15)
	If ThisForm.Parametrizado And Not Empty(pGpr)
		ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntFiltros.getCgru.Value = pGpr
		ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntFiltros.getDtIni.Value = Ctod([01/01/1900])
		ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntFiltros.getDtFim.Value = Ctod([31/12/2900])
		ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntFiltros.getCgru.Refresh
		ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntFiltros.getDtIni.Refresh
		ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntFiltros.getDtFim.Refresh
	EndIf
	
	If Empty(ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntFiltros.getCgru.Value) And Not ThisForm.Parametrizado 
		=MessageBox('Selecione Um Grupo de Produto!!!', 0+48, 'Grupo Inválido - Preparadados')
		ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntFiltros.getCgru.SetFocus
		Return 0
	EndIf

	If Empty(ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntFiltros.getDtIni.Value)
		=MessageBox('Selecione Uma Data Inicial Para o Período!!!', 0+48, 'Data Inicial Inválida')
		ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntFiltros.getDtIni.SetFocus
		Return 0
	EndIf

	If Empty(ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntFiltros.getDtFim.Value)
		=MessageBox('Selecione Uma Data Final Para o Período!!!', 0+48, 'Data Final Inválida')
		ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntFiltros.getDtFim.SetFocus
		Return 0
	EndIf
		
	ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntMensagem.Top = 180
	ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntMensagem.Draw
	ThisForm.Draw

	ThisForm.LockScreen = .t.

	ThisForm.SqlDados

	ThisForm.HabilitaControles(.t.)
	
	With ThisForm.Pagina.Lista
		Clear Resources
		.ImgFigJpg.Picture = ''
		.ImgFigJpg.Visible = .f.
	EndWith
	
	Select crSigCdGrp
	Go Top
	ThisForm.OrdGrade = Int(Val(Substr(crSigCdGrp.CfgGerGprs, 6, 1)))
	lcMercs = crSigCdGrp.Mercs
	
	ThisForm.poDatamgr.CursorQuery('SigCdGpr','crSigCdGpr','Codigos',crSigCdGrp.Mercs)
	Select crSigCdGpr
	Go Top

	Set Order To CPros In crListaPro
	With ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.Grade
		.Column1.Header1.BackColor = RGB(220,255,220)
		.Column2.Header1.BackColor = .Column4.Header1.BackColor
		.Column5.Header1.BackColor = .Column4.Header1.BackColor
		.Column6.Header1.BackColor = .Column4.Header1.BackColor
		.Column1.SetFocus
		.Refresh
	EndWith

	=fCarregaGrade(ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.Grade)

	ThisForm.LockScreen = .f.

	ThisForm.Pagina.Refresh
EndIf
* Fim *********************************************************************************
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE inserecompos
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE inserecompos
Local lcLin

lcLin = ThisFOrm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.getLin.Value

If Not Empty(lcLin) And Not ThisForm.Tipo2 And InList(ThisForm.pcEscolha, 'INSERIR', 'ALTERAR')
	Select * From crSigPrCpo Into Cursor csTemCompo
	If (Reccount('csTemCompo') < 1)
		Select CrSigPrCpo
		Zap
		ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdLni', 'LocalLinI', 'Linhas', lcLin)
		If (Reccount('LocalLinI') > 0)
			lcTip = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgCusto.cmbTipos.Value 

			Select LocalLinI
			Scan
				Scatter Memvar Memo
				m.CidChaves = fUniqueIds()
				m.Cpros     = crSigCdPro.CPros
				
				lcSql = [Select CustoFs as pCompos, MoeCusfs as Moeds From SigCdPro Where Cpros = ']+LocalLini.Mats+[']
				ThisForm.PodataMgr.SqlExecute(lcSql,'TmpProL')
				Select TmpProl
				Scatter Memvar
				Insert Into crSigPrCpo From Memvar
				Replace Tipos With lcTip, ;
						TpCalcCus With 1 In crSigPrCpo
			EndScan
			Go Top In crSigPrCpo
		EndIf
	EndIf
EndIf
* Fim **************************************************************************************
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE atuapreco
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE atuapreco
Lparameters pAltCusto

cCompo = Alias()

lcMat = &cCompo..Mats
If Not Empty(lcMat)
	If ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdPro', 'crPro', 'CPros', lcMat)
		Go Top In crPro
		ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdGrp', 'crGru', 'CGrus', crPro.CGrus)

		If CrGru.pvCompos = 2
			Replace pCompos With CrPro.Pvens,;
					Moeds   with CrPro.Moevs,;
					Dtmovs  With DateTime() ,;
					Cgrus   With CrPro.Cgrus In &cCompo.
		Else
			Replace PCompos With crPro.Custofs,;
					Moeds   With Iif(Not Empty(CrPro.MoeCusFs),crPro.MoeCusfs,Moeds),;
					Dtmovs  With DateTime() ,;
					Cgrus   With CrPro.Cgrus In &cCompo.
		Endif
		If ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdUni', 'crUni', 'CUnis', crPro.CUnis)
			Go Top In crUni
			If Not Empty(crUni.PCustVens)
				Replace QtdCvs With Round(&cCompo..Qtds * (1 + (crUni.PcustVens/100)), 3) In &cCompo.
			Else
				Replace QtdCvs With &cCompo..Qtds In &cCompo.
			EndIf 
		EndIf
		Use In crUni
		
		If ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdGrp', 'crGru', 'CGrus', crPro.CGrus) And Not pAltCusto
			Go Top In crGru
			If Not Empty(crGru.PcustVens)
				Replace VlrCvs With Round(&cCompo..PCompos * (1 + (crGru.PcustVens/100)), 3) In &cCompo.
			Else
				Replace VlrCvs With &cCompo..Pcompos In &cCompo.
			EndIf
		EndIf
		Replace VlrPvs With CrPro.Pvens in &cCompo.
		If &cCompo..Moeds <> CrPro.Moevs
			ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdMoe', 'crMoe', 'CMoes', &cCompo..Moeds)
			Go Top In crMoe
			If Not Empty(crMoe.Moeqs)
				m.Moedas = crMoe.Moeqs
				_Qtdeqs = Iif(crMoe.Qtdeqs=0, 1, crMoe.Qtdeqs)
			Else
				m.Moedas = &cCompo..Moeds
				_Qtdeqs = 1
			EndIf
			CotMcf = fBuscarCotacao(m.Moedas, DateTime(), ThisForm.poDataMgr) * _qtdeqs

			ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdMoe', 'crMoe', 'CMoes', crPro.Moevs)
			Go Top In crMoe
			If Not Empty(crMoe.Moeqs)
				m.Moedas = crMoe.Moeqs
				_Qtdeqs = Iif(crMoe.Qtdeqs=0, 1, crMoe.Qtdeqs)
			Else
				m.Moedas = CrPro.Moevs
				_Qtdeqs = 1
			EndIf
			CotMpv= fBuscarCotacao(m.Moedas,DateTime(), ThisForm.poDataMgr) * _qtdeqs

			_MarkCv = Round(Iif(&cCompo..VlrCvs = 0 , 0 , ( ( CrPro.Pvens * CotmPv / CotmCf ) / &cCompo..VlrCvs )),6)
		Else
			_MarkCv = Round(Iif(&cCompo..VlrCvs = 0, 0 , (CrPro.Pvens / &cCompo..VlrCvs)) ,6)
		EndIf
		Replace MarkCvs With _MarkCv in &cCompo.

		Use In crGru
	EndIf
	Use In crPro
EndIf

Select &cCompo.
Return .t.
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE mqtdemin
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE mqtdemin
ThisForm.poDatamgr.SqlExecute([Select EstMins From SigCdPac],'csSigCdPac')

If csSigCdPac.EstMins = 1

	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.CntQtMin.GrdQtMin.RecordSource = ''

	pPro = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.getCpro.Value
	ThisForm.poDataMgr.Requery('crSigCdMin')
	Select crSigCdMin
	Go Top In crSigCdMin

	If Eof()
		DO FORM SigCdEmn With pPro
	EndIf 
	
EndIf

USE in csSigCdPac
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE totalplan
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE totalplan
Private pPro, pDat, pHor
Local MarkCus,MarkVen,lnAltC,SGrupo

MarkCus = CrSigCdPro.Cftiocs
MarkVen = CrSigCdPro.cftios
SGrupo = []

Zap In CsGrade

* Richard em 22/02/2013 - Alterado pra seguir novo cálculo da grade, por peso ou quantidade
*Select Cgrus as Grupo, Mats as CPros, Moeds as Moeda, Val(Str((pCompos * Qtds), 12, 4)) as ValGrupo
Select Cgrus As Grupo, Mats As CPros, Moeds As Moeda, Pesos, Qtds, PCompos, 00000000.000 As ValGrupo, chkInstalas, Space(6) As sGrus ;
	From crSigPrCpo ;
	Order By 1, 2, 3 ;
	Into Cursor LocalTGrupo Readwrite

Update LocalTGrupo Set ValGrupo = Iif(chkInstalas=2, Pesos, Qtds) * PCompos

Select LocalTGrupo
Go Top
Scan
	=Thisform.poDataMgr.CursorQuery([SigCdPro],[crTmpSGr],[Cpros],LocalTGrupo.CPros,[sGrus])
	Select crTmpSGr
	If Reccount([crTmpSGr])>0
		Replace sGrus With crTmpSGr.sGrus In LocalTGrupo
	Endif
	Select LocalTGrupo
Endscan

If Not Empty(MarkCus)
	lcSql = [Select * From SigPrFti Where Cods = ']+MarkCus+[']
	Thisform.poDataMgr.Sqlexecute(lcSql,'TmpFtio')
	Select TmpFtio
	If Reccount() > 0 And TmpFtio.Acrescs = 0 And TmpFtio.Valors = 0

		Thisform.poDataMgr.CursorQuery([SigCdPro],[crTmpSGru],[Cpros],LocalTGrupo.CPros,[Sgrus])
		SGrupo = crTmpSGru.sGrus

		lcSql = [Select a.*, b.Dgrus From SigPrFto a, SigCdGrp b ] + ;
			[Where a.Cods = ']+MarkCus+[' ] + ;
			[And a.Cgrus = b.Cgrus ] + ;
			[And (a.Cgrus <> ' ' or a.SGrus <> ' ') ] + ;
			[Order by a.Cods ]
		Thisform.poDataMgr.Sqlexecute(lcSql,'TmpFtioC')

		_lnCnt = 1
		_vacm  = 0
		_vFt   = 0

		If TmpFtio.AplsCus <> 1
			Select LocalTGrupo
			Scan
				Select TmpFtioC
				*-- Rafael - Localiza o Feitio pelo SubGrupo
				Locate For CPros = LocalTGrupo.CPros
				If Not Empty(LocalTGrupo.sGrus)
					If Eof([TmpFtioC])
						Locate For sGrus = LocalTGrupo.sGrus And Empty(Cgrus)
						SGrupo = TmpFtioC.sGrus
					Endif
					If Eof([TmpFtioC])
						Locate For Cgrus = LocalTGrupo.Grupo And sGrus = LocalTGrupo.sGrus And Empty(CPros)
						SGrupo = TmpFtioC.sGrus
					Endif
					If Eof([TmpFtioC])
						Locate For Cgrus = LocalTGrupo.Grupo And CPros = LocalTGrupo.CPros And sGrus = LocalTGrupo.sGrus
						SGrupo = TmpFtioC.sGrus
					EndIf
				EndIf 
				*--
				If Eof([TmpFtioC])
					Locate For Cgrus = LocalTGrupo.Grupo And CPros = LocalTGrupo.CPros
				EndIf
				If Eof([TmpFtioC])
					Locate For Cgrus = LocalTGrupo.Grupo And Empty(CPros) And Empty(sGrus)
				Endif
				If Eof([TmpFtioC])
					Locate For Cgrus = LocalTGrupo.Grupo And Empty(CPros)
				Endif

				If Not Eof([TmpFtioC])
					_Coef = TmpFtioC.Coefs
					If Eof()
						_Coef = 1
					Endif

					Moec = 1
					Moep = 1
					If TmpFtio.Moedas <> LocalTGrupo.Moeda
						Thisform.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdMoe', 'crMoe', 'CMoes', TmpFtio.Moedas)
						Go Top In crMoe
						If Not Empty(crMoe.Moeqs)
							m.Moedas = crMoe.Moeqs
							_Qtdeqs = Iif(crMoe.Qtdeqs=0, 1, crMoe.Qtdeqs)
						Else
							m.Moedas = TmpFtio.Moedas
							_Qtdeqs = 1
						Endif
						Moec = fBuscarCotacao(m.Moedas, Datetime(), Thisform.poDataMgr) * _Qtdeqs

						Thisform.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdMoe', 'crMoe', 'CMoes', LocalTGrupo.Moeda)
						Go Top In crMoe
						If Not Empty(crMoe.Moeqs)
							m.Moedas = crMoe.Moeqs
							_Qtdeqs = Iif(crMoe.Qtdeqs=0, 1, crMoe.Qtdeqs)
						Else
							m.Moedas = LocalTGrupo.Moeda
							_Qtdeqs = 1
						Endif
						Moep  = fBuscarCotacao(m.Moedas, Datetime(), Thisform.poDataMgr) * _Qtdeqs
					Endif
					_vcoef = Round(( LocalTGrupo.ValGrupo * Moep / Moec ),3)
					_vadic = Round((( _vcoef * _Coef ) - _vcoef ),3)
					_vacm  = _vacm + _vcoef + _vadic
					_vFt   = _vFt + _vadic

					Select CsGrade
					Append Blank
					Replace Tipos    With [C],;
						Ordem    With _lnCnt,;
						CPros    With Iif(Empty(TmpFtioC.CPros), TmpFtioC.Cgrus, TmpFtioC.CPros), ;
						Dpros    With TmpFtioC.Dgrus,;
						Totas    With _vcoef,;
						Coefs    With _Coef,;
						Valos    With _vadic,;
						TotalG   With _vcoef + _vadic,;
						Acumulas With _vacm ,;
						sGrus	 With SGrupo
					_lnCnt = _lnCnt + 1
				Endif
			Endscan
		Else
			_vacm  = CrSigCdPro.PCuss
			Select CsGrade
			Append Blank
			Replace Tipos    With [C],;
				Ordem    With _lnCnt,;
				CPros    With 'Custo',;
				Dpros    With 'Custo',;
				Totas    With _vacm,;
				Coefs    With 1,;
				Valos    With 0,;
				TotalG   With 0,;
				Acumulas With _vacm

			_lnCnt = _lnCnt + 1
		Endif

		lcSql = [Select a.*, b.Dpros From SigPrFto a, SigCdPro b Where a.Cods = ']+MarkCus+[' And ]+;
			[a.Cpros = b.Cpros And a.Cgrus = Space(3) Order by a.Seqs ]
		Thisform.poDataMgr.Sqlexecute(lcSql,'TmpFtioC')

		Select TmpFtioC
		Scan
			_vcoef = ( _vacm )
			If TmpFtio.DivMults = 1
				_vadic = Round((( _vcoef * TmpFtioC.Coefs ) - _vcoef ),3)
			Else
				_vadic = Round(( ( _vcoef / ( 1-( TmpFtioC.Coefs/100 ) ) ) -_vcoef ),3)
			Endif
			_vacm  = _vacm + _vadic
			_vFt   = _vFt  + _vadic

			Select CsGrade
			Append Blank
			Replace Tipos    With [C],;
				Ordem    With _lnCnt,;
				CPros    With TmpFtioC.CPros,;
				Dpros    With TmpFtioC.Dpros,;
				Totas    With _vcoef,;
				Coefs    With TmpFtioC.Coefs,;
				Valos    With _vadic,;
				TotalG   With 0,;
				Acumulas With _vacm
			_lnCnt = _lnCnt + 1
		Endscan
		Thisform.Pagina.Dados.PgframeDados.PgComposicao.Get_pftioc.Value = _vFt
		Thisform.Pagina.Dados.PgframeDados.PgComposicao.Get_pftioc.Refresh
	Endif
EndIf

If Not Empty(MarkVen)
	lcSql = [Select * From SigPrFti Where Cods = ']+MarkVen+[']
	Thisform.poDataMgr.Sqlexecute(lcSql,'TmpFtio')
	Select TmpFtio
	If Reccount() > 0 And TmpFtio.Acrescs = 0 And TmpFtio.Valors = 0

		lcSql = [Select a.*, b.Dgrus, 0 as altcoef ] + ;
			[From SigPrFto a, SigCdGrp b ] + ;
			[Where a.Cods = ']+MarkVen+[' And ]+;
			[a.Cgrus = b.Cgrus And ] + ;
			[(a.Cgrus <> ' ' or a.SGrus <> ' ') Order by a.Cods ]
		Thisform.poDataMgr.Sqlexecute(lcSql,'TmpFtioC')

		_lnCnt = 1
		_vacm  = 0
		_vFt   = 0

		**** Substitui linha de feitio por coeficiente alterado ****
		Select crPrFtp
		Go Top
		If Not Eof()
			Scan
				Select TmpFtioC
				Locate For Cgrus+cods=crPrFtp.Cgrus+crPrFtp.cods
				If Not Eof()
					If Coefs <> crPrFtp.Coefs	&& se coeficiente năo mudou, continua pegando da tabela
						Replace Coefs With crPrFtp.Coefs
						Replace cidchaves With crPrFtp.cidchaves
						Replace altcoef With 1
					Endif
				Endif
			Endscan
		EndIf

		If TmpFtio.AplsCus <> 1
			Select LocalTGrupo
			Scan
				SGrupo = []
				
				Select TmpFtioC
				*-- Rafael - Localiza o Feitio pelo SubGrupo
				Locate For CPros = LocalTGrupo.CPros
				If Not Empty(LocalTGrupo.sGrus)
					If Eof([TmpFtioC])
						Locate For sGrus = LocalTGrupo.sGrus And Empty(Cgrus)
						SGrupo = TmpFtioC.sGrus
					Endif
					If Eof([TmpFtioC])
						Locate For Cgrus = LocalTGrupo.Grupo And sGrus = LocalTGrupo.sGrus And Empty(CPros)
						SGrupo = TmpFtioC.sGrus
					Endif
					If Eof([TmpFtioC])
						Locate For Cgrus = LocalTGrupo.Grupo And CPros = LocalTGrupo.CPros And sGrus = LocalTGrupo.sGrus
						SGrupo = TmpFtioC.sGrus
					EndIf
				EndIf
				*--
				If Eof([TmpFtioC])
					Locate For Cgrus = LocalTGrupo.Grupo And CPros = LocalTGrupo.CPros
				EndIf
				If Eof([TmpFtioC])
					Locate For Cgrus = LocalTGrupo.Grupo And Empty(CPros) And Empty(sGrus)
				Endif
				If Eof([TmpFtioC])
					Locate For Cgrus = LocalTGrupo.Grupo And Empty(CPros)
				Endif
				
*!*					Locate For Cgrus = LocalTGrupo.Grupo And CPros = LocalTGrupo.CPros
*!*					If Eof([TmpFtioC])
*!*						Locate For Cgrus = LocalTGrupo.Grupo And Empty(CPros)
*!*					Endif
				If Not Eof([TmpFtioC])
					_Coef = TmpFtioC.Coefs
					If Eof()
						_Coef = 1
					Endif
				
					Moec = 1
					Moep = 1
					If TmpFtio.Moedas <> LocalTGrupo.Moeda
						Thisform.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdMoe', 'crMoe', 'CMoes', TmpFtio.Moedas)
						Go Top In crMoe
						If Not Empty(crMoe.Moeqs)
							m.Moedas = crMoe.Moeqs
							_Qtdeqs = Iif(crMoe.Qtdeqs=0, 1, crMoe.Qtdeqs)
						Else
							m.Moedas = TmpFtio.Moedas
							_Qtdeqs = 1
						Endif
						Moec = fBuscarCotacao(m.Moedas, Datetime(), Thisform.poDataMgr) * _Qtdeqs

						Thisform.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdMoe', 'crMoe', 'CMoes', LocalTGrupo.Moeda)
						Go Top In crMoe
						If Not Empty(crMoe.Moeqs)
							m.Moedas = crMoe.Moeqs
							_Qtdeqs = Iif(crMoe.Qtdeqs=0, 1, crMoe.Qtdeqs)
						Else
							m.Moedas = LocalTGrupo.Moeda
							_Qtdeqs = 1
						Endif
						Moep  = fBuscarCotacao(m.Moedas, Datetime(), Thisform.poDataMgr) * _Qtdeqs
					Endif
					_vcoef = Round(( LocalTGrupo.ValGrupo * Moep / Moec ),3)
					_vadic = Round((( _vcoef * _Coef ) - _vcoef ),3)
					_vacm  = _vacm + _vcoef + _vadic
					_vFt   = _vFt + _vadic

					Select CsGrade
					Append Blank
					Replace Tipos With [V],;
						Ordem     With _lnCnt,;
						CPros     With Iif(Empty(TmpFtioC.CPros), TmpFtioC.Cgrus, TmpFtioC.CPros),;
						Dpros     With TmpFtioC.Dgrus,;
						Totas     With _vcoef,;
						Coefs     With _Coef,;
						Valos     With _vadic,;
						TotalG    With _vcoef + _vadic,;
						Acumulas  With _vacm, ;
						Cgrus     With TmpFtioC.Cgrus,;
						cods      With TmpFtioC.cods,;
						cidchaves With TmpFtioC.cidchaves,;
						altcoef   With TmpFtioC.altcoef ,;
						sGrus	  With SGrupo
						
					_lnCnt = _lnCnt + 1
				Endif

			Endscan
		Else
			_vacm  = CrSigCdPro.PCuss
			_vacm  = CrSigCdPro.PCuss
			Select CsGrade
			Append Blank
			Replace Tipos    With [V],;
				Ordem     With _lnCnt,;
				CPros     With 'Custo',;
				Dpros     With 'Custo',;
				Totas     With _vacm,;
				Coefs     With 1,;
				Valos     With 0,;
				TotalG    With 0,;
				Acumulas  With _vacm,;
				Cgrus     With TmpFtioC.Cgrus,;
				cods      With TmpFtioC.cods,;
				cidchaves With TmpFtioC.cidchaves,;
				altcoef   With TmpFtioC.altcoef
			_lnCnt = _lnCnt + 1
		Endif
		lcSql = [Select a.*, b.Dpros From SigPrFto a, SigCdPro b Where a.Cods = ']+MarkVen+[' And ]+;
			[a.Cpros = b.Cpros And a.CGrus = Space(3) Order by a.Seqs ]
		Thisform.poDataMgr.Sqlexecute(lcSql,'TmpFtioC')

		Select TmpFtioC
		Scan
			_vcoef = ( _vacm )
			If TmpFtio.DivMults = 1
				_vadic = Round((( _vcoef * TmpFtioC.Coefs ) - _vcoef ),3)
			Else
				_vadic = Round(( ( _vcoef / ( 1-( TmpFtioC.Coefs/100 ) ) ) -_vcoef ),3)
			Endif
			_vacm  = _vacm + _vadic
			_vFt   = _vFt + _vadic

			Select CsGrade
			Append Blank
			Replace Tipos    With [V],;
				Ordem    With _lnCnt,;
				CPros    With TmpFtioC.CPros,;
				Dpros    With TmpFtioC.Dpros,;
				Totas    With _vcoef,;
				Coefs    With TmpFtioC.Coefs,;
				Valos    With _vadic,;
				TotalG   With 0,;
				Acumulas With _vacm
			_lnCnt = _lnCnt + 1
		Endscan
		** Verifica se adicional teve alteracao no coeficiente para setar vermelho
		Select CsGrade
		lnAltC = 0
		Sum altcoef To lnAltC For altcoef = 1
		Thisform.Pagina.Dados.PgframeDados.PgComposicao.Get_pftio.ForeColor=Iif(lnAltC > 0, Rgb(255,0,0), Rgb(0,0,0))

		Thisform.Pagina.Dados.PgframeDados.PgComposicao.Get_pftio.Value = _vFt
		Thisform.Pagina.Dados.PgframeDados.PgComposicao.Get_pftio.Refresh
	Endif
Endif

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE inativar
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE inativar
If (ThisForm.Situas <> crSigCdPro.Situas) And (crSigCdPro.Situas = 2)
	lcQuery = [Select Top 1 CPros, Datars ] + ;
				[From SigMvHst ] + ;
			   [Where CPros = '] + crSigCdPro.CPros + [' And ] + ;
					 [Opers = 'E' ] + ;
			   [Order By Datars]

	If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'LocalHis') < 1)
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (LocalHis)')
		Return .f.
	EndIf
	Go Top In LocalHis
	If Not Eof([LocalHis]) And Not IsEmpty(LocalHis.Datars)
		ldDtI = Ttod(LocalHis.Datars)
		ldDtH = Ttod(Datetime())
		Replace DiasInas With (ldDtH - ldDtI) + 1 In crSigCdPro
	EndIf
EndIf
* Fim *********************************************************************************
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE retcodpro
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE retcodpro
Lparameters pRet

Select crSigPrCpo
ThisForm.LimpaFilCompo()

Select Mats, ObsCompos ;
  From crSigPrCpo ;
 Where Qtds > 0 And ;
       TpCalcCus = 1 ;
 Order By Mats ;
  Into Cursor crMontaCPros

Dimension laCompos(Max(Reccount([crMontaCPros]), 1),2)

If (Reccount([crMontaCPros]) < 1)
	laCompos(1,1) = []
	laCompos(1,2) = []
EndIf

Select crMontaCPros
Scan
	laCompos(Recno([crMontaCPros]),1) = crMontaCPros.Mats
	laCompos(Recno([crMontaCPros]),2) = crMontaCPros.ObsCompos 
EndScan

lcPro = fGerarCodPro(crSigCdPro.CGrus, crSigCdPro.SGrus, crSigCdPro.Reffs, crSigCdPro.CodFinP, crSigCdPro.CodCors, ;
					 crSigCdPro.ObsEtqs, @laCompos, ThisForm.poDataMgr, pRet, crSigCdPro.Conjunts, crSigCdPro.Colecoes, crSigCdPro.Linhas, crSigCdPro.CodTams)

If Empty(lcPro)
	Return []
EndIf

Return lcPro
* Fim **************************************************************************************
ENDPROC

PROCEDURE acertacpros
Lparameters pPro

Replace CPros With pPro In crSigCdPro

Select CrSigPrCpo
ThisForm.LimpaFilCompo
Update crSigPrCpo Set CPros = pPro
Update crSigSubCp Set CPros = pPro
Update crSigPrMdl Set CPros = pPro
Update crSigCdPrc Set CPros = pPro
Update crSigPrCp2 Set CPros = pPro
Update crSigSubC2 Set CPros = pPro
Update crSigPrMdc Set CPros = pPro
Update crSigPrPmi Set CPros = pPro
Update crSigCdMin Set CPros = pPro
Update crSigPrCrr Set CPros = pPro
Update crSigCdPft Set CPros = pPro, ProCarTits = Cpros + CCars + CTits
Update crSigCdPrf Set Produtos = pPro
Update crSigPrMtz Set CPros = pPro
Update crSigCdPfc Set Produtos = pPro
Update crSigPrMt2 Set CPros = pPro
Update crSigPrTam Set CPros = pPro
Update crSigPrCar Set CPros = pPro
Update crSigPrTa2 Set CPros = pPro
Update crSigPrCa2 Set CPros = pPro
Update crListaPro Set CPros = pPro &&& Tiago - 17/07/2013 - Inclui para atualizar o cursor principal pois quando copiava um produto estava gravado o produto copiado com o código do original
Update crSigPrTar Set CPros = pPro
Update crSigPrArq Set CPros = pPro
* Fim **************************************************************************************
ENDPROC

Scan
	Scatter Memvar Memo
	m.TpCalcCus = 1 && Tiago - Vianna - 29/11/2011 - Opçăo de copiar um produto que tenha código automático IDENTIFICADOR + CODIFICAÇĂO năo funciona se esse campos se = 1

	=MessageBox([Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!], 16, [Falha na Conexăo (CopiarProFt)])
	ThisForm.mAtivaPagina1

lcQuery = [Select * From SigPrCar Where CPros = '] + lcPro + [']
If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, [CopiarProCar]) < 1)
	=MessageBox([Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!], 16, [Falha na Conexăo (CopiarProCar)])
	ThisForm.mAtivaPagina1
	Return .f.
EndIf
Zap In crSigPrCar

	Scatter Memvar Memo
	Insert Into crSigPrCar From Memvar

	ThisForm.AcertaCPros(lcPro)

   Set DtMovs = DateTime(), ;
	   cIdChaves = fUniqueIds()

   Set FigProcs  = Iif(IsEmpty(FigProcs), Null, FigProcs), ;
   	   Obs       = Iif(IsEmpty(Obs),      Null, Obs), ;
   	   cIdChaves = fUniqueIds()

   Set cIdChaves = fUniqueIds()

   Set cIdChaves = fUniqueIds(), ;
   	   ProCarTits= Cpros + CCars + CTits

   Set cIdChaves = fUniqueIds(), ;
       DtMovs = DateTime()

Update crSigPrCar ;
   Set pkChaves = fUniqueIds()

Update crSigPrTar ;
   Set pkChaves = fUniqueIds()

   Set pkChaves = fUniqueIds()

		Datas     With DateTime(), ;
		DtIncs    With DateTime(), ;
		Flagctabs With .t., ;
		Transps   With .f., ;
		CProEqs   With [], ;
		UltComps  With Null, ;
		UsuIncs   With Usuar, ;
		vUltComps With 0 In crSigCdPro

ThisForm.LockScreen = .f.
ThisForm.Copiando = .f.

*** Tiago - 17/07/2013 - Comentei pois já chama esse método no botăo salvar
*!*	ThisForm.mAtivaPagina1
* Fim *********************************************************************************
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE filtrarcompo
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE filtrarcompo
Lparameters pPgn

cCompo = Alias()

If Upper(Alltrim(cCompo)) <> 'CRSIGPRCPO' or Upper(Alltrim(cCompo)) <> 'CRSIGSUBCP'
	Return .T.
EndIf 

If ThisForm.TemTipos And ThisForm.TempTipos
	Select &cCompo.
	ThisForm.LimpaFilCompo
	If (pPgn > 0)
		Select &cCompo.
		Scan
			Select crSigCdCom
			Go Top In crSigCdCom
			Locate For CGrus = &cCompo..CGrus And Custos = pPgn
			Replace TpCalcCus With Iif(Eof([crSigCdCom]), 0, 1) In &cCompo.
		EndScan
		If (pPgn = 1)
			Set Filter To (TpCalcCus = 1) Or Empty(Mats) In &cCompo.
		Else
			Select &cCompo.
			Scan
				If Empty(&cCompo..Tipos)
					Select crSigCdCom
					Go Top In crSigCdCom
					Locate For CGrus = &cCompo..CGrus And Custos = pPgn And Tipos = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgCusto.cmbTipos.Value
					If Not Eof([crSigCdCom])
						Replace Tipos With crSigCdCom.Tipos In &cCompo.
					EndIf
				EndIf
			EndScan
			Set Filter To ((TpCalcCus = 1) And Tipos = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgCusto.cmbTipos.Value) Or Empty(Mats) In &cCompo.
		EndIf
	EndIf
	Go Top In &cCompo.
	If Not Empty(ThisForm.Composiciona)
		Scan While Mats <> ThisForm.Composiciona
		EndScan
	Else
		Go Bottom In &cCompo.
	EndIf
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgComposicao.grdCompo.Refresh 
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgCusto.grdCompo.Refresh 
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgComposicao.get_Desc.Refresh 
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgCusto.get_Desc.Refresh
	
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgComposicao.grdSubCp.Refresh 
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgComposicao.get_Desccp.Refresh 

	ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery([SigCdGrp], [LocalGru], [CGrus], &cCompo..CGrus, [DGrus])
	If Not Used([LocalGru])
		=MessageBox([Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!], 16, [Falha na Conexăo (grdCompo - CursorQuery - LocalGru)])
		Return 0
	EndIf
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgCusto.getDGruCompos.Value = LocalGru.DGrus
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgCusto.getDGruCompos.Refresh
EndIf
* Fim *********************************************************************************
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE limpafilcompo
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE limpafilcompo
cCompo = Alias()

If Upper(Alltrim(cCompo)) <> 'CRSIGPRCPO' or Upper(Alltrim(cCompo)) <> 'CRSIGSUBCP'
	Return .T.
EndIf 

Select &cCompo.
lcRec = &cCompo..Mats
Set Filter To 
Go Top In &cCompo.
Locate For Mats = lcRec
* Fim **************************************************************************************
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE calcfornec
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE calcfornec
Lparameters pMat

Local lnVal, lcMoe

cCompo = Alias()

lnVal = &cCompo..PCompos
lcMoe = &cCompo..Moeds


Replace Bloqueio With 0 In &cCompo.

lcQuery = [Select * ] + ;
		    [From SigPrFnc ] + ;
		   [Where CPros = '] + pMat + ['] +;
		   [ AND IFors = ']+crSigCdPro.IFors+[']+;
		   [ And Reffs = ']+crSigCdPro.Reffs+[']+;
		   [ And Colecoes = ']+crSigCdPro.Colecoes+[']

If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, [LocalFPro]) < 1)
	=MessageBox([Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!], 16, [Falha na Conexăo (LocalFPro)])
	Return .f.
EndIf

IF RECCOUNT('LocalFPro') > 1
	xBrow = CreateObject('fwBuscaSel', 'LocalFPro', '', '', 'Cadastro de Fornecedores')
	xBrow.AddColuna('CPROS', '', 'Material', .t.)
	xBrow.AddColuna('pvens', '999,999.99', 'Valor',    .t.)
	xBrow.AddColuna('moevs', '', 'Moeda', .t.)
	xBrow.Show
	If (Lastkey() <> 27)
		lnVal = LocalFPro.PVens
		lcMoe = LocalFPro.Moevs
		Replace Bloqueio With 1 In &cCompo.
	ENDIF
ELSE
	Do Case
		Case Not Empty(crSigCdPro.IFors) And Not Empty(crSigCdPro.Reffs) And Not Empty(crSigCdPro.Colecoes)
			Select LocalFPro
			Go Top In LocalFPro
			Locate For IFors = crSigCdPro.IFors And Reffs = crSigCdPro.Reffs And Colecoes = crSigCdPro.Colecoes
			If Not Eof([LocalFPro])
				lnVal = LocalFPro.PVens
				lcMoe = LocalFPro.Moevs
				Replace Bloqueio With 1 In &cCompo.
			EndIf
	
		Case Not Empty(crSigCdPro.IFors) And Not Empty(crSigCdPro.Reffs)
			Select LocalFPro
			Go Top In LocalFPro
			Locate For IFors = crSigCdPro.IFors And Reffs = crSigCdPro.Reffs
			If Not Eof([LocalFPro])
				lnVal = LocalFPro.PVens
				lcMoe = LocalFPro.Moevs
				Replace Bloqueio With 1 In &cCompo.
			EndIf

		Case Not Empty(crSigCdPro.IFors) And Not Empty(crSigCdPro.Colecoes)
			Select LocalFPro
			Go Top In LocalFPro
			Locate For IFors = crSigCdPro.IFors And Colecoes = crSigCdPro.Colecoes
			If Not Eof([LocalFPro])
				lnVal = LocalFPro.PVens
				lcMoe = LocalFPro.Moevs
				Replace Bloqueio With 1 In &cCompo.
			EndIf

		Case Not Empty(crSigCdPro.IFors)
			Select LocalFPro
			Go Top In LocalFPro
			Locate For IFors = crSigCdPro.IFors And Empty(Colecoes)
			If Not Eof([LocalFPro])
				lnVal = LocalFPro.PVens
				lcMoe = LocalFPro.Moevs
				Replace Bloqueio With 1 In &cCompo.
			EndIf
	EndCase
ENDIF


Replace PCompos With lnVal, ;
		Moeds 	With lcMoe In &cCompo.
* Fim **************************************************************************************
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE setadadosjoalheria
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE setadadosjoalheria
Local lnReg, lcArea, lcQuery, lnPesoPdrs, lnPesoBris, cCodGarras, lcFiltro, lnPesoMetal

lcArea = Alias()
lnReg = Recno('crSigPrCpo')
lnPesoPdrs = 0
lnPesoBris = 0
lnPesoMetal = 0
cCodGarras = ''

Select crSigPrCpo
lcFiltro = Set('FILTER')

Set Filter To In crSigPrCpo
Go Top in crSigPrCpo
Scan
	ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdGrp','crGru','cGrus',crSigPrCpo.cGrus,'nTipoJoals,cUniPs')
	ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdPro','crItem','cPros',crSigPrCpo.Mats,'Varias')
	If not Used([crGru]) or not Used([crItem])		
		Loop
	Endif
	If( crItem.Varias == 1 )
		lnPesoMetal = lnPesoMetal + (crSigPrCpo.Qtds+crSigPrCpo.Pesos)
	EndIf
	
	* Alterado em 14/06/2013 Por richard para Passar a Considerar a configuraçăo de colunas de Peso / Quantidade
	lnQtC = Iif(crSigPrCpo.chkInstalas=2, crSigPrCpo.Pesos, crSigPrCpo.Qtds)

	Do Case
		Case crGru.nTipoJoals == 1
*			lnPesoPdrs = lnPesoPdrs + Iif(crSigPrCpo.UniCompos == crGru.cUniPs,crSigPrCpo.Qtds,crSigPrCpo.Pesos)
			lnPesoPdrs = lnPesoPdrs + lnQtC
		Case crGru.nTipoJoals == 2
*			If( crSigPrCpo.Etiqs = 'N' )
*				lnPesoBris = lnPesoBris + Iif(crSigPrCpo.UniCompos == crGru.cUniPs,crSigPrCpo.Qtds,crSigPrCpo.Pesos)
				lnPesoBris = lnPesoBris + lnQtC
*			Else
*				lnPesoPdrs = lnPesoPdrs + Iif(crSigPrCpo.UniCompos == crGru.cUniPs,crSigPrCpo.Qtds,crSigPrCpo.Pesos)
*				lnPesoPdrs = lnPesoPdrs + lnQtC
*			Endif				
		Case crGru.nTipoJoals == 3
*			lnPesoMetal = lnPesoMetal + Iif(crSigPrCpo.UniCompos == crGru.cUniPs,crSigPrCpo.Qtds,crSigPrCpo.Pesos)
			lnPesoMetal = lnPesoMetal + lnQtC
			cCodGarras = crSigPrCpo.Mats
		Case crGru.nTipoJoals == 6
*			lnPesoMetal = lnPesoMetal + Iif(crSigPrCpo.UniCompos == crGru.cUniPs And crSigPrCpo.UniCompos <> ' ',;
*						  crSigPrCpo.Qtds,Iif(CrSigPrCpo.cUniPs == crGru.cUniPs And CrSigPrCpo.cUniPs <> ' ', crSigPrCpo.Pesos, 0 ) )
			lnPesoMetal = lnPesoMetal + lnQtC
	EndCase
EndScan

With ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.PgDadosFaseP
	.getPesoPdrs.Value = lnPesoPdrs
	.getPesoBris.Value = lnPesoBris
	.getCodGarras.Value = cCodGarras  
	.getPesoMetal.Value = lnPesoMetal
EndWith

* Montando o Campo de Composiçăo Resumida
Wait Window 'Aguarde!!! Montando o Campo de Composiçăo Resumida...' NoWait
lcCom = []

Do Case
	Case InList(crSigCdGrp.MnCompos, 0, 1) && Automático
		lcQuery = [Select CGrus ] + ;
				    [From SigCdGrp ] + ;
				   [Where MtPrimas In (1,2) And ] + ;
				   		 [CGrus = '] + crSigCdPro.CGrus + [']

		If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'crTmp') < 1)
			=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (Salva - 1)')
			Wait Clear
			Return 0
		EndIf
		Go Top In crTmp
		If Eof('crTmp')
			Select *, 999 as DigiMaxs ;
			  From crSigPrCpo ;
			 Where 0 = 1 ;
			  Into Cursor crOrdCompos Readwrite
			Select crOrdCompos
			Index On Str(OrdCompos, 10) + Compos + Mats + DCompos Tag Ordem

			Select crSigPrCpo
			Scan
				If ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdPro', 'crTmp', 'Cpros', crSigPrCpo.Mats)
					Go Top In crTmp

					Replace Compos 	  With crTmp.Compos, ;
							DtMovs    With DateTime(),;
							OrdCompos With crTmp.OrdCompos In crSigPrCpo
							
					Select crSigPrCpo
					Scatter Memvar Memo
					m.DigiMaxs = crTmp.DigiMaxs
					Insert Into crOrdCompos From Memvar								
				EndIf
			EndScan

			Select crOrdCompos
			Scan
				llTem = .f.
				For I=1 To 30 Step 3
					If (Padr(Subs(lcCom, I, 3), 3, '_') = Padr(Subs(crOrdCompos.Compos, 1, 3), 3, '_')) And ;
					   (Padr(Subs(crOrdCompos.Compos, 1, 3), 3, '_') <> '___')
						llTem = .t.
					EndIf
				Next
				If Not llTem And (crOrdCompos.DigiMaxs > 0)
					lcCom = lcCom + Alltrim(Padr(crOrdCompos.Compos, 3, '_'))
				EndIf
			EndScan
			Replace Compos With lcCom In crSigCdPro
		EndIf

	Case (crSigCdGrp.MnCompos = 2) && Grupo + Classificaçăo
		Replace Compos With crSigCdPro.CGrus + crSigCdPro.CClass In crSigCdPro

	Case InList(crSigCdGrp.MnCompos, 3) && Classificaçăo dos Componentes
		Select Mats From CrSigPrCpo Where Etiqs = 'S' Into Cursor selecao Order by OrdTs
		
		Create Cursor CsClass (cods c(3))

		Select Selecao
		Scan
			If ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdPro', 'crTmp', 'Cpros', Selecao.Mats,[cClass])
				Go Top In crTmp
				Select CsClass
				Locate for Cods = CrTmp.cClass
				If Eof()
					Insert Into csClass (Cods ) Values (CrTmp.cClass)
					lcCom = lcCom + Alltrim(CrTmp.cClass)
				EndIf
			EndIf
		EndScan
		Replace Compos With lcCom In crSigCdPro
		
	Case (crSigCdGrp.MnCompos = 4) && Identificador + Código
		Replace Compos With Alltrim(crSigCdPro.idecpros) + Alltrim(crSigCdPro.Cpros) In crSigCdPro
EndCase
ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgComposicao.cntMtPrima.getCompos.Refresh()   

If !Empty(lcFiltro)
	Set Filter To &lcFiltro in crSigPrCpo
Endif	

If Between(lnReg,1,Reccount('crSigPrCpo'))
	Goto lnReg in crSigPrCpo
EndIf

If !Empty(lcArea)
	Select &lcArea
EndIf

Return
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE retresulttab
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE retresulttab
Lparameters pTipo, pMercs, pIndicador, pVlrCampo, pMask

Local lcChave, lcResult 

pVlrCampo = Iif(Type('pVlrCampo') <> 'C', Alltrim(Str(pVlrCampo)), pVlrCampo)

lcChave = pTipo+Padr(pMercs,3)+Padr(pIndicador,10)+pVlrCampo

lcQuery = [Select resultado from SigPrSic where cIdChaves = ']+lcChave+[']
If( ThisForm.poDataMgr.SQLExecute(lcQuery,[crSigPrSic]) < 1 )
	=MessageBox([Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!], 16, [Falha na Conexăo (crSigPrSic)])
	Return .F.		
EndIf

If Eof('crSigPrSic')
	If( pTipo == [I] )
		lcResult = Transform(fGerUniqueKey([IDENTIDADE]+pMercs+pIndicador),pMask)
	Else
		lcResult = Transform(fGerUniqueKey([CONCEITO]+pMercs+pIndicador),pMask)
	Endif		
	lcQuery = [Insert into SigPrSic(cTipos,Mercs,Indicador,ValorCmp,Resultado,cIdChaves) Values ('] + ;
				pTipo+[',']+pMercs+[',']+pIndicador+[',']+pVlrCampo+[',']+lcResult+[',']+lcChave+[')]
	ThisForm.poDataMgr.SQLExecute(lcQuery)
	ThisForm.poDataMgr.Commit()
Else
	lcResult = Alltrim(crSigPrSic.Resultado)
EndIf
Return(lcResult)


ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE montadescrs
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE montadescrs
Local lcDes, laCarac(5)

laCarac(1) = [ ]
laCarac(2) = [,]
laCarac(3) = [.]
laCarac(4) = [/]
laCarac(5) = [-]
 
Select Distinct CGrus, Linguas, TpMontas ;
  From crSigCdPrd ;
 Where CGrus = crSigCdPro.CGrus ;
 Order By TpMontas ;
  Into Cursor LocalMontas

Select LocalMontas
Scan
	lcDes = fGerDescritivo(ThisForm.poDataMgr, crSigCdPro.CPros, LocalMontas.TpMontas)

	If Not lcDes = Chr(254)
		If Not Empty(lcDes) And (LocalMontas.Linguas = 2) && Descriçăo Em Inglęs
			lcDes = lcDes + [ ]
			Select crSigCdDic
			Scan									
				For i = 1 to 5
					lcDes = Strtran(lcDes, Alltrim(crSigCdDic.Expressao)+laCarac(i), Alltrim(crSigCdDic.Traducao)+laCarac(i))
				EndFor	
			EndScan			
			lcDes = Alltrim(lcDes)
		EndIf

		Do Case
			Case (LocalMontas.TpMontas = 1) && Descriçăo do Produto	
				Replace DPros With lcDes In crSigCdPro

			Case (LocalMontas.TpMontas = 2) && Descriçăo de Compra	
				Replace DscCompras With lcDes In crSigCdPro

			Case (LocalMontas.TpMontas = 3) && Descriçăo Completa	
				Replace DPro3s With lcDes In crSigCdPro

			Case (LocalMontas.TpMontas = 4) && Observaçăo da Compra	
				Replace ObsCompras With lcDes In crSigCdPro

			Case (LocalMontas.TpMontas = 5) && Descriçăo Fiscal		
				Replace DescFis With lcDes In crSigCdPro

			Case (LocalMontas.TpMontas = 6) && Descriçăo ECF		
				Replace DescEcfs With lcDes In crSigCdPro
		EndCase
	EndIf
EndScan
* Fim **************************************************************************************
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE atualizapeso
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE atualizapeso
Private pGru

pGru = crSigCdPro.CGrus

Local lcdescricao,lcgrupo,lcunidade,lcfornecedor, total, xRegistro
Local lnvalor,lcmoeda,lnprecoc,lcmoedac,lnprecov,lcmoedav,lnfcusto,lcmoepc,lnfvenda,lcmoepv

oPagD = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgDados
oPagC = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgComposicao

Select crSigPrCpo
xRegistro = Recno()
ThisForm.FiltrarCompo(1)
Select crSigPrCpo
Count to _xnrg
If InList(ThisForm.pcEscolha, 'INSERIR','ALTERAR') And _xnrg > 0

	TotQtd   = 0
	Select crSigPrCpo
	Scan
		If Not Empty(crSigPrCpo.Mats)
			lcQuery = [Select a.cUnis, a.cUnips, b.BPesos ] + ;
					  [From SigCdPro a, SigCdGrp b ] + ;
					  [Where a.CPros = '] + crSigPrCpo.Mats + [' And ] + ;
					  [a.CGrus = b.CGrus]

			If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'crSomaGru') < 1)
				=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (crSomaGru - 1)')
				Return 0
			EndIf
			Go Top In crSomaGru
			If (InList(crSomaGru.BPesos,1,3))
				If Empty(crSigCdPro.MoePcs)
					With oPagC.getMoepc
						.Value = crSigPrCpo.Moeds
						.Refresh
					EndWith
				EndIf
				lcSql = [Select Fators From SigCdUni Where Cunis = ']+Iif(CrSomaGru.bPesos=1,CrSomaGru.Cunis,CrSomagru.CUnips)+[']
				=ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcsql,'LocalUni')
				lnFator = Iif(LocalUni.Fators = 0, 1, LocalUni.Fators )
				Select crSigPrCpo
				TotQtd = TotQtd + ( Iif(CrSomaGru.bPesos=1,crSigPrCpo.Qtds,CrSigPrCpo.Pesos) * lnFator )
			EndIf
		EndIf
		Select crSigPrCpo
	EndScan
	Select CrSigPrCpo
	Locate For Recno() = xRegistro
	
	If (TotQtd <> 0)
		With oPagC.getPesom
			.Value = TotQtd
			.Refresh
		EndWith
	EndIf
EndIf

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE chkforcomp
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE chkforcomp
IF !EMPTY(crSigCdPro.IFors) OR !EMPTY(crSigCdPro.Reffs) OR !empty(crSigCdPro.Colecoes)
	SELECT crSigPrCpo
	SCAN
		lcSql = [Select a.*, b.rClis From SigPrFnc a Inner Join SigCdCli b on b.iClis = a.IFors Where cPros = ']+crSigPrCpo.mats+[']
		lcSql = [Select * ] + ;
				    [From SigPrFnc ] + ;
				   [Where CPros = '] + crSigPrCpo.mats + ['] +;
				   [ AND IFors = ']+crSigCdPro.IFors+[']+;
				   [ And Reffs = ']+crSigCdPro.Reffs+[']+;
				   [ And Colecoes = ']+crSigCdPro.Colecoes+[']

		thisform.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcSql,'CrSigPrFnctmp')

		lachou = .t.
		SELECT CrSigPrFnctmp
		SCAN
			lnVal = CrSigPrFnctmp.pvens
			
			SELECT crSigPrCpo
			LOCATE FOR crSigPrCpo.Mats = CrSigPrFnctmp.cPros AND crSigPrCpo.PCompos = lnval		
			IF EOF()
				MESSAGEBOX([Material '] + CrSigPrFnctmp.cpros + [' com valor ] + ALLTRIM(TRANSFORM(lnval,'9,999,999.99')) + [ năo encontrado.],64,'Aviso')
				RETURN .f.
			ENDIF
			SELECT CrSigPrFnctmp
		ENDSCAN
	ENDSCAN
ENDIF
RETURN .t.

ENDPROC
