* PROCEDURE calcpremoe
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE calcpremoe
* No momento năo faz nada; futuramente podemos calcular os custos
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE calcvals
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE calcvals
* Calcula os Valores de Custo e Venda Pelas Moedas Informadas

* Calculando o Custo
If (Not Empty(crSigCdPro.Moecs) And Not Empty(crSigCdPro.MoePcs) And Not Empty(crSigCdPro.PftioCs) And ;
   (Not Empty(crSigCdPro.PCuss) Or  Not Empty(crSigCdPro.FCustos)))

	lnCt1 = fBuscarCotacao(crSigCdPro.Moecs,  Datetime(), ThisForm.poDataMgr)
	lnCt2 = fBuscarCotacao(crSigCdPro.MoePcs, Datetime(), ThisForm.poDataMgr)

	If Not Empty(crSigCdPro.PCuss)
		lnVal = (crSigCdPro.PCuss * lnCt1) / lnCt2
		lnVal = lnVal + ((lnVal * crSigCdPro.PftioCs) / 100)
		
		Replace FCustos With lnVal In crSigCdPro
		ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgComposicao.getFCusto.Refresh 
	Else
		lnVal = (crSigCdPro.FCustos / lnCt1) * lnCt2
		lnVal = lnVal - ((lnVal * crSigCdPro.PftioCs) / 100)

		Replace PCuss With lnVal In crSigCdPro
		ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgComposicao.getPcus.Refresh 
	EndIf
EndIf

* Calculo do Valor de Venda Pelo de Custo
lnCt1 = fBuscarCotacao(crSigCdPro.Moecs,  Datetime(), ThisForm.poDataMgr)
lnCt2 = fBuscarCotacao(crSigCdPro.Moedas, Datetime(), ThisForm.poDataMgr)
lnCt3 = fBuscarCotacao(crSigCdPro.Moevs,  Datetime(), ThisForm.poDataMgr)

If Not Empty(crSigCdPro.Margems)
	lnVal = (crSigCdPro.Pcuss * lnCt1) / lnCt2
	lnVal = lnVal + ((lnVal * crSigCdPro.Margems) / 100)
	Replace PVIdeals With lnVal In crSigCdPro
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgComposicao.getPvideal.Refresh 
EndIf

* Calculo de Valores de Venda
If (Not Empty(crSigCdPro.Moedas) And Not Empty(crSigCdPro.MoeVs) And Not Empty(crSigCdPro.MarkupA) And ;
   (Not Empty(crSigCdPro.PvIdeals) Or Not Empty(crSigCdPro.PVens)))
	* Se Tem Markup Informado e Valores de Custo Vai Recalcular os Valores de Venda Que Estiverem em Branco
	
	If Not Empty(crSigCdPro.Margems) Or Not Empty(crSigCdPro.PVIdeals)
		lnVal = (crSigCdPro.PVIdeals * lnCt2) / lnCt3
		lnVal = lnVal + ((lnVal * crSigCdPro.MarkupA) / 100)
		Replace PVens With lnVal In crSigCdPro
		ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgComposicao.getPVen.Refresh
	Else
		lnVal = (crSigCdPro.PVens / lnCt2) * lnCt3
		lnVal = lnVal - ((lnVal * crSigCdPro.MarkupA) / 100)
		Replace PvIdeals With lnVal In crSigCdPro
		ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgComposicao.getPvIdeal.Refresh
	EndIf
EndIf

* Fim **************************************************************************************
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE obrigatorios
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE obrigatorios
&& Subgrupo Obrigatório
lcCpo = Alltrim(crSigCdPro.SGrus)
If (crSigCdGrp.ObrSGrus = 1) And Empty(lcCpo)
	=MessageBox([O Subgrupo Necessita Ser Preenchido Neste Grupo!!!], 0+16, [Dados Incompletos!!!])
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.ActivePage = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.PageOrder 
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.getCSGru.SetFocus 
	Return .f.
EndIf

&& Classificaçăo Fiscal Obrigatória
lcCpo = Alltrim(Strtran(crSigCdPro.ClFiscals, [.], []))
If (crSigCdGrp.ObrigFiscs = 1) And Empty(lcCpo)
	=MessageBox([A Classificaçăo Fiscal Necessita Ser Preenchida Neste Grupo!!!], 0+16, [Dados Incompletos!!!])
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.ActivePage = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDadosFiscais.PageOrder 
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDadosFiscais.getClfiscal.SetFocus 
	Return .f.
EndIf

&& Identificador Obrigatório
lcCpo = Alltrim(crSigCdPro.IdeCPros)
If (crSigCdGrp.ObrIdecs = 1) And Empty(lcCpo)
	=MessageBox([O Identificador Necessita Ser Preenchido Neste Grupo!!!], 0+16, [Dados Incompletos!!!])
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.ActivePage = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.PageOrder 
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.getIdeCPros.SetFocus 
	Return .f.
EndIf

&& Classificaçăo Obrigatória
lcCpo = Alltrim(crSigCdPro.CClass)
If (crSigCdGrp.ObrCclas = 1) And Empty(lcCpo)
	lcStr = Alltrim(Chrtran(thisform.pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.lblClassificacao.Caption,':',''))
	=MessageBox(lcStr + [ Necessita Ser Preenchida Neste Grupo!!!], 0+16, [Dados Incompletos!!!])
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.ActivePage = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.PageOrder 
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.get_Class.SetFocus 
	Return .f.
EndIf

&& Modelo Obrigatório
lcCpo = Alltrim(crSigCdPro.CodFinP)
If (crSigCdGrp.ObrFinps = 1) And Empty(lcCpo)
	lcStr = Alltrim(Chrtran(thisform.pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.lblModelo.Caption,':',''))
	=MessageBox(lcStr + [ Necessita Ser Preenchida Neste Grupo!!!], 0+16, [Dados Incompletos!!!])
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.ActivePage = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.PageOrder 
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.getCodFinP.SetFocus 
	Return .f.
EndIf

&& Linha Obrigatória
lcCpo = Alltrim(crSigCdPro.Linhas)
If (crSigCdGrp.ObrLinha = 1) And Empty(lcCpo)
	=MessageBox([A Linha Necessita Ser Preenchida Neste Grupo!!!], 0+16, [Dados Incompletos!!!])
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.ActivePage = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.PageOrder 
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.getLin.SetFocus 
	Return .f.
EndIf

&& Grupo de Venda Obrigatório
lcCpo = Alltrim(crSigCdPro.Colecoes)
If (crSigCdGrp.ObrColec = 1) And Empty(lcCpo)
	=MessageBox([O Grupo de Venda Necessita Ser Preenchido Neste Grupo!!!], 0+16, [Dados Incompletos!!!])
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.ActivePage = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.PageOrder 
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.getCol.SetFocus 
	Return .f.
EndIf

&& Dimensőes Obrigatória
If (crSigCdGrp.ObrDimes = 1) And Empty(crSigCdPro.TamPs) And Empty(crSigCdPro.TamHs) And Empty(crSigCdPro.TamLs)
	=MessageBox([Dimensőes Necessitam Ser Preenchidas Neste Grupo!!!], 0+16, [Dados Incompletos!!!])
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.ActivePage = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.PageOrder 
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.fwget6.SetFocus 
	Return .f.
EndIf

&& Cor Obrigatória
If (crSigCdGrp.AJPvens = 1) And Empty(crSigCdPro.CodCors)
	=MessageBox([A Cor Necessita Ser Preenchida Neste Grupo!!!], 0+16, [Dados Incompletos!!!])
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.ActivePage = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.PageOrder 
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.getCor.SetFocus 
	Return .f.
EndIf

&& Imagem Obrigatória
If (crSigCdGrp.ObrFigJpgs = 1) And IsEmpty(crSigCdPro.FigJpgs) 
	=MessageBox([A Foto do Produto Precisa Ser Preenchida Neste Grupo!!!], 0+16, [Dados Incompletos!!!])
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.ActivePage = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.PageOrder 
	Return .f.
EndIf

&& Produto Equivalente Obrigatório
lcCpo = Alltrim(crSigCdPro.CProEqs)
If (Not Empty(Substr(crSigCdGrp.CfgGerGprs, 1, 1))) And Empty(lcCpo)
	=MessageBox([O Produto Equivalente Necessita Ser Preenchido Neste Grupo!!!], 0+16, [Dados Incompletos!!!])
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.ActivePage = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.PageOrder 
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.get_CProEq.SetFocus 
	Return .f.
EndIf

&& Tamanho Mínimo da Referęncia do Fornecedor
lcCpo = Alltrim(crSigCdPro.Reffs)
lnMin = Int(Val(Substr(crSigCdGrp.CfgGerGprs, 3, 2)))
If (lnMin > 0) And (Len(Alltrim(lcCpo)) < lnMin)
	=MessageBox([A Ref. do Fornecedor Necessita Ser Preenchida] + Chr(13) + ;
				[Com No Mínimo ] + Alltrim(Str(lnMin, 12, 0)) + [ Caracteres Neste Grupo!!!], ;
				0+16, [Dados Incompletos!!!])
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.ActivePage = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.PageOrder 
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.getRefs.SetFocus 
	Return .f.
EndIf

&& Tamanho Mínimo da Observaçăo de Componente
lcCpo = Alltrim(crSigCdPro.ObsEtqs)
lnMin = Int(Val(Substr(crSigCdGrp.CfgGerGprs, 7, 2)))
If (lnMin > 0) And (Len(Alltrim(lcCpo)) < lnMin)
	=MessageBox([A Obs. do Componente Necessita Ser Preenchida] + Chr(13) + ;
				[Com No Mínimo ] + Alltrim(Str(lnMin, 12, 0)) + [ Caracteres Neste Grupo!!!], ;
				0+16, [Dados Incompletos!!!])
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.ActivePage = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.PageOrder 
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.getObs3.SetFocus
	Return .f.
EndIf

*** Tiago - 12/05/2014 - Incluído a pedido do Richard
&& Compos Obrigatório
lcCpo = Alltrim(crSigCdPro.Compos)
If (Int(Val(Substr(crSigCdGrp.CfgGerGprs, 16, 1))) = 1 And Empty(lcCpo))
	*** mena - 22/07/2015 - gera campo compos conforme tabela de intervalos de valores ***
	lcCheTp = ''
	lcCheVal=''
	&& mena 22/07/2015 foi incluida esta tabela para gerar compos conforme os intervalos de valores
	lcSql = [Select * From SigcdCpo Where grupos = ']+crSigCdPro.cgrus+[']
	ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcSql,'crSigCdCpo')

	SELECT crSigcdCpo
	GO top
	IF !EOF()
		lcFi = crSigCdPro.codfinp
		lcCl = crSigCdPro.cClass
		lcSg = crSigCdPro.sgrus
		lcLi = crSigCdPro.linhas
		lcPv = crSigCdPro.pvens
		lcPc = crSigCdPro.pcuss
		
		lcCheTp = 	IIF(crSigcdCpo.tipos='MODELO',   [ and vltps = lcFi ], ;
					IIF(crSigcdCpo.tipos='CLASSIFICA', [ and vltps = lcCl ], ;
					IIF(crSigcdCpo.tipos='SUBGRUPO', [ and vltps = lcSg ], ;
					IIF(crSigcdCpo.tipos='LINHA',    [ and vltps = lcLi ],[]))))
		lcCheVal=	IIF(crSigcdCpo.valors='PV',    	 [ and fxinis <= lcPv and fxfins > lcPv ], ;
					IIF(crSigcdCpo.valors='PC',    	 [ and fxinis <= lcPc and fxfins > lcPc ], []))

		lcQ = [SELECT * from crsigcdcpo where 1=1 ]+lcCheTp + lcCheVal + [ into cursor crCpo]
		&lcQ	&& executa a querie
		SELECT crCpo
		GO top
		lcCpo = crCpo.compos
		replace compos with lcCpo in crSigcdPro
	endif
	***************************************************************************************
	SELECT crSigcdPro
	
	IF EMPTY(lcCpo)
	    =MessageBox([A Composiçăo do Produto Necessita Ser Preenchida Neste Grupo!!!], 0+16, [Dados Incompletos!!!])
	    ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.ActivePage = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgComposicao.PageOrder 
	    ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgComposicao.cntMtPrima.getCompos.SetFocus
	    Return .f.
	ENDIF
Endif

*** Tiago - 29/06/2015 - Vianna - Material principal obrigatório
If Int(Val(Substr(crSigCdGrp.CfgGerGprs, 39, 1))) = 1 And Empty(crSigCdPro.MatPrincs)
	=MessageBox([Material Principal necessita ser preenchido neste grupo!!!], 0+16, [Dados Incompletos!!!])
    ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.ActivePage = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgComposicao.PageOrder
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgComposicao.get_matP.SetFocus()
    Return .f.
Endif

Return .t.
* Fim **************************************************************************************
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE preenchimento
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE preenchimento
Go Top In crSigCdGrp

&& Classificaçăo Fiscal 
lcCpo = Alltrim(crSigCdGrp.ClFiscals)
If Not Empty(lcCpo)
	Replace ClFiscals With lcCpo In crSigCdPro
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDadosFiscais.getClfiscal.Refresh 
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDadosFiscais.getClfiscal.Valid()
EndIf

&& Identificador 
lcCpo = Alltrim(crSigCdGrp.IdeCPros)
If Not Empty(lcCpo)
	Replace IdeCPros With lcCpo In crSigCdPro
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.getIdeCPros.Refresh
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.getIdeCPros.Valid()
EndIf

&& Classificaçăo 
lcCpo = Alltrim(crSigCdGrp.PadCclas)
If Not Empty(lcCpo)
	Replace CClass With lcCpo In crSigCdPro
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.get_Class.Refresh
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.get_Class.Valid()
EndIf

&& Modelo 
lcCpo = Alltrim(crSigCdGrp.PadFinPs)
If Not Empty(lcCpo)
	Replace CodFinP With lcCpo In crSigCdPro
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.getCodFinP.Refresh
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.getCodFinP.Valid()
EndIf

&& Linha Obrigatória
lcCpo = Alltrim(crSigCdGrp.PadLinha)
If Not Empty(lcCpo)
	Replace Linhas With lcCpo In crSigCdPro
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.getLin.Refresh
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.getLin.Valid()
EndIf

&& Grupo de Venda Obrigatório
lcCpo = Alltrim(crSigCdGrp.PadColec)
If Not Empty(lcCpo)
	Replace Colecoes With lcCpo In crSigCdPro
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.getCol.Refresh
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.getCol.Valid()
EndIf

Return .t.
* Fim **************************************************************************************
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE carregainstal
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE carregainstal
Lparameters pMat

lcQuery = [Select b.chkInstalas ] + ;
			[From SigCdPro a, SigCdGrp b ] + ;
		   [Where a.CPros = '] + pMat + [' And ] + ;
		   		 [a.CGrus = b.CGrus]

If ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery,'LocalInstal') < 1
	=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (LocalInstal)')
	Return .f.
EndIf
Go Top In LocalInstal

Replace chkInstalas With LocalInstal.chkInstalas In crSigPrCpo

Return .t.
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE calcprecpm
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE calcprecpm
* Cálculo Para Custo x Peso x MKP Vda // Criado por Richard para Vianna em 14/08/2012
Local lnFct, lnFat, lcMda, lnEqv, lnMPC, lnMFC, lnTct, lnMFC, lnMTC, lnPrI, lnAdi, lnMPI, lnFid, lnPat, lnMTV

* Calculando o "Fator de Custo"
lnFct = crSigCdPro.Pcuss + crSigCdPro.PFTioCs
lnFat = 1

If Empty(crSigCdPro.MoeCs) And Not Empty(crSigCdPro.MoePcs)
	Replace MoeCs With crSigCdPro.MoePcs In crSigCdpro
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.PgframeDados.pgComposicao.getMoeC.Refresh
EndIf

If Not Empty(crSigCdPro.MoeCs) And Empty(crSigCdPro.MoePcs)
	Replace MoePCs With crSigCdPro.MoeCs In crSigCdpro
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.PgframeDados.pgComposicao.getMoePC.Refresh
EndIf

If (crSigCdPro.MoeCs <> crSigCdPro.MoePcs) And Not Empty(crSigCdPro.MoeCs)
	ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdMoe', 'crMoe', 'CMoes', crSigCdPro.MoeCs)
	Go Top In crMoe
	lcMda = Iif(Empty(crMoe.MoeQs), crSigCdPro.MoeCs, crMoe.MoeQs)
	lnEqv = Iif(Empty(crMoe.QtdEqs) Or Empty(crMoe.Moeqs), 1, crMoe.QtdEqs)
	lnMPC = fBuscarCotacao(lcMda, DateTime(), ThisForm.poDataMgr) * lnEqv

	ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdMoe', 'crMoe', 'CMoes', crSigCdPro.MoePcs)
	Go Top In crMoe
	lcMda = Iif(Empty(crMoe.MoeQs), crSigCdPro.MoePcs, crMoe.MoeQs)
	lnEqv = Iif(Empty(crMoe.QtdEqs) Or Empty(crMoe.Moeqs), 1, crMoe.QtdEqs)
	lnMFC = fBuscarCotacao(lcMda, DateTime(), ThisForm.poDataMgr) * lnEqv

	lnFat = lnMPC / lnMFC
EndIf

Replace FCustos With lnFct * lnFat In crSigCdPro
ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.PgframeDados.pgComposicao.getFCusto.Refresh

* Calculando o "Total de Custo"
lnTct = crSigCdPro.FCustos * crSigCdPro.PesoMs
lnFat = 1

If Empty(crSigCdPro.MoeCusFs) And Not Empty(crSigCdPro.MoePcs)
	Replace MoeCusFs With crSigCdPro.MoePcs In crSigCdPro
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.PgframeDados.pgComposicao.getMoePc.Refresh
EndIf

If (crSigCdPro.MoeCusFs <> crSigCdPro.MoePcs) And Not Empty(crSigCdPro.MoeCusFs)
	ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdMoe', 'crMoe', 'CMoes', crSigCdPro.MoePcs)
	Go Top In crMoe
	lcMda = Iif(Empty(crMoe.MoeQs), crSigCdPro.MoeCs, crMoe.MoeQs)
	lnEqv = Iif(Empty(crMoe.QtdEqs) Or Empty(crMoe.Moeqs), 1, crMoe.QtdEqs)
	lnMFC = fBuscarCotacao(lcMda, DateTime(), ThisForm.poDataMgr) * lnEqv

	ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdMoe', 'crMoe', 'CMoes', crSigCdPro.MoeCusFs)
	Go Top In crMoe
	lcMda = Iif(Empty(crMoe.MoeQs), crSigCdPro.MoeCusFs, crMoe.MoeQs)
	lnEqv = Iif(Empty(crMoe.QtdEqs) Or Empty(crMoe.Moeqs), 1, crMoe.QtdEqs)
	lnMTC = fBuscarCotacao(lcMda, DateTime(), ThisForm.poDataMgr) * lnEqv

	lnFat = lnMFC / lnMTC
EndIf

Replace CustoFs With lnTct * lnFat In crSigCdPro
ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.PgframeDados.pgComposicao.getCustoF.Refresh

* Calculando o "Fator Ideal de Venda"
If Not Empty(crSigCdPro.CustoFs)
	If Empty(crSigCdPro.Margems) And Not Empty(crSigCdPro.PVIdeals)
		Replace Margems With crSigCdPro.PVIdeals / crSigCdPro.CustoFs In crSigCdPro
		ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.PgframeDados.pgComposicao.getMargem.Refresh
	EndIf

	If Not Empty(crSigCdPro.MoeCusFs) And Empty(crSigCdPro.Moedas)
		Replace Moedas With crSigCdPro.MoeCusFs In crSigCdPro
		ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.PgframeDados.pgComposicao.getMoeda.Refresh
	EndIf	

	* Calculando o "Preço Ideal"
	lnPrI = crSigCdPro.CustoFs * crSigCdPro.Margems 
	lnFat = 1
	lnAdi = crSigCdPro.PfTios

	If (crSigCdPro.MoeCusFs <> crSigCdPro.Moedas) And Not Empty(crSigCdPro.MoeCusFs)
		ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdMoe', 'crMoe', 'CMoes', crSigCdPro.MoeCusFs)
		Go Top In crMoe
		lcMda = Iif(Empty(crMoe.MoeQs), crSigCdPro.MoeCusFs, crMoe.MoeQs)
		lnEqv = Iif(Empty(crMoe.QtdEqs) Or Empty(crMoe.Moeqs), 1, crMoe.QtdEqs)
		lnMTC = fBuscarCotacao(lcMda, DateTime(), ThisForm.poDataMgr) * lnEqv

		ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdMoe', 'crMoe', 'CMoes', crSigCdPro.Moedas)
		Go Top In crMoe
		lcMda = Iif(Empty(crMoe.MoeQs), crSigCdPro.Moedas, crMoe.MoeQs)
		lnEqv = Iif(Empty(crMoe.QtdEqs) Or Empty(crMoe.Moeqs), 1, crMoe.QtdEqs)
		lnMPI = fBuscarCotacao(lcMda, DateTime(), ThisForm.poDataMgr) * lnEqv

		lnFat = lnMTC / lnMPI
	EndIf

	Replace PVIDeals With lnPrI * lnFat In crSigCdPro
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.PgframeDados.pgComposicao.getPVIdeal.Refresh	

	* Calculando o "Fator  Ideal"
	If Empty(crSigCdPro.MfTios) And Not Empty(crSigCdPro.Moedas)
		Replace MfTios With crSigCdPro.Moedas In crSigCdPro
		ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.PgframeDados.pgComposicao.get_Mftio.Refresh
	EndIf	
		
	* Checando se Possui Valor Adicional
	If Not Empty(crSigCdPro.PfTios) And (crSigCdPro.MfTios <> crSigCdPro.Moedas) And Not Empty(crSigCdPro.Moedas)
		ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdMoe', 'crMoe', 'CMoes', crSigCdPro.MoeCusFs)
		Go Top In crMoe
		lcMda = Iif(Empty(crMoe.MoeQs), crSigCdPro.MoeCusFs, crMoe.MoeQs)
		lnEqv = Iif(Empty(crMoe.QtdEqs) Or Empty(crMoe.Moeqs), 1, crMoe.QtdEqs)
		lnMTC = fBuscarCotacao(lcMda, DateTime(), ThisForm.poDataMgr) * lnEqv

		ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdMoe', 'crMoe', 'CMoes', crSigCdPro.Moedas)
		Go Top In crMoe
		lcMda = Iif(Empty(crMoe.MoeQs), crSigCdPro.Moedas, crMoe.MoeQs)
		lnEqv = Iif(Empty(crMoe.QtdEqs) Or Empty(crMoe.Moeqs), 1, crMoe.QtdEqs)
		lnMPI = fBuscarCotacao(lcMda, DateTime(), ThisForm.poDataMgr) * lnEqv

		lnAdi = lnAdi * (lnMTC / lnMPI)
	EndIf

	lnFid = crSigCdPro.PVIDeals + lnAdi
	
	Replace FIDeals With lnFId In crSigCdPro
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.PgframeDados.pgComposicao.getFIdeals.Refresh

	* Calculando o "Preço Atual"
	If Empty(crSigCdPro.MarkupA)
		Replace MarkupA With 1 In crSigCdPro
		ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.PgframeDados.pgComposicao.getMarkupA.Refresh	
	EndIf

	lnPat = crSigCdPro.FIdeals * crSigCdPro.MarkupA
	lnFat = 1

	If Not Empty(crSigCdPro.Moedas) And Empty(crSigCdPro.Moevs)
		Replace Moevs With crSigCdPro.Moedas In crSigCdPro
		ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.PgframeDados.pgComposicao.getMoev.Refresh
	EndIf	

	If (crSigCdPro.Moevs <> crSigCdPro.Moedas) And Not Empty(crSigCdPro.Moevs)
		ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdMoe', 'crMoe', 'CMoes', crSigCdPro.Moedas)
		Go Top In crMoe
		lcMda = Iif(Empty(crMoe.MoeQs), crSigCdPro.Moedas, crMoe.MoeQs)
		lnEqv = Iif(Empty(crMoe.QtdEqs) Or Empty(crMoe.Moeqs), 1, crMoe.QtdEqs)
		lnMPI = fBuscarCotacao(lcMda, DateTime(), ThisForm.poDataMgr) * lnEqv

		ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdMoe', 'crMoe', 'CMoes', crSigCdPro.Moevs)
		Go Top In crMoe
		lcMda = Iif(Empty(crMoe.MoeQs), crSigCdPro.Moevs, crMoe.MoeQs)
		lnEqv = Iif(Empty(crMoe.QtdEqs) Or Empty(crMoe.Moeqs), 1, crMoe.QtdEqs)
		lnMTV = fBuscarCotacao(lcMda, DateTime(), ThisForm.poDataMgr) * lnEqv

		lnFat = lnMPI / lnMTV
	EndIf
	
	Replace PVens With lnPat * lnFat In crSigCdPro
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.PgframeDados.pgComposicao.getPVen.Refresh	
EndIf
* Fim **************************************************************************************


ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE atupesos
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE atupesos
* Richard em 23/10/2013 - Rotina que irá apanhar os pesos médios cadastrados
* em cada componente e os atualizará na grade de componentes deste produto. 
Local llAtu

Select crSigPrCpo
Scan
	llAtu = .f.
	lnMtl = 1
	
	If Not Empty(crSigPrCpo.Mats)
		lcQuery = [Select a.PesoMs, b.CfgGerGprs ] + ;
				    [From SigCdPro a, SigCdGrp b ] + ;
				   [Where a.CPros = '] + crSigPrCpo.Mats + [' And ] + ;
				   		 [a.CGrus = b.CGrus]

		If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, [LocalProCp]) < 1)
			=MessageBox([Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!], 16, [Falha na Conexăo (LocalProCp 1)])
			=MessageBox([Os Pesos Podem Năo Ter Sido Calculados! Refaça o Processo!], 16, [Atençăo!!!])
			Return .f.
		EndIf
		Go Top In LocalProCp
		If Not Eof([LocalProCp]) And (LocalProCp.PesoMs > 0) And (Int(Val(Substr(LocalProCp.CfgGerGprs, 9, 1))) > 1)
			If (Int(Val(Substr(LocalProCp.CfgGerGprs, 9, 1))) = 2) && Lança na Unidade 1
				If Not Empty(crSigPrCpo.UniCompos) And (crSigPrCpo.Qtds <> LocalProCp.PesoMs)
					If Not Empty(crSigPrCpo.CUniPs) And (crSigPrCpo.Pesos > 0)
						lnMtl = crSigPrCpo.Pesos
					EndIf 
					
					Replace Qtds With LocalProCp.PesoMs * lnMtl In crSigPrCpo
					llAtu = .t.
				EndIf
			Else && Lança na Unidade 2
				If Not Empty(crSigPrCpo.CUniPs) And (crSigPrCpo.Pesos <> LocalProCp.PesoMs)
					If Not Empty(crSigPrCpo.UniCompos) And (crSigPrCpo.Qtds > 0)
						lnMtl = crSigPrCpo.Qtds
					EndIf 

					Replace Pesos With LocalProCp.PesoMs * lnMtl In crSigPrCpo
					llAtu = .t.
				EndIf
			EndIf
			Use In LocalProCp
		EndIf
	EndIf

	If llAtu
		Select crSigPrCpo
		ThisForm.Atuapreco()
		ThisForm.CalcFornec(crSigPrCpo.Mats)
		ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgComposicao.cmdgCompo.cmdCompoAtualiza.Click()
	EndIf
EndScan
* Fim **************************************************************************************
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE variacaocusto
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE variacaocusto
parameters pCusto
lnRet = pCusto

If Not Empty(pCusto)
	ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdGrp', 'crGrupo', 'cGrus', crSigCdPro.cGrus)
	ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdPro', 'LocalPro', 'Cpros', crSigCdPro.Cpros)
	CFalhb    = crGrupo.VarCustots
	CustoReal = pCusto
	xCusto    = CustoReal

	If ( xCusto <> LocalPro.custofs) And Not Empty(CFalhb)
		xDif = (((xCusto / LocalPro.custofs) -1) * 100 )
		If ( xDif < ( CFalhb * -1 ) ) Or ( xDif > CFalhb And crSigCdPam.Sinals <> 2 )
			lcMsg = 'Custo Diferente do Custo da Tabela e fora do Limite de '+Transf(CFalhb,"@Z 999999.99%")+Chr(13)+;
				'Tabela: '+Alltrim(Transf(LocalPro.custofs,"@Z 999999.999"))+' Real:'+Alltrim(Transform(xCusto,"@Z 999999.999"))+' Dif. '+Transf(xDif,"@Z 999999.99%")
			Messagebox( lcMsg, 32, '' )
			If Not fChecaAcesso('SIGCDPRO','LIBCUSTOTS')
				lnRet = LocalPro.custofs
			Else
				lnRet = CustoReal
			Endif
		Endif
	EndIf
EndIf 
Return lnRet
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE msv_excluir
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE msv_excluir
Private pPro, llOK

pPro = Iif(Empty(crSigCdPro.CPros), Replicate(Chr(254), 14), crSigCdPro.CPros)

llOK = .t.

* Eliminando os Registros
If llOK
	If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SQLExecute([Delete From SigOpArq Where fkChaves = '] + Padr(pPro, 30) + ['], '') < 1)
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (msv_excluir - 1.0a)')
		llOK = .f.
	EndIf
EndIf
If llOK
	If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SQLExecute([Delete From SigCdPro Where CPros = ?pPro], '') < 1)
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (msv_excluir - 1.0)')
		llOK = .f.
	EndIf
EndIf
If llOK
	If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SQLExecute([Delete From SigPrMdl Where CPros = ?pPro], '') < 1)
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (msv_excluir - 1)')
		llOK = .f.
	EndIf
EndIf
If llOK
	If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SQLExecute([Delete From SigCdPrf Where Produtos = ?pPro], '') < 1)
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (msv_excluir - 2)')
		llOK = .f.
	EndIf
EndIf
If llOK
	If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SQLExecute([Delete From SigPrCpo Where CPros = ?pPro], '') < 1)
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (msv_excluir - 3)')
		llOK = .f.
	EndIf
EndIf
If llOK
	If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SQLExecute([Delete From SigPrPmi Where CPros = ?pPro], '') < 1)
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (msv_excluir - 4)')
		llOK = .f.
	EndIf
EndIf
If llOK
	If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SQLExecute([Delete From SigPrCrr Where CPros = ?pPro], '') < 1)
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (msv_excluir - 4.1)')
		llOK = .f.
	EndIf
EndIf
If llOK
	If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SQLExecute([Delete From SigCdPft Where CPros = ?pPro], '') < 1)
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (msv_excluir - 4.2)')
		llOK = .f.
	EndIf
EndIf
If llOK
	If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SQLExecute([Delete From SigSubCp Where CPros = ?pPro], '') < 1)
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (msv_excluir - 4.5)')
		llOK = .f.
	EndIf
EndIf
If llOK
	If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SQLExecute([Delete From SigCdCat Where Cods = '] + Left(pPro,6) + ['], '') < 1)
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (msv_excluir - 4.6)')
		llOK = .f.
	EndIf
EndIf
If llOK
	If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SQLExecute([Delete From SigCdSvc Where cCats = '] + Left(pPro,6) + ['], '') < 1)
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (msv_excluir - 4.7)')
		llOK = .f.
	EndIf
EndIf
If llOK
	If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SQLExecute([Delete From SigPrFnc Where CPros = ?pPro], '') < 1)
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (msv_excluir - 4.8)')
		llOK = .f.
	EndIf
EndIf
If llOK
	If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SQLExecute([Delete From SigPrTam Where CPros = ?pPro], '') < 1)
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (msv_excluir - 4.9)')
		llOK = .f.
	EndIf
EndIf
If llOK
	If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SQLExecute([Delete From SigPrCar Where CPros = ?pPro], '') < 1)
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (msv_excluir - 4.10)')
		llOK = .f.
	EndIf
EndIf
If llOK
	If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SQLExecute([Delete From SigOpArq Where fkChaves = '] + Padr(pPro, 30) + ['], '') < 1)
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (msv_excluir - 4.11)')
		llOK = .f.
	EndIf
EndIf


* Excluindo os Registros
If llOK
	If Not ThisForm.poDataMgr.Update('crSigCdPrc')
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (msv_excluir - 5)')
		llOK = .f.
	EndIf
EndIf
If llOK
	If Not ThisForm.poDataMgr.Update('crSigPrMdc')
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (msv_excluir - 6)')
		llOK = .f.
	EndIf
EndIf
If llOK
	If Not ThisForm.poDataMgr.Update('crSigCdPfc')
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (msv_excluir - 7)')
		llOK = .f.
	EndIf
EndIf
If llOK
	If Not ThisForm.poDataMgr.Update('crSigPrMt2')
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (msv_excluir - 7.1)')
		llOK = .f.
	EndIf
EndIf
If llOK
	If Not ThisForm.poDataMgr.Update('crSigPrCp2')
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (msv_excluir - 8)')
		llOK = .f.
	EndIf
EndIf
If llOK
	If Not ThisForm.poDataMgr.Update('crSigPrCrr')
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (msv_excluir - 9)')
		llOK = .f.
	EndIf
EndIf
If llOK
	If Not ThisForm.poDataMgr.Update('crSigSubC2')
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (msv_excluir - 10)')
		llOK = .f.
	EndIf
EndIf
If llOK
	If Not ThisForm.poDataMgr.Update('crSigPrTa2')
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (msv_excluir - 11)')
		llOK = .f.
	EndIf
Endif
If llOK
	If Not ThisForm.poDataMgr.Update('crSigPrCa2')
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (msv_excluir - 12)')
		llOK = .f.
	EndIf
Endif

If llOK
	=fGravarLog('E', 'CADPRO', 'EXCLUIR', 'O Produto [' + Alltrim(crListaPro.CPros) + '], Cód. Barras  '+;
				  Alltrim(Str(crListaPro.cbars)) + ' Foi Excluido.' , Usuar)

	Delete From crProcurar Where CPros = pPro

	With ThisForm
		.poDataMgr.Commit()
		=fGravarLog('C',ThisForm.Name,'EXCLUIR',;
					('Tabela('+.poDataMgr.pfSqlTabela(2).pcTabela+;
					 ') C.P.('+.poDataMgr.pfSqlTabela(2).pcChaveprimaria+')='+;
					 Alltrim(Transform(Evaluate(.poDataMgr.pfSqlTabela(2).pcNomecursor+'.'+.poDataMgr.pfSqlTabela(2).pcChaveprimaria)))),;
					 Iif(Type('m.usuar')=='C',m.usuar,''))
	EndWith
Else
	ThisForm.poDataMgr.Rollback()
	Return 0
EndIf
NoDefault
* Fim *********************************************************************************
ENDPROC

		Gather MemVar Memo
	EndIf

	With ThisForm
		.poDataMgr.Commit()

						('Tabela('+.poDataMgr.pfSqlTabela(2).pcTabela+;
						 ') C.P.('+.poDataMgr.pfSqlTabela(2).pcChaveprimaria+')='+;

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE msv_inserir
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE msv_inserir
Private pPro, llOK

pPro = Iif(Empty(crSigCdPro.CPros), Replicate(Chr(254), 14), crSigCdPro.CPros)

llOK = .t.

* Incluindo os Registros
If llOK
	If Not ThisForm.poDataMgr.Update('crSigCdPro')
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (msv_Inserir - 1.0)')
		llOK = .f.
	EndIf
EndIf
If llOK
	If Not ThisForm.poDataMgr.Update('crSigPrMdl')
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (msv_Inserir - 1)')

		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (msv_Inserir - 2)')

If llOK
	If Not ThisForm.poDataMgr.Update('crSigPrCpo')
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (msv_Inserir - 3)')

	EndIf
EndIf
If llOK
	If Not ThisForm.poDataMgr.Update('crSigPrPmi')
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (msv_Inserir - 4)')
		llOK = .f.
	EndIf
EndIf
If llOK
	If Not ThisForm.poDataMgr.Update('crSigCdPrc')
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (msv_Inserir - 5)')
		llOK = .f.
	EndIf
EndIf
If llOK
	If Not ThisForm.poDataMgr.Update('crSigPrMdc')
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (msv_Inserir - 6)')
		llOK = .f.
	EndIf
EndIf
If llOK
	If Not ThisForm.poDataMgr.Update('crSigCdPfc')
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (msv_Inserir - 7)')
		llOK = .f.
	EndIf
EndIf
If llOK
	If Not ThisForm.poDataMgr.Update('crSigPrMt2')
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (msv_Inserir - 7.1)')
		llOK = .f.
	EndIf
EndIf
If llOK
	If Not ThisForm.poDataMgr.Update('crSigPrCp2')
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (msv_Inserir - 8)')
		llOK = .f.
	EndIf
EndIf
If llOK
	If Not ThisForm.poDataMgr.Update('crSigPrCrr')
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (msv_Inserir - 9)')
		llOK = .f.
	EndIf
EndIf
If llOK
	If not ThisForm.podatamgr.Update('crSigPrFnc')
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (msv_Inserir - 9.8)')
		llOK = .f.
	Endif 
Endif
If llOK
	If Not ThisForm.poDataMgr.Update('CrSigCdCat')
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (msv_Alterar - 13.4)')
		llOK = .f.
	EndIf
EndIf
If llOK
	If Not ThisForm.poDataMgr.Update('crSigCdSvc')
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (msv_Alterar - 13.5)')
		llOK = .f.
	EndIf
EndIf
If llOK And Not ThisForm.Copiando
	If Not ThisForm.poDataMgr.Update('crSigCdPft')
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (msv_Inserir - 10)')
		llOK = .f.
	EndIf
EndIf
If llOK
	If Not ThisForm.poDataMgr.Update('crSigSubCp')
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (msv_Inserir - 14)')
		llOK = .f.
	EndIf
EndIf
If llOK
	If Not ThisForm.poDataMgr.Update('crSigSubC2')
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (msv_Inserir - 15)')
		llOK = .f.
	EndIf
EndIf
If llOK
	If Not ThisForm.poDataMgr.Update('crSigPrTam')
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (msv_Inserir - 16)')
		llOK = .f.
	EndIf
EndIf
If llOK
	If Not ThisForm.poDataMgr.Update('crSigPrCar')
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (msv_Inserir - 17)')
		llOK = .f.
	EndIf
EndIf
If llOK
	If Not ThisForm.poDataMgr.Update('crSigPrTa2')
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (msv_Inserir - 18)')
		llOK = .f.
	EndIf
EndIf
If llOK
	If Not ThisForm.poDataMgr.Update('crSigPrCa2')
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (msv_Inserir - 19)')
		llOK = .f.
	EndIf
EndIf
If llOK
	If Not ThisForm.poDataMgr.Update('crSigPrTar')
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (msv_Inserir - 20)')
		llOK = .f.
	EndIf
EndIf
If llOK
	If Not ThisForm.poDataMgr.Update('crSigPrArq')
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (msv_Inserir - 21)')
		llOK = .f.
	EndIf
EndIf

If llOK
	With ThisForm
		.poDataMgr.Commit()
		=fGravarLog('C',ThisForm.Name,'INSERIR',;
					('Tabela('+.poDataMgr.pfSqlTabela(2).pcTabela+;
					 ') C.P.('+.poDataMgr.pfSqlTabela(2).pcChaveprimaria+')='+;
					 Alltrim(Transform(Evaluate(.poDataMgr.pfSqlTabela(2).pcNomecursor+'.'+.poDataMgr.pfSqlTabela(2).pcChaveprimaria)))),;
					 Iif(Type('m.usuar')=='C',m.usuar,''))
	EndWith
	NoDefault
Else
	ThisForm.poDataMgr.RollBack()
	Return 0
EndIf

Delete From crProcurar Where CPros = pPro

ThisForm.msv_Procurar
* Fim *********************************************************************************
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE msv_procurar
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE msv_procurar
Private pPro, pGru, pDes, pBar, pRff, pStI, pStF

pGru = Padr(ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntFiltros.getCgru.Value, 3)
pPro = Padr(ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.getCpro.Value, 14)
pDes = Padr(ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.getDpro.Value, 40)
pD2s = Padr(ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.getDpro2s.Value, 40)
pRff = Padr(ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.getRefs.Value, 15)
pFor = Padr(ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.Getifor.Value, 10)
pBar = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.getCbar.Value
pStI = Iif(ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntFiltros.optFilSituas.Value = 3, 2, 1)
pStF = Iif(ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntFiltros.optFilSituas.Value = 2, 1, 2)
pCnj = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.getconjunto.Value

If Used([crTmp])
	Use In CrTmp
EndIf

lcBus = Iif(Empty(pGru), [], [CGrus = ?pGru And ])

Do Case
	Case Not Empty(pPro)
		If ThisForm.Tipo2
			ThisForm.poDatamgr.CursorQuery([SigCdPrc], [crTmp], [CPros], pPro)
		Else
			ThisForm.poDatamgr.CursorQuery([SigCdPro], [crTmp], [CPros], pPro)
		EndIf
		ThisForm.BuscaPor = 1

	Case Not Empty(pDes)
		If ThisForm.Tipo2
			ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute([Select * From SigCdPrc Where ] + lcBus + [DPros = ?pDes], [crTmp])
		Else
			ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute([Select * From SigCdPro Where ] + lcBus + [DPros = ?pDes], [crTmp])
		EndIf
			
		If (Reccount([crTmp]) < 1)
			If MessageBox([Năo Foi Encontrada Uma Descriçăo Igual a Digitada!!! ] + Chr(13) + ;
						  [Deseja Procurar Parte da Descriçăo?], 4+32+256, [Procura])=6
				Wait Window [Aguarde!!! Procurando Produtos Iniciados Com a Descriçăo Informada...] NoWait
				pDes = [%] + Alltrim(pDes) + [%]
				If ThisForm.Tipo2
					ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute([Select * From SigCdPrc Where ] + lcBus + [Rtrim(DPros) Like ?pDes], [crTmp])
				Else
					ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute([Select * From SigCdPro Where ] + lcBus + [Rtrim(DPros) Like ?pDes], [crTmp])
				EndIf
				Wait Clear
			EndIf
		EndIf
		ThisForm.BuscaPor = 2

	Case Not Empty(pD2s)
		If ThisForm.Tipo2
			ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute([Select * From SigCdPrc Where ] + lcBus + [DPro2s = ?pD2s], [crTmp])
		Else
			ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute([Select * From SigCdPro Where ] + lcBus + [DPro2s = ?pD2s], [crTmp])
		EndIf
			
		If (Reccount([crTmp]) < 1)
			If MessageBox([Năo Foi Encontrado Um Descritivo Igual ao Digitado!!! ] + Chr(13) + ;
						  [Deseja Procurar Parte da Descriçăo?], 4+32+256, [Procura])=6
				Wait Window [Aguarde!!! Procurando Produtos Iniciados Com o Descritivo Informado...] NoWait
				pD2s = [%] + Alltrim(pD2s) + [%]
				If ThisForm.Tipo2
					ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute([Select * From SigCdPrc Where ] + lcBus + [Rtrim(DPro2s) Like ?pD2s], [crTmp])
				Else
					ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute([Select * From SigCdPro Where ] + lcBus + [Rtrim(DPro2s) Like ?pD2s], [crTmp])
				EndIf
				Wait Clear
			EndIf
		EndIf
		ThisForm.BuscaPor = 2

	Case Not Empty(pFor)
		If ThisForm.Tipo2
			ThisForm.poDatamgr.CursorQuery([SigCdPrc], [crTmp], [Ifors], pFor)
		Else
			ThisForm.poDatamgr.CursorQuery([SigCdPro], [crTmp], [Ifors], pFor)
		EndIf
		
		ThisForm.BuscaPor = 1

	Case Not Empty(pRff)
		If ThisForm.Tipo2
			ThisForm.poDatamgr.CursorQuery([SigCdPrc], [crTmp], [Reffs], pRff)
		Else
			ThisForm.poDatamgr.CursorQuery([SigCdPro], [crTmp], [Reffs], pRff)
		EndIf
		If (Reccount([crTmp]) < 1)
			If MessageBox([Năo Foi Encontrada Uma Referęncia Igual a Digitada!!! ] + Chr(13) + ;
						  [Deseja Procurar Parte da Referęncia?], 4+32+256, [Procura])=6
				Wait Window [Aguarde!!! Procurando Produtos Iniciados Com a Referęncia Informada...] NoWait

				pRff = [%] + Alltrim(pRff) + [%]
				If ThisForm.Tipo2
					ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute([Select * From SigCdPrc Where Rtrim(Reffs) Like ?pRff], [crTmp])
				Else
					ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute([Select * From SigCdPro Where Rtrim(Reffs) Like ?pRff], [crTmp])
				EndIf
				Wait Clear
			EndIf
		EndIf
		
		ThisForm.BuscaPor = 5

	Case Not Empty(pCnj) && Tiago - 08/02/2016 - Buscar por conjunto
		If ThisForm.Tipo2
			ThisForm.poDatamgr.CursorQuery([SigCdPrc], [crTmp], [Conjunts], pCnj)
		Else
			ThisForm.poDatamgr.CursorQuery([SigCdPro], [crTmp], [Conjunts], pCnj)
		EndIf
		
		ThisForm.BuscaPor = 1
		
	Case Not Empty(pBar)
		If ThisForm.Tipo2
			ThisForm.poDatamgr.CursorQuery([SigCdPrc], [crTmp], [CBars], pBar)
		Else
			ThisForm.poDatamgr.CursorQuery([SigCdPro], [crTmp], [CBars], pBar)
		EndIf
		ThisForm.BuscaPor = 1
EndCase

If Used([crTmp]) 
	Select CrTmp
	Scan
		If Not Seek(CrTmp.Cgrus,'crSigCdGrpFilter','CGrus')
			MessageBox('Usuario Sem Acesso ao Grupo de Produto '+CrTmp.Cgrus,0+16,'')
			Delete In CrTmp
		Endif
	EndScan
	
	Select * From CrTmp Into Cursor CrTmp2 ReadWrite
	
	If  (Reccount([crTmp2]) > 0)
		Select crTmp2
		If ThisForm.Tipo2
			Scan
				If Not Seek(CrTmp2.Cgrus,'crSigCdGrpFilter','CGrus')
					Loop
				Endif

				lcChv = crTmp2.cIdChaves
				If Not Seek(lcChv, [crProcurar], [cIdChaves])
					Scatter MemVar Memo
				 	Insert Into crProcurar From MemVar
				EndIf 
			EndScan
		Else
			Scan
				If Not Seek(crTmp2.Cgrus,'crSigCdGrpFilter','CGrus')
					Loop
				Endif
				lcChv = crTmp2.CPros
				If Not Seek(lcChv, [crProcurar], [CPros])
					Scatter MemVar Memo
				 	Insert Into crProcurar From MemVar
				EndIf 
			EndScan
		EndIf
		Go Top In crTmp2
		
		ThisForm.CodPros = crTmp2.CPros
		If ThisForm.Tipo2
			ThisForm.cIdChaves = crTmp2.cIdChaves
		EndIf
		Use In crTmp2
		ThisForm.Habilitacontroles(.t.)
	Endif
	Use In crTmp
EndIf 
* Fim ***********************************************************************
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE mativapagina1
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE mativapagina1
Private pPro, pGru, pDtI, pDtF, pDtA, pHrA, pUsA, pStI, pStF

Select crListaPro
pPro = Iif(Empty(crListaPro.CPros), Replicate(Chr(254), 14), crListaPro.CPros)
pGru = ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntFiltros.getCgru.Value
pDtI = fDtoSQL(ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntFiltros.getDtIni.Value)
pDtF = fDtoSQL(ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntFiltros.getDtFim.Value, '23:59:59')
pStI = Iif(ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntFiltros.optFilSituas.Value = 3, 2, 1)
pStF = Iif(ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntFiltros.optFilSituas.Value = 2, 1, 2)

If ThisForm.Tipo2
	pDtA = crListaPro.DataAlts
	pHrA = crListaPro.HoraAlts
	pUsA = crListaPro.UsuaAlts
EndIf

=DoDefault()

ThisForm.LockScreen = .t.

Select crListaPro
If ThisForm.Tipo2
	Index On CPros  + Dtos(DataAlts) + HoraAlts Tag CPros
	Index On DPros  + Dtos(DataAlts) + HoraAlts Tag DPros
	Index On DPro2s + Dtos(DataAlts) + HoraAlts Tag DPro2s
	Index On Dtos(DataAlts) + HoraAlts + CPros  Tag Reffs
	Index On UsuaAlts + Dtos(DataAlts) + HoraAlts + CPros Tag UsuaAlts
Else
	Index On CPros  Tag CPros
	Index On DPros  Tag DPros
	Index On DPro2s Tag DPro2s
	Index On Reffs  Tag Reffs
EndIf
Index On cIdChaves Tag cIdChaves
Set Order To CPros

If (Reccount('crProcurar') > 0)
	If ThisForm.Tipo2
		Select crProcurar
		Scan
			lcChv = crProcurar.cIdChaves
			If Not Seek(lcChv, 'crListaPro', 'cIdChaves')
				Scatter MemVar Memo
			 	Insert Into crListaPro From MemVar
			EndIf 
		EndScan
	Else
		Select crProcurar
		Scan
			lcChv = crProcurar.CPros
			If Not Seek(lcChv, 'crListaPro', 'CPros')
				Scatter MemVar Memo
			 	Insert Into crListaPro From MemVar
			EndIf 
		EndScan
	EndIf
EndIf
ThisForm.RetiraNulls

Select crListaPro
Set Near On
Seek ThisForm.CodPros
If ThisForm.Tipo2
	Scan While CPros = ThisForm.CodPros And cIdChaves <> ThisForm.cIdChaves
	EndScan
EndIf
Set Near Off

Do Case
	Case (ThisForm.BuscaPor = 1)
		Set Order To CPros In crListaPro
		With ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.Grade
			.Column1.Header1.BackColor = RGB(220,255,220)
			.Column2.Header1.BackColor = .Column4.Header1.BackColor
			.Column5.Header1.BackColor = .Column4.Header1.BackColor
			.Column6.Header1.BackColor = .Column4.Header1.BackColor
			.Refresh
		EndWith

	Case (ThisForm.BuscaPor = 2)
		Set Order To DPros In crListaPro
		With ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.Grade
			.Column1.Header1.BackColor = .Column4.Header1.BackColor
			.Column2.Header1.BackColor = RGB(220,255,220)
			.Column5.Header1.BackColor = .Column4.Header1.BackColor
			.Column6.Header1.BackColor = .Column4.Header1.BackColor
			.Refresh
		EndWith

	Otherwise
		Set Order To Reffs In crListaPro
		With ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.Grade
			.Column1.Header1.BackColor = .Column4.Header1.BackColor
			.Column2.Header1.BackColor = .Column4.Header1.BackColor
			.Column5.Header1.BackColor = RGB(220,255,220)
			.Column6.Header1.BackColor = .Column4.Header1.BackColor
			.Refresh
		EndWith
EndCase

With ThisForm.Pagina.Lista
	.lblProdutos.Caption = 'Produtos Selecionados : ' + Alltrim(Str(Reccount('crListaPro')))

	pGru = .cntFiltros.getCgru.Value
	If Empty(.cntFiltros.getCgru.Value) And Not Empty(crListaPro.CGrus)
		pGru = crListaPro.CGrus
		.cntFiltros.getCgru.Value  = crSigCdGrp.CGrus
		.cntFiltros.getDGru.Value  = crSigCdGrp.DGrus
		.cntFiltros.getCgru.Refresh
		.cntFiltros.getDGru.Refresh
		.cntFiltros.getDtIni.Refresh
		.cntFiltros.getDtFim.Refresh
	EndIf

	ThisForm.poDataMgr.Requery('crSigCdGrp')
	Go Top In crSigCdGrp
	ThisForm.OrdGrade = Int(Val(Substr(crSigCdGrp.CfgGerGprs, 6, 1)))

	If Not ThisForm.Primeira
		lcCol = Padr(ThisForm.BuscaPor, 1)
		.Grade.SetFocus
		.Grade.Column&lcCol..SetFocus
		.Grade.Refresh
	Endif
EndWith

ThisForm.LockScreen = .f.
* Fim **************************************************************************************
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Init
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Init
LParameters prCon, prPro, prTp2, lcNomeFrm1, prFil, prEca, pIns, pGpr, pFor, pAcot

Private pPro, pGru, pSgr, pDtI, pDtF, pDtA, pHrA, pUsA, pIds, pStI, pStF
Local loTree1
PUBLIC aCot
DIMENSION aCot(5,2)

lcNomeFrm1 = Iif(Type('lcNomeFrm1')=='C' And Not Empty(lcNomeFrm1),lcNomeFrm1,ThisForm.Name)
ThisForm.Name = lcNomeFrm1

ThisForm.ConGP = (Type('prCon')<>'L') && A Consulta Genérica de Produtos Chama o Cadastro de 
									  && Produtos Passando o 1ş Parâmetro "CONGP" = Caracter

ThisForm.PConG = prPro				  && A Consulta Genérica de Produtos Chama o Cadastro de 
									  && Produtos Passando o 2ş Parâmetro Com o Cód. Produto

ThisForm.Tipo2 = prTp2  			  && O Parametro é Passado Para Informar Qual o Tipo que
								      && Será Utilizado : .f.- Cadastro de Produtos (SigCdPro)
								      &&                  .t.- Consulta Históricos (SigCdPrc)
ThisForm.prEca = prEca

aCot = pAcot						  && mena - 02/08/2017

ThisForm.OrdGrade = 1

If ThisForm.ConGP
	ThisForm.WindowType = 1
	ThisForm.AlwaysOnTop = .t.
EndIf

ThisForm.Parametrizado = pIns
ThisForm.RetCodProduto = []
If ThisForm.Parametrizado
	ThisForm.WindowType = 1
	If Not Empty(pGpr)
		ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntFiltros.getCgru.Value = pGpr
		ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntFiltros.getDtIni.Value = Ctod([01/01/1900])
		ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntFiltros.getDtFim.Value = Ctod([31/12/2900])
		ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntFiltros.getCgru.Refresh
		ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntFiltros.getDtIni.Refresh
		ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntFiltros.getDtFim.Refresh
	EndIf
EndIf

ThisForm.Pesagem = Iif(Type('PrCon')<>'L' and PrCon = 'PESAGEM',.t.,.f.)
ThisForm.VeioDoGridCompo = .f.
ThisForm.Tpcalcp = 0
ThisForm.CodigoTipo6 = .f.
ThisForm.Situas = 0
ThisForm.Composiciona = []
ThisForm.TemTipos = .f.
ThisForm.TempTipos = .f.
ThisForm.PrimeiraCus = .t.
ThisForm.PrimeiraCom = .t.
ThisForm.FilStatus = Iif(Type([prFil])=[L], prFil, .f.)

If ThisForm.Pesagem
	ThisForm.AlwaysOnTop = .t.
	ThisForm.WindowType = 1
EndIf

pPro = Iif(ThisForm.ConGP Or ThisForm.Parametrizado, ThisForm.PConG, Replicate(Chr(254), 14))
pGru = Replicate(Chr(254), 03)
pSGr = Replicate(Chr(254), 06)
pDtI = fDtoSQL(Date() - 30)
pDtF = fDtoSQL(Date(), [23:59:59])
pDtA = fDtoSQL(Date())
pHrA = Replicate(Chr(254), 06)
pUsA = Replicate(Chr(254), 10)
pIds = Replicate(Chr(254), 20)
pStI = 1
pStF = 2

If ThisForm.Parametrizado And Not Empty(pGpr)
	pGru = pGpr
EndIf 

With ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntFiltros
	.getDtIni.Value = Date()
	.getDtFim.Value = Date()
EndWith 

ThisForm.BuscaPor       = 1
ThisForm.CodPros        = Replicate(Chr(254),14)
ThisForm.cIdChaves      = Replicate(Chr(254),20)
ThisForm.AntCpros	    = ''
ThisForm.plIniProcesso  = .t.
ThisForm.AlterouCompo   = .f.
ThisForm.VeiodoGrid     = .f.
ThisForm.JaGravou       = .f.
ThisForm.TopMensa       = ThisForm.Pagina.Top + ThisForm.Pagina.Height
ThisForm.Copiando	    = .f.
ThisForm.Primeira       = .t.
ThisForm.poObjExt1      = Null
ThisForm.TamIdent       = 10
ThisForm.AcessoDesigner = fChecaAcesso([SIGCDPRO], [DESIGNER]) 



If ThisForm.Tipo2
	ThisForm.Caption = 'Alteraçőes de Produtos'

	lcLstPro = [Select CPros, DPros, DPro2s, CGrus, SGrus, Reffs, Colecoes, ImpEtiqs, Situas, Compos, ] + ;
					  [Encoms, CBars, CproEqs, PVens, DataAlts, HoraAlts, UsuaAlts, cIdChaves ] + ;
				 [From SigCdPrc ] + ;
				[Where DataAlts BetWeen ?pDtI And ?pDtF And ] + ;
					  [CGrus = ?pGru And ] + ;
					  [Situas In (?pStI, ?pStF)]

	lcQryPro = [Select * From SigCdPrc Where cIdChaves = ?pIds]
	lcQryCompo = 'Select *, 0 as TpCalcCus, Space(20) as Tipos, 0 as Bloqueio, 0 as chkInstalas From SigPrCp2 Where CPros = ?pPro And DataAlts = ?pDtA And HoraAlts = ?pHrA And UsuaAlts = ?pUsA'
	lcQrySubCp = 'Select *, 0 as TpCalcCus, Space(20) as Tipos, 0 as Bloqueio From SigSubC2 Where CPros = ?pPro And DataAlts = ?pDtA And HoraAlts = ?pHrA And UsuaAlts = ?pUsA'
	lcQryModP  = 'Select * From SigPrMdc Where CPros = ?pPro And DataAlts = ?pDtA And HoraAlts = ?pHrA And UsuaAlts = ?pUsA'
	lcQryProF  = 'Select a.*,b.Descrs From SigCdPfc a Inner Join SigCdGcr b On a.Grupos = b.Codigos Where Produtos = ?pPro And DataAlts = ?pDtA And HoraAlts = ?pHrA And UsuaAlts = ?pUsA'
	lcQryMtz   = 'Select a.*, b.Locals From SigPrMt2 a Inner Join SigCdPro b On a.CMats = b.CPros Where a.CPros = ?pPro And a.DataAlts = ?pDtA And a.HoraAlts = ?pHrA And a.UsuaAlts = ?pUsA'
Else
	ThisForm.Caption = [Cadastro de Produtos]

	If ThisForm.ConGP Or ThisForm.Parametrizado
		lcQryPro = [Select *, Space(20) as cIdChaves From SigCdPro Where CPros = ?pPro]
		lcLstPro = lcQryPro
	Else
		If ThisForm.FilStatus && Filtro Por Status
			lcLstPro = [Select a.CPros, a.DPros, a.DPro2s, a.CGrus, a.SGrus, a.Reffs, a.Colecoes, a.ImpEtiqs, ] + ;
							  [a.Situas, a.Encoms, a.CBars, a.CproEqs, Space(20) as cIdChaves, a.compos ] + ;
						 [From SigCdPro a, SigCdPst b ] + ;
						[Where a.Status = b.Cods And ] + ;
							  [b.Tipos = 3 And ] + ;
					  		  [a.Situas In (?pStI, ?pStF)]
		Else
			lcLstPro = [Select CPros, DPros, DPro2s, CGrus, SGrus, Reffs, Colecoes, ImpEtiqs, Situas, ] + ;
							  [Encoms, CBars, CproEqs, Space(20) as cIdChaves, compos ] + ;
						 [From SigCdPro ] + ;
						[Where Datas BetWeen ?pDtI And ?pDtF And ] + ;
							  [CGrus = ?pGru And ] + ;
					  		  [Situas In (?pStI, ?pStF)]
		EndIf
		
		lcQryPro = [Select *, Space(20) as cIdChaves ] + ;
					 [From SigCdPro ] + ;
					[Where CPros = ?pPro]
	EndIf
	lcQryCompo = 'Select *, 0 as TpCalcCus, 0 as Bloqueio, 0 as chkInstalas From SigPrCpo Where CPros = ?pPro Order by OrdTs'
	lcQrySubCp = 'Select *, 0 as TpCalcCus, 0 as Bloqueio From SigSubCp Where CPros = ?pPro Order by OrdTs'	
	lcQryModP  = 'Select * From SigPrMdl  Where CPros = ?pPro'
	lcQryProF  = 'Select a.*,b.Descrs, a.Grupos+Str(a.Ordems,2) as GrpOrdem From SigCdPrf a Inner Join SigCdGcr b On a.Grupos = b.Codigos Where Produtos = ?pPro'
	lcQryMtz   = 'Select a.*, b.Locals From SigPrMtz a Inner Join SigCdPro b On a.CMats = b.CPros Where a.CPros = ?pPro'
EndIf

lcQryPro2  = 'Select * From SigCdPrc Where CPros = ?pPro'
lcQryComp2 = 'Select * From SigPrCp2 Where CPros = ?pPro And DataAlts = ?pDtA And HoraAlts = ?pHrA And UsuaAlts = ?pUsA'
lcQrySubC2 = 'Select * From SigSubC2 Where CPros = ?pPro And DataAlts = ?pDtA And HoraAlts = ?pHrA And UsuaAlts = ?pUsA'
lcQryModP2 = 'Select * From SigPrMdc Where CPros = ?pPro And DataAlts = ?pDtA And HoraAlts = ?pHrA And UsuaAlts = ?pUsA'
lcQryProF2 = 'Select * From SigCdPfc Where Produtos = ?pPro And DataAlts = ?pDtA And HoraAlts = ?pHrA And UsuaAlts = ?pUsA'
lcQryMtz2  = 'Select * From SigPrMt2 Where CPros = ?pPro And DataAlts = ?pDtA And HoraAlts = ?pHrA And UsuaAlts = ?pUsA'
lcQryProMI = 'Select * From SigPrPmi Where CPros = ?pPro'
lcQryPrEmp = 'Select * From SigCdMin Where CPros = ?pPro'
lcQryGru   = 'Select * From SigCdGrp Where CGrus = ?pGru'
lcQrySGru  = 'Select * From SigCdPsg Where CGrus = ?pGru And Codigos = ?pSGr'
lcQryCrPro = 'Select * From SigPrCrr Where CPros = ?pPro'
lcQryProFT = 'Select * From SigCdPft Where CPros = ?pPro'
lcQryFPro  = 'Select a.*, b.rClis From SigPrFnc a Inner Join SigCdCli b on b.iClis = a.IFors Where cPros = ?pPro'
lcQryGccr  = 'Select * From SigCdGcr'
lcQryParam = 'Select * From SigCdPam'
lcQryMTal  = 'Select * From SigCdMtl'
lcQryPFtp  = 'Select * From SigPrFtp'
lcQryProTp = 'Select * from SigProTp Where Cpros = ?pPro'
lcQryCmv = 'Select * from SigCdCmv where Cpros = ?pPro'
lcQryPrTam = [Select a.*, b.Descs from SigPrTam a Inner Join SigCdTam b On a.CodTams = b.Cods where a.Cpros = ?pPro]
lcQryPrCar = [Select a.*, b.Descrs from SigPrCar a Inner Join SigCrRap b On a.Codigos = b.Codigos Where a.CPros = ?pPro]
lcQryPrTa2 = [Select a.*, b.Descs from SigPrTa2 a Inner Join SigCdTam b On a.CodTams = b.Cods where a.Cpros = ?pPro And a.DataAlts = ?pDtA And a.HoraAlts = ?pHrA And a.UsuaAlts = ?pUsA]
lcQryPrCa2 = [Select a.*, b.Descrs from SigPrCa2 a Inner Join SigCrRap b On a.Codigos = b.Codigos Where a.CPros = ?pPro And a.DataAlts = ?pDtA And a.HoraAlts = ?pHrA And a.UsuaAlts = ?pUsA]
lcQryPrTar = [Select * From SigPrTar Where CPros = ?pPro]
lcQryPrArq = [Select * From SigPrArq Where CPros = ?pPro]

With ThisForm
	.poDataMgr  = CreateObject('fSqlConector', ThisForm.Name)

	If ThisForm.Parametrizado
		ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery([SigCdGrp], [LocalGru], [CGrus], pGpr, [CGrus])
		If Not Used([LocalGru])
			=MessageBox([Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!], 16, [Falha na Conexăo (CursorQuery - LocalGru)])
			Return .f.
		EndIf
		Select LocalGru
		Go Top In LocalGru
		If Eof([LocalGru])
			=MessageBox([O Grupo Passado Como Parâmetro é Inválido!!!], 0+16, [Grupo: ] + pGrp)
			Return .f.
		EndIf
	EndIf

	With .poDataMgr
		If ThisForm.Tipo2
			.AddCursor('SigCdPrc', 'cIdChaves', 'crListaPro', '', ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.Grade, lcLstPro, .t.)
			.AddCursor('SigCdPrc', 'cIdChaves', 'crSigCdPro', '', '', lcQryPro)
			.AddCursor('SigPrCp2', 'cIdChaves', 'crSigPrCpo', '', '', lcQryCompo)
			.AddCursor('SigSubC2', 'cIdChaves', 'crSigSubCp', '', '', lcQrySubCp)
			.AddCursor('SigPrMdc', 'cIdChaves', 'crSigPrMdl', '', '', lcQryModP)
			.AddCursor('SigCdPfc', 'cIdChaves', 'crSigCdPrf', '', '', lcQryProF)
			.AddCursor('SigPrMt2', 'cIdChaves', 'crSigPrMtz', '', '', lcQryMtz)
		Else
			.AddCursor('SigCdPro', 'CPros',     'crListaPro', '', ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.Grade, lcLstPro, .t.)
			.AddCursor('SigCdPro', 'CPros',     'crSigCdPro', '', '', lcQryPro)
			.AddCursor('SigPrCpo', 'cIdChaves', 'crSigPrCpo', '', '', lcQryCompo)
			.AddCursor('SigSubCp', 'cIdChaves', 'crSigSubCp', '', '', lcQrySubCp)
			.AddCursor('SigPrMdl', 'CPros',     'crSigPrMdl', '', '', lcQryModP)
			.AddCursor('SigCdPrf', 'cIdChaves', 'crSigCdPrf', '', '', lcQryProF)
			.AddCursor('SigPrMtz', 'cIdChaves', 'crSigPrMtz', '', '', lcQryMtz)
		EndIf

		.AddCursor('SigCdPrc', 'cIdChaves', 'crSigCdPrc', '', '', lcQryPro2)
		.AddCursor('SigPrCp2', 'cIdChaves', 'crSigPrCp2', '', '', lcQryComp2)
		.AddCursor('SigSubC2', 'cIdChaves', 'crSigSubC2', '', '', lcQrySubc2)		
		.AddCursor('SigPrMdc', 'cIdChaves', 'crSigPrMdc', '', '', lcQryModP2)
		.AddCursor('SigCdPfc', 'cIdChaves', 'crSigCdPfc', '', '', lcQryProF2)
		.AddCursor('SigPrMt2', 'cIdChaves', 'crSigPrMt2', '', '', lcQryMtz2)
		.AddCursor('SigPrPmi', 'cIdChaves', 'crSigPrPmi', '', '', lcQryProMi)
		.AddCursor('SigCdMin', 'cIdChaves', 'crSigCdMin', '', '', lcQryPrEmp)
		.AddCursor('SigCdGrp', 'CGrus',     'crSigCdGrp', '', '', lcQryGru)
		.AddCursor('SigCdPsg', 'cIdChaves', 'crSigCdPsg', '', '', lcQrySGru)
		.AddCursor('SigPrCrr', 'cIdChaves', 'crSigPrCrr', '', '', lcQryCrPro)
		.AddCursor('SigCdPft', 'ProCarTits','crSigCdPft', '', '', lcQryProFT)
		.AddCursor('SigPrFnc', 'cIdChaves', 'crSigPrFnc', '', '', lcQryFPro)
		.AddCursor('SigCdSvc', 'cIdChaves', 'CrSigCdSvc', '', '')
		.AddCursor('SigCdCat', 'cIdChaves', 'CrSigCdCat', '', '')
		.AddCursor('SigProTp', 'pkchaves',  'crSigProTp',  '', '', lcQryProTp)	
		.AddCursor('SigCdCmv', 'pkchaves',  'crSigCdCmv',  '', '', lcQryCmv)
		.AddCursor('SigPrTam', 'cidchaves', 'crSigPrTam',  '', '', lcQryPrTam)
		.AddCursor('SigPrCar', 'pkChaves',  'crSigPrCar',  '', '', lcQryPrCar)
		.AddCursor('SigPrTa2', 'cidchaves', 'crSigPrTa2',  '', '', lcQryPrTa2)
		.AddCursor('SigPrCa2', 'pkChaves',  'crSigPrCa2',  '', '', lcQryPrCa2)
		.AddCursor('SigPrTar', 'pkChaves',  'crSigPrTar',  '', '', lcQryPrTar)
		.AddCursor('SigPrArq', 'pkChaves',  'crSigPrArq',  '', '', lcQryPrArq)
		
		* Cursores Carregados Totalmente (Tabela Pequena)
		.AddCursor('SigCdGcr', 'cIdChaves', 'crSigCdGcr', '', '', lcQryGccr)
		.AddCursor('SigCdPam', 'GesInd',    'crSigCdPam', '', '', lcQryParam)
		.AddCursor('SigCdPac', 'cIdChaves', 'crSigCdPac')
		.AddCursor('SigCdMtl', 'cIdChaves', 'crSigCdMtl', '', '', lcQryMTal)
		.AddCursor('SigPrFtp', 'CPros',     'crSigPrFtp', '', '', lcQryPFtp)
		
		* Trazendo os Dados Das Tabelas Pequenas
		If ThisForm.ConGP Or ThisForm.Parametrizado
			.Requery('crListaPro')
			Go Top In crListaPro
			
			With ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntFiltros
				.getCgru.Value  = crListaPro.CGrus
				.getDtIni.Value = crListaPro.Datas
				.getDtFim.Value = crListaPro.Datas

				.getCgru.Visible  = .f.
				.getDgru.Visible  = .f.
				.getDtIni.Visible = .f.
				.getDtFim.Visible = .f.
				.lblGrupo.Visible = .f.
				.lblData1.Visible = .f.
				.lblData2.Visible = .f.
			EndWith
		EndIf
		.Requery('crSigCdGcr')
		.Requery('crSigCdPam')
		.Requery('crSigCdPac')
		.Requery('crSigCdMtl')
	EndWith
EndWith

lcQuery = [select cgrus,codigos, cgrucods  from sigcdpsg]
If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, [crSubGrupo]) < 1)
	=MessageBox([Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!], 16, [Falha na Conexăo (crSubGrupo)])
	Return .f.
EndIf
Select crSubGrupo
Index On CGrus Tag CGrus
Index On Codigos Tag SGrus Additive 
Index On cgrucods Tag cgrucods Additive 

lcQuery = [Select a.Tipos, a.Custos, b.CGrus ] + ;
		    [From SigCdTpc a, SigCdCom b ] + ;
		   [Where a.Tipos = b.Tipos]

If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, [crSigCdCom]) < 1)
	=MessageBox([Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!], 16, [Falha na Conexăo (crSigCdCom)])
	Return .f.
EndIf
Select crSigCdCom
Index On Tipos + CGrus Tag Tipos

lcQuery = [Select a.Cods, a.Descs, b.CGrus ] + ;
			[From SigCdCls a ] + ;
			[Left Join SigCdCla b On a.Cods = b.Cods]

If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, [crSigCdCls]) < 1)
	=MessageBox([Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!], 16, [Falha na Conexăo (crSigCdCls)])
	Return .f.
EndIf
Select crSigCdCls
Index On Cods + CGrus Tag Cods
Update crSigCdCls Set CGrus = [] Where IsNull(CGrus )
Go Top In crSigCdCls

lcQuery = [Select * From SigCdPrd]
If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, [crSigCdPrd]) < 1)
	=MessageBox([Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!], 16, [Falha na Conexăo (crSigCdPrd)])
	Return .f.
EndIf
Select crSigCdPrd
Index On CGrus + Str(TpMontas, 2) + Str(COrds, 2) Tag CGrus
Go Top In crSigCdPrd

lcQuery = [Select Tipos ] + ;
		    [From SigCdTpc ] + ;
		   [Where Custos = 2]

If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, [crSigCdTpc]) < 1)
	=MessageBox([Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!], 16, [Falha na Conexăo (crSigCdTpc)])
	Return .f.
EndIf
Select crSigCdTpc
Index On Tipos Tag Tipos

lcSql = [Select Count(1) as Qt From SigCdUni WherE cEstos = '3' ]
If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcSql, 'CstmpUni') < 1)
	=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (Init - CsTmpUni)')
	Return 0
EndIf
Go Top in CsTmpUni
ThisForm.Habilitapeso = CsTmpUni.Qt > 0

Goto Top In crSigCdPam

lcSql = [Select * From SigCdPac]
If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcSql, 'CrSigCdPac') < 1)
	=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (CrSigCdPac)')
	Return 0
EndIf
Go Top in CrSigCdPac

lcQuery = [Select * From SigCdCat]
If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, [CsProCat]) < 1)
	=MessageBox([Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!], 16, [Falha na Conexăo (CsProCat)])
	Return .f.

Index On Cods Tag Cods

lcQuery = [Select * From SigCdSvc ]
If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, [CsProSer]) < 1)
	=MessageBox([Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!], 16, [Falha na Conexăo (CsProSer)])

Select crSigCdGcr
Index On Codigos Tag Codigos

* Seleciona Matérias-Primas **************************************************************
* Se o Grupo do Produto da Composiçăo For Secundário: Permitir Somente os Produtos Que
* Tenham o Campo "Montagem" (SigCdPro.MontaDescs) Preenchido
lStrQuery = [Select Distinct a.CPros, a.DPros, a.Locals, a.CGrus, a.MontaDescs, b.MtPrimas, Space(20) as Tipos, 1 as Custos, b.CfgGerGprs, a.Situas, a.Reffs ] + ;
			  [From SigCdPro a, SigCdGrp b ] + ;
			 [Where a.CGrus = b.CGrus And ] + ;
				   [Not b.MtPrimas = 3 ] + ;
			 [Order By a.CPros]
If ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lStrQuery,'CrMtPrimaC') < 1
	MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo !!!',16,'Falha na Conexăo (CrMtPrimaC)')
	Return(.F.)
EndIf

Select * From CrMtPrimaC Where MtPrimas = 4 Into Cursor crMatrizes ReadWrite
Select crMatrizes
Index On DPros Tag DPros
Index On CPros Tag CPros
Go Top In crMatrizes

Select * From CrMtPrimaC Where MtPrimas In (1, 2) And Iif(Int(Val(Substr(CfgGerGprs, 38, 1))) = 1,Situas = 1,.t.) Into Cursor crMtPrima ReadWrite
Select CrMtPrima
Index On DPros Tag DPros
Index On CPros Tag CPros
Index On Reffs Tag Reffs
Go Top In CrMtPrima

*** Tiago - 26/01/2016 - Rosana Joias - Criado cursor com a relaçăo de conjuntos criados
lcQuery = [Select Distinct a.Conjunts From SigCdPro a Inner Join SigCdGrp b On a.CGrus = b.CGrus Where b.MtPrimas = 3 And a.Conjunts <> '' Order By a.Conjunts]
If ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery,'CrConjunto') < 1
	MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo !!!',16,'Falha na Conexăo (CrConjunto)')
	Return(.F.)
Endif
Select crConjunto
Index on Conjunts Tag Conjunts

lStrQuery = [Select Tipos From SigCdCom]			  
If ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lStrQuery,'LocalCdCom') < 1
	MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo !!!',16,'Falha na Conexăo (LocalCdCom)')
	Return(.F.)
EndIf
Go Top In LocalCdCom
If Eof([LocalCdCom])
	Select * From CrMtPrima Into Cursor CrMtPrimaT ReadWrite
	Index On DPros Tag DPros
	Index On CPros Tag CPros
	Go Top In CrMtPrimaT
Else
	ThisForm.TemTipos = .t.
	ThisForm.TempTipos = .t.

	lStrQuery = [Select Distinct a.CPros, a.DPros, a.CGrus, a.MontaDescs, b.MtPrimas, c.Tipos, d.Custos, a.Reffs ] + ;
				  [From SigCdPro a, SigCdGrp b, SigCdCom c, SigCdTpc d ] + ;
				 [Where a.CGrus = b.CGrus And ] + ;
					   [(b.MtPrimas In (1, 2) Or d.UsarPAs = 1) And ] + ;
					   [b.CGrus = c.CGrus And ] + ;
					   [c.Tipos = d.Tipos ] + ;
				 [Order By a.CPros]

	If ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lStrQuery,'CrMtPrimaT') < 1
		MessageBox('Favor reinicializar o processo !!!',16,'Falha na Conexăo (CrMtPrimaT)')
		Return(.F.)
	EndIf
	Select CrMtPrimaT
	Index On DPros Tag DPros
	Index On CPros Tag CPros
	Index On Reffs Tag Reffs
	Go Top In CrMtPrimaT
EndIf

* Apanhando os Grupos Que o Usuário Tem Acesso *******************************************
lcQuery = [Select CGrus, DGrus, Mercs, Margems, 'S' as Apagar From SigCdGrp]
If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'crSigCdGrpFilter') < 1)
	=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (crSigCdGrpFilter)')
	Return 0
EndIf
Select crSigCdGrpFilter
Index On CGrus Tag CGrus
Index On DGrus Tag DGrus
Index On Mercs Tag Mercs

lcGru = fAcessoProduto('', Usuar, .f., .f., ThisForm.poDataMgr)

If Not Empty(Alltrim(lcGru))
	lnBus = 1
	lcBus = Substr(lcGru, lnBus, 3)
	Do While Not Empty(lcBus)
		lcBus = Substr(lcGru, lnBus, 3)
		lnBus = lnBus + 3
		If Not Empty(lcBus) And Seek(lcBus, 'crSigCdGrpFilter', 'CGrus')
			Replace Apagar With 'N' In crSigCdGrpFilter
		EndIf
	EndDo
EndIf
Delete From crSigCdGrpFilter Where Apagar = 'S'

EndScan
