================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGCDPRO.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.Get_Class
* Classe: fwget (Base: textbox)
* Registro: 131
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE When
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE When
DoDefault()

pGru = Padr(ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntFiltros.getCgru.Value, 3)

If Not Empty(pGru)
	ThisForm.poDataMgr.Requery('crSigCdGrp')
	Go Top In crSigCdGrp
	ThisForm.OrdGrade = Int(Val(Substr(crSigCdGrp.CfgGerGprs, 6, 1)))
	lnCPro = Iif(Empty(crSigCdGrp.CodProds), crSigCdPam.CodProds, crSigCdGrp.CodProds)
Else
	lnCPro = crSigCdPam.CodProds
EndIf
If (lnCPro=9) And (ThisForm.pcEscolha = 'ALTERAR')
	Return .f.
EndIf
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Valid
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Valid
Local loLista

If Not Empty(This.Value)
	Select * ;
	  From crSigCdCls ;
	 Where CGrus In (crSigCdPro.CGrus, Space(3)) ;
	 Order By Cods ;
	  Into Cursor LocalClas ReadWrite
	Select LocalClas
	Index On Cods Tag Cods	  

	Select LocalClas
	Go Top In LocalClas
	Locate For Cods = Padr(This.Value, 3)
	If Eof([LocalClas])
		loLista = CreateObject([fwBuscaInt], [LocalClas], [Cods], This.Value, [Classificaçăo], .t.)
		loLista.mAddColuna([Cods],  [], [Cód], 	     .t.)
		loLista.mAddColuna([Descs], [], [Descriçăo], .t.)
		loLista.Show()
	EndIf
	If (Lastkey() <> 27)
		This.Value = LocalClas.Cods
		ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.PgframeDados.PgDados.get_DClass.Value = LocalClas.Descs
	Else
		This.Value = []
		ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.PgframeDados.PgDados.get_DClass.Value = []
	EndIf	
	Use In LocalClas
EndIf

*** Tiago
pGru = Padr(ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntFiltros.getCgru.Value, 3)
If Not Empty(pGru)
	ThisForm.poDataMgr.Requery('crSigCdGrp')
	Go Top In crSigCdGrp
	ThisForm.OrdGrade = Int(Val(Substr(crSigCdGrp.CfgGerGprs, 6, 1)))
	lnCPro = Iif(Empty(crSigCdGrp.CodProds), crSigCdPam.CodProds, crSigCdGrp.CodProds)
Else
	lnCPro = crSigCdPam.CodProds
EndIf
If lnCPro = 9 and (ThisForm.pcEscolha = "INSERIR")
	lcsgru = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.PgFrameDados.pgDados.getcsGru.Value
	lcide = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.PgFrameDados.pgDados.getIdeCPros.Value
	lccla = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.PgFrameDados.pgDados.get_Class.Value
	lcfina = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.getCodFinP.Value
	coldprod = pGru + Alltrim(lcsgru) + Alltrim(This.peAntValue) + Alltrim(lcide) + Alltrim(lcfina)
	cnewprod = pGru + Alltrim(lcsgru) + Alltrim(lccla) + Alltrim(lcide) + Alltrim(lcfina)
	
	If !(coldprod == cnewprod)  and !Empty(coldprod)
		_Codigo = Val(Right(Alltrim(crSigCdPro.CPros),4))
		=fCanUniqueKey(_Codigo, "PRODUTO" + coldprod)
	EndIf
	If !(coldprod == cnewprod) or Empty(CrSigCdPro.cpros)	
		lnserial = Transf(fGerUniqueKey("PRODUTO" + cnewprod), "@L 9999")
		cnewprod = cnewprod + lnserial
		replace cpros with cnewprod in CrSigCdPro
		ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgDados.GetCpro.Refresh()		
	EndIf
EndIf

This.Refresh
* Fim **************************************************************************************
ENDPROC

* PROCEDURE When

PROCEDURE When
llret = DoDefault()

pGru = Padr(ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntFiltros.getCgru.Value, 3)

If Not Empty(pGru)
	ThisForm.poDataMgr.Requery('crSigCdGrp')
	Go Top In crSigCdGrp
	ThisForm.OrdGrade = Int(Val(Substr(crSigCdGrp.CfgGerGprs, 6, 1)))
	lnCPro = Iif(Empty(crSigCdGrp.CodProds), crSigCdPam.CodProds, crSigCdGrp.CodProds)
Else
	lnCPro = crSigCdPam.CodProds

If (lnCPro=9) And (ThisForm.pcEscolha = 'ALTERAR')
	llRet = .f.

Return llRet

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Valid

PROCEDURE Valid
*** Tiago
pGru = Padr(ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntFiltros.getCgru.Value, 3)
If Not Empty(pGru)
	ThisForm.poDataMgr.Requery('crSigCdGrp')
	Go Top In crSigCdGrp
	ThisForm.OrdGrade = Int(Val(Substr(crSigCdGrp.CfgGerGprs, 6, 1)))
	lnCPro = Iif(Empty(crSigCdGrp.CodProds), crSigCdPam.CodProds, crSigCdGrp.CodProds)
Else
	lnCPro = crSigCdPam.CodProds
ENDIF

If lnCPro = 9 and (ThisForm.pcEscolha = "INSERIR")
	lcsgru = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.PgFrameDados.pgDados.getcsGru.Value
	lcide = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.PgFrameDados.pgDados.getIdeCPros.Value
	lccla = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.PgFrameDados.pgDados.get_Class.Value
	lcfina = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.getCodFinP.Value
*!*		coldprod = pGru + Alltrim(lcsgru) + Alltrim(lccla) + Alltrim(This.peAntValue) + Alltrim(lcfina) && mena 11/2012 This.peAntValue esta com .F. na INCLUSAO 
	coldprod = pGru + Alltrim(lcsgru) + Alltrim(lccla) + IIF(VARTYPE(This.peAntValue) = 'L', '', Alltrim(This.peAntValue)) + Alltrim(lcfina)
	cnewprod = pGru + Alltrim(lcsgru) + Alltrim(lccla) + Alltrim(lcide) + + Alltrim(lcfina)
	
	If !(coldprod == cnewprod)  and !Empty(coldprod)
		_Codigo = Val(Right(Alltrim(crSigCdPro.CPros),4))
		=fCanUniqueKey(_Codigo, "PRODUTO" + coldprod)
	EndIf
	If !(coldprod == cnewprod) or Empty(CrSigCdPro.cpros)	
		lnserial = Transf(fGerUniqueKey("PRODUTO" + cnewprod), "@L 9999")
		cnewprod = cnewprod + lnserial
		replace cpros with cnewprod in CrSigCdPro
		ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgDados.GetCpro.Refresh()		
	EndIf
EndIf

ENDPROC


================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGCDPRO.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.Bot_Fornecedor
* Classe: commandgroup (Base: commandgroup)
* Registro: 136
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Bot_Fornecedor.Valid
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Bot_Fornecedor.Valid
ThisForm.ProcForn = .F.
If Type('ThisForm.Produto') <> 'C' or ( ThisForm.Produto <> crSigCdPro.cPros ) Then
	ThisForm.Produto = crSigCdPro.cPros
	ThisForm.Procforn = .T.
Endif

Do Form SigCdFop With Thisform, ThisForm.DataSessionId, ThisForm.pcEscolha
* Fim *********************************************************************************

ENDPROC

================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGCDPRO.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.getCodFinP
* Classe: fwget (Base: textbox)
* Registro: 146
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Valid
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Valid
Local loLista

If Not Empty(This.Value)
	loLista = CreateObject([fwBuscaExt], ThisForm.poDataMgr.pnIdConn, [SigCdFip], ;
						   [crListaRemota], [Cods], This.Value, [Seleçăo], .t.)

	If Not loLista.plAchouRegistro
		loLista.mAddColuna([Cods],  [], [Código])
		loLista.mAddColuna([Descs], [], [Descriçăo])
		loLista.Show()
	EndIf
	
	If (Lastkey() <> 27)
		ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.getCodFinP.Value = crListaRemota.Cods
		ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.getDesFinP.Value = crListaRemota.Descs
	Else
		ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.getCodFinP.Value = []
		ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.getDesFinP.Value = []
	EndIf
	Use In crListaRemota
Else
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.getDesFinP.Value = []
EndIf
ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.getCodFinP.Refresh 
ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.getDesFinP.Refresh 

*** Tiago
pGru = Padr(ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.cntFiltros.getCgru.Value, 3)
If Not Empty(pGru)
	ThisForm.poDataMgr.Requery('crSigCdGrp')
	Go Top In crSigCdGrp
	ThisForm.OrdGrade = Int(Val(Substr(crSigCdGrp.CfgGerGprs, 6, 1)))
	lnCPro = Iif(Empty(crSigCdGrp.CodProds), crSigCdPam.CodProds, crSigCdGrp.CodProds)
Else
	lnCPro = crSigCdPam.CodProds
EndIf
If lnCPro = 9 and (ThisForm.pcEscolha = "INSERIR")
	lcsgru = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.PgFrameDados.pgDados.getcsGru.Value
	lcide = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.PgFrameDados.pgDados.getIdeCPros.Value
	lccla = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.PgFrameDados.pgDados.get_Class.Value
	lcfina = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.getCodFinP.Value
	coldprod = pGru + Alltrim(lcsgru) + Alltrim(lccla) + Alltrim(lcide) + Alltrim(This.peAntValue)
	cnewprod = pGru + Alltrim(lcsgru) + Alltrim(lccla) + Alltrim(lcide) + + Alltrim(lcfina)
	
	If !(coldprod == cnewprod)  and !Empty(coldprod)
		_Codigo = Val(Right(Alltrim(crSigCdPro.CPros),4))
		=fCanUniqueKey(_Codigo, "PRODUTO" + coldprod)
	EndIf
	If !(coldprod == cnewprod) or Empty(CrSigCdPro.cpros)	
		lnserial = Transf(fGerUniqueKey("PRODUTO" + cnewprod), "@L 9999")
		cnewprod = cnewprod + lnserial
		replace cpros with cnewprod in CrSigCdPro
		ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgDados.GetCpro.Refresh()		
	EndIf
EndIf

If Type([CrSigCdGrp.VendPeso])=[N] And CrSigCdGrp.VendPeso = 1 And Not Empty(This.Value)
	ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery([SigCdFip],[LocalCdFip],[Cods], This.Value)
	If Not Used([LocalCdFip])
		=MessageBox([Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!], 16, [Falha na Conexăo (CursorQuery - LocalCdFip)])
		Return .f.
	EndIf
	If Type([LocalCdFip.VendPeso])=[N] And LocalCdFip.VendPeso = 1
		This.parent.parent.pgComposicao.getPven.Value = crSigCdPro.PesoMs
	EndIf 
EndIf 
* Fim **************************************************************************************
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE GotFocus
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE GotFocus
This.Tag = Padr(This.Value, 3)
This.peAntValue = this.Value
ENDPROC

================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGCDPRO.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.cmdMinimo
* Classe: commandgroup (Base: commandgroup)
* Registro: 175
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE btnMinimo.Valid
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE btnMinimo.Valid
If InList(ThisForm.pcEscolha, [INSERIR], [ALTERAR], [CONSULTAR])
	If (ThisForm.pcEscolha = [CONSULTAR])
		lcQuery = [Select a.CPros ] + ;
					[From SigCdMin a ] + ;
				   [Where a.CPros = '] + crSigCdPro.CPros + [']

		If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, [LocalBusca]) < 1)
			=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (btnMinimo - LocalBusca)')
			Return .f.
		EndIf
		Go Top In LocalBusca
		If Eof([LocalBusca])
			=MessageBox([O Produto Năo Possui Estoque Mínimo Cadastrado!!!], 0+64, [Atençăo!!!])
			Return .f.
		EndIf
	EndIf
		
	Do Form SigCdEmn With crSigCdPro.CPros, [], ThisForm.pcEscolha, ;
						  crSigCdPro.DPros, crSigCdPro.CGrus, crSigCdPro.IFors, crSigCdPro.Reffs, crSigCdPro.QMins
EndIf
* Fim **************************************************************************************
ENDPROC


================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGCDPRO.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.Commandgroup1
* Classe: commandgroup (Base: commandgroup)
* Registro: 178
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Click
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Click
Local lnConfirma, lcFigura, lcDiretorio, lcArquivo, lcFigJpg, llBmp, llJpg, lcArquivo1

Select crSigCdPro
If InList(ThisForm.pcEscolha, 'INSERIR', 'ALTERAR')
	lcAntPath = Sys(5) + Sys(2003)
	lcDir = goSistema.DirImagens
	If Directory(lcDir)
		Set Default To &lcDir.
	EndIf

	lcFigura = Alltrim(GetPict('Formato Jpeg:JPG;Formato Bitmap:BMP', 'Nome do Arquivo:', 'Selecionar'))

	Set Default To &lcAntPath.

	If Not Empty(lcFigura) And File(lcFigura)
		If Not fTamanhoImagem(lcFigura, ThisForm.poDataMgr, .t.)
			Return 0
		EndIf

		If (MessageBox('Confirma a Transferęncia da Imagem ?', 4+32+256, '') <> 6)
			ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.Grupo_Salva.Cancelar.SetFocus
			Return .t.
		EndIf

		Wait Window 'Aguarde!!! Transferindo a Imagem...' NoWait

		Replace FigTecs With FileToStr(lcFigura) IN CrSigCdPro

		Wait Clear
	
		lcArquivo = Sys(2023) + [\] + goSistema.Sys2015Tmp + Sys(2015) + [.jpg]

		Select crSigCdPro
		With ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgDados
			Clear Resources
			.ImgFigTec.Picture = ''
			.ImgFigTec.Visible = .f.

			* Figura no Campo Memo
			If Not Empty(crSigCdPro.FigTecs) And Not IsNull(crSigCdPro.FigTecs)
				If (StrToFile(crSigCdPro.FigTecs, lcArquivo) > 0)
					.ImgFigTec.Visible = .t.
					.ImgFigTec.Picture = (lcArquivo)
				EndIf
			EndIf
		EndWith

		If (MessageBox('Deseja Excluir a Imagem Original ?', 4+32+256, '') = 6)
			Delete File (lcFigura)
		EndIf
	EndIf
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.Grupo_salva.Salva.SetFocus
EndIf
* Fim *********************************************************************************
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE cmdFigura.When
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE cmdFigura.When
Return InList(ThisForm.pcEscolha, 'INSERIR', 'ALTERAR')
ENDPROC

================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGCDPRO.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDados.cmdgFigCam
* Classe: commandgroup (Base: commandgroup)
* Registro: 204
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Click
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Click
Local lnConfirma, lcFigura, lcDiretorio, lcArquivo, lcFigJpg, llBmp, llJpg, lcArquivo1

Select crSigCdPro
If InList(ThisForm.pcEscolha, 'INSERIR', 'ALTERAR')

	lcAntPath = Sys(5) + Sys(2003)
	lcDir = goSistema.DirImagens
	If Directory(lcDir)
		Set Default To &lcDir.
	EndIf
	
	lcFigura = []
	DO form SigImage TO lcFigura

	*lcFigura = Alltrim(GetPict('Formato Jpeg:JPG;Formato Bitmap:BMP', 'Nome do Arquivo:', 'Selecionar'))

	Set Default To &lcAntPath.

	If Not Empty(lcFigura) And File(lcFigura)
		
		llMudaImg = .F.
	
		If Not fTamanhoImagem(lcFigura, Thisform.poDataMgr, .F.)

			*-- Rafael - 25/07/2016 - Altera o Tamanho da Imagem automaticamente
			Local lcStrImg1 As String, lcStrImg2 As String, lnRetTamImg1 As Integer, ImgCam as String 
			
			m.ImgCam = Filetostr(lcFigura)
			
			If crSigCdPac.nLargImgs > 0 And Not IsEmpty(m.ImgCam)

				m.lcStrImg1 = m.ImgCam
				m.lcStrImg2 = ''
				m.lnRetTamImg1 = fAjustarImg(m.lcStrImg1, @m.lcStrImg2, crSigCdPac.nLargImgs)

				If m.lnRetTamImg1 > 0
					llMudaImg = .T.
					= Messagebox('Largura / Altura da Imagem do Produto Alterada ' + Alltrim(Str(crSigCdPac.nLargImgs, 20, 0)) + ' para Pixels.', 64, [Atençâo !],100)
				Endif

			Endif

		Endif

		If (Messagebox('Confirma a Transferęncia da Imagem ?', 4+32+256, '') <> 6)
			Thisform.Pagina.Dados.Grupo_Salva.Cancelar.SetFocus
			Return .T.
		Endif

		Wait Window 'Aguarde!!! Transferindo a Imagem...' Nowait
				
		If llMudaImg
			lcImag = [data:image/jpeg;base64,]+Strconv(FileToStr(m.lcStrImg2),13,1046)
			Replace FigJpgs With m.lcStrImg2 In crSigCdPro
		Else
			lcImag = [data:image/jpeg;base64,]+Strconv(FileToStr(lcFigura),13,1046)
			Replace FigJpgs With lcImag In crSigCdPro
		EndIf 
		
		Wait Clear
	
		Replace DtFilms With Datetime() In crSigCdPro

		lcArquivo = Sys(2023) + [\] + goSistema.Sys2015Tmp + Sys(2015) + [.jpg]

		Select crSigCdPro
		With ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgDados 
			Clear Resources
			.ImgFigJpg.Picture = ''
			.ImgFigJpg.Visible = .f.

			* Figura no Campo Memo
			If Not Empty(crSigCdPro.FigJpgs) And Not IsNull(crSigCdPro.FigJpgs)
				lcFoto=Strconv(Strtran(Strtran(Strtran(crSigCdPro.FigJpgs,[data:image/png;base64,],[]),[data:image/jpeg;base64,],[]),[data:image/jpg;base64,],[]),14)
				If (StrToFile(lcFoto, lcArquivo) > 0)
					.ImgFigJpg.Visible = .t.
					.ImgFigJpg.Picture = (lcArquivo)
				EndIf
			EndIf
		EndWith

		If (MessageBox('Deseja Excluir a Imagem Original ?', 4+32+256, '') = 6)
			Delete File (lcFigura)
		EndIf
	EndIf
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgDados.getDPro.SetFocus
EndIf
* Fim *********************************************************************************

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE cmdFigura.When
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE cmdFigura.When
Return InList(ThisForm.pcEscolha, 'INSERIR', 'ALTERAR')
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE cmdCompoInserir.Click
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE cmdCompoInserir.Click
Local obrow, mater

oPagC = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgComposicao

If InList(ThisForm.pcEscolha, 'INSERIR', 'ALTERAR')
	Select crSigPrCpo
	Go Top In crSigPrCpo
	Locate For Empty(Mats)
	If Eof([crSigPrCpo])
		Insert Into crSigPrCpo (Cpros, DtMovs, cIdChaves, TpCalcCus) Values (crSigCdPro.Cpros, DateTime(), fUniqueIds(), 1)
	EndIf
	obrow = oPagC.grdCompo
	obrow.Refresh
	obrow.SetFocus 
	obrow.Column1.SetFocus
	obrow.Column1.Text1.SetFocus
EndIf

If ThisForm.TemTipos And ThisForm.TempTipos
	ThisForm.FiltrarCompo(1)
EndIf
* Fim *********************************************************************************
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE cmdCompoIexcluir.Click
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE cmdCompoIexcluir.Click
If InList(ThisForm.pcEscolha, 'INSERIR', 'ALTERAR')
	Select crSigPrCpo
	If Not Eof([crSigPrCpo])
		Delete
	EndIf
	
	If Not Eof()
		Skip 
		Skip - 1
	EndIf 
	If (crSigCdPam.AutComps=1)
		This.Parent.cmdCompoAtualiza.Click
	EndIf
	
	If ThisForm.TemTipos And ThisForm.TempTipos
		ThisForm.FiltrarCompo(1)
	EndIf

	ThisForm.TotalGrupocv
	ThisForm.TotalGrupo
	ThisForm.TotalPlan
	
	Goto Bottom
	
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgComposicao.grdCompo.SetFocus
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgComposicao.grdCompo.Refresh
EndIf
* Fim *********************************************************************************
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE cmdCompoAtualiza.Click
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE cmdCompoAtualiza.Click
Private pGru

pGru = crSigCdPro.CGrus

Local lcdescricao,lcgrupo,lcunidade,lcfornecedor, total, xRegistro
Local lnvalor,lcmoeda,lnprecoc,lcmoedac,lnprecov,lcmoedav,lnfcusto,lcmoepc,lnfvenda,lcmoepv

oPagD = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgDados
oPagC = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgComposicao

Select crSigPrCpo
xRegistro = Recno()
ThisForm.FiltrarCompo(1)
Select crSigPrCpo
Count to _xnrg
If InList(ThisForm.pcEscolha, 'INSERIR','ALTERAR') 
	If _xnrg > 0
		lnPrecoc = oPagC.getPcus.Value
		lcMoedac = oPagC.getmoec.Value
		lnFCusto = oPagC.getfcusto.Value
		lcMoePc	 = oPagC.getmoepc.Value

		* Consiste o Campo Moedac
		If (Empty(lcMoedac) Or Not ThisForm.poDataMgr.ChkRegister('SigCdMoe', 'CMoes', lcMoedac))
			=MessageBox('Moeda do Preço da Composiçăo Inválida (Custo)!!!', 16, 'Atençăo!!!')
			ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.ActivePage = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgComposicao.PageOrder
			OpagC.getmoec.SetFocus
			Return 0
		EndIf

		* Consiste o Campo Moepc
		If Not Empty(lnFCusto) And (Empty(lcMoePc) Or Not ThisForm.poDataMgr.ChkRegister('SigCdMoe', 'CMoes', lcMoepc))
			=MessageBox('Moeda do Fator Inválida (Custo)!!!', 16, 'Atençăo!!!')
			ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.ActivePage = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgComposicao.PageOrder
			OpagC.getmoepc.SetFocus
			Return 0
		EndIf

		ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdMoe', 'crMoe', 'CMoes', crSigCdPro.Moevs)
		Go Top In crMoe
		If (crMoe.FMults = 'S')
			If Empty(crSigCdPro.FVendas)
				=MessageBox('Fator de Venda Deve Ser Preenchido!!!', 16, 'Atençăo!!!')
				OpagC.getfvenda.SetFocus
				Return 0
			EndIf
			
			If Empty(crSigCdPro.MoePvs)
				=MessageBox('Moeda do Fator Deve Ser Preenchida!!!', 16, 'Atençăo!!!')
				OpagC.getmoepv.SetFocus
				Return 0
			EndIf
		Else
			If Not Empty(crSigCdPro.FVendas)
				=MessageBox('Fator de Venda Năo Pode Ser Preenchido!!!', 16, 'Atençăo!!!')
				OpagC.getfvenda.SetFocus
				Return 0
			EndIf
			
			If Not Empty(crSigCdPro.MoePvs)
				=MessageBox('Moeda do Fator Năo Pode Ser Preenchida!!!', 16, 'Atençăo!!!')
				oPagc.getmoepv.SetFocus
				Return 0
			EndIf
		EndIf

		Total    = 0
		TotPeso  = 0
		TotQtd   = 0
		TotCv    = 0
		Totpcv   = 0

		ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdMoe', 'crMoe', 'CMoes', crSigCdPro.Moecs)
		Go Top In crMoe
		If Not Empty(crMoe.Moeqs)
			m.Moedas = crMoe.Moeqs
			_Qtdeqs = Iif(crMoe.Qtdeqs = 0, 1, crMoe.Qtdeqs)
		Else
			m.Moedas = crSigCdPro.Moecs
			_Qtdeqs = 1
		EndIf
		Moec = fBuscarCotacao(m.Moedas, DateTime(), ThisForm.poDataMgr)  * _Qtdeqs

		ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdMoe', 'crMoe', 'CMoes', crSigCdPro.Moepcs)
		Go Top In crMoe
		If Not Empty(crMoe.Moeqs)
			m.Moedas = crMoe.Moeqs
			_Qtdeqs = Iif(crMoe.Qtdeqs = 0, 1, crMoe.Qtdeqs)
		Else
			m.Moedas = crSigCdPro.Moepcs
			_Qtdeqs = 1
		EndIf
		Moepc = fBuscarCotacao(m.Moedas, DateTime(), ThisForm.poDataMgr)  * _Qtdeqs

		ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdMoe', 'crMoe', 'CMoes', crSigCdPro.Moedas)
		Go Top In crMoe
		If Not Empty(crMoe.Moeqs)
			m.Moedas = crMoe.Moeqs
			_Qtdeqs = Iif(crMoe.Qtdeqs = 0, 1, crMoe.Qtdeqs)
		Else
			m.Moedas = crSigCdPro.Moedas
			_Qtdeqs = 1
		EndIf
		Moeda = fBuscarCotacao(m.Moedas, DateTime(), ThisForm.poDataMgr)  * _Qtdeqs

		Select crSigPrCpo
		Scan
			If Empty(crSigPrCpo.Mats) Or Empty(crSigPrCpo.Moeds)
				Loop
			EndIf

			lcQuery = [Select a.cUnis, a.cUnips, b.BPesos, A.Moevs, b.chkInstalas, b.AtuComps ] + ;
						[From SigCdPro a, SigCdGrp b ] + ;
					   [Where a.CPros = '] + crSigPrCpo.Mats + [' And ] + ;
					   		 [a.CGrus = b.CGrus]

			If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'crSomaGru') < 1)
				=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (crSomaGru - 1)')
				Return 0
			EndIf

			ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdMoe', 'crMoe', 'CMoes', crSigPrCpo.Moeds)
			Go Top In crMoe
			If Not Empty(crMoe.Moeqs)
				m.Moedas = crMoe.Moeqs
				_Qtdeqs = Iif(crMoe.Qtdeqs = 0, 1, crMoe.Qtdeqs)
			Else
				m.Moedas = crSigPrCpo.Moeds
				_Qtdeqs = 1
			EndIf
			Moem = fBuscarCotacao(m.Moedas, DateTime(), ThisForm.poDataMgr)  * _Qtdeqs

			ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdMoe', 'crMoe', 'CMoes', CrSomaGru.Moevs)
			Go Top In crMoe
			If Not Empty(crMoe.Moeqs)
				m.Moedas = crMoe.Moeqs
				_Qtdeqs = Iif(crMoe.Qtdeqs = 0, 1, crMoe.Qtdeqs)
			Else
				m.Moedas = CrSomaGru.Moevs
				_Qtdeqs = 1
			EndIf
			Moev = fBuscarCotacao(m.Moedas, DateTime(), ThisForm.poDataMgr)  * _Qtdeqs

			Go Top In crSomaGru
			If (InList(crSomaGru.BPesos,1,3))
				If Empty(crSigCdPro.MoePcs)
					With oPagC.getMoepc
						.Value = crSigPrCpo.Moeds
						.Refresh
					EndWith
				EndIf
				lcSql = [Select Fators From SigCdUni Where Cunis = ']+Iif(CrSomaGru.bPesos=1,CrSomaGru.Cunis,CrSomagru.CUnips)+[']
				=ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcsql,'LocalUni')
				lnFator = Iif(LocalUni.Fators = 0, 1, LocalUni.Fators )
				Select crSigPrCpo
				TotQtd = TotQtd + ( Iif(CrSomaGru.bPesos=1,crSigPrCpo.Qtds,CrSigPrCpo.Pesos) * lnFator )
			EndIf
			If (crSomaGru.AtuComps <> 2)
				Total = Total + (crSigPrCpo.PCompos * Iif(crSigPrCpo.chkInstalas=2, crSigPrCpo.Pesos, crSigPrCpo.Qtds)) * Moem / Moec
			EndIf
			TotCv  = (TotCv + ((crSigPrCpo.Vlrcvs * crSigPrCpo.Qtdcvs) * Moem / Moec))
			TotpCv = (TotPCv + ((crSigPrCpo.Vlrpvs * crSigPrCpo.Qtdcvs) * Moev / Moeda))

			Select crSigPrCpo
		EndScan
		Select CrSigPrCpo
		Locate For Recno() = xRegistro
		
		If Not Empty(crSigPrCpo.Mats)
			ThisForm.TotalGrupoCv
			ThisForm.TotalGrupo
			ThisForm.TotalPlan
		EndIf
		
		If (TotQtd <> 0)
			With oPagC.getPesom
				.Value = TotQtd
				.Refresh
			EndWith
		EndIf
		
		If (Total <> 0)
			With oPagC.getPcus
				.Value = Total
				.Refresh
			EndWith
		EndIf
		
		Replace TComps With .t. In crSigCdPro

	Endif

	If Not Empty(crSigCdPro.CFtios)
		If ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigPrFti', 'crSigPrFti', 'Cods', crSigCdPro.cftios)
			Go Top In crSigPrFti
			Cotftio = fBuscarCotacao(crSigPrFti.Moedas, DateTime(), ThisForm.poDataMgr)
			TotFtio = (crSigPrFti.Valors * Iif(CrSigPrFti.TpFtios=2,1,crSigCdPro.PesoMs) )
			With oPagC.get_pftio
				.Value = Totftio
				.Refresh
			EndWith
		EndIf
	Else
		With oPagC.get_pftio
			.Value = 0
			.Refresh
		EndWith
		With oPagC.get_mftio
			.Value = Space(3)
			.Refresh
		EndWith
	EndIf
	ThisForm.CalcPreco
EndIf
* Fim *********************************************************************************

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE cmdCompoPreco.Click
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE cmdCompoPreco.Click
Local lnRegAnt, xRegistro

Select CrSigCdPro
If Empty(CrSigCdPro.Moedas)
	Replace CrSigCdPro.Moedas With CrSigCdPro.MOecs in CrSigCdPro
Endif

Select crSigPrCpo
xRegistro = Recno()

ThisForm.FiltrarCompo(1)

Select crSigPrCpo
Scan
	=ThisForm.AtuaPreco()
	ThisForm.CalcFornec(crSigPrCpo.Mats)
EndScan
Select CrSigPrCpo
Locate For Recno() = xRegistro

ThisForm.CalcPreco

This.Parent.Parent.Refresh

ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgComposicao.cmdgCompo.cmdCompoAtualiza.Click
* Fim *********************************************************************************
ENDPROC

ENDPROC

================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE LostFocus

If ThisForm.habilitacompo And Not Eof([crSigPrCpo])
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgComposicao.grdCompo.SetFocus
EndIf

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE GotFocus
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE GotFocus
This.Tag = This.Value
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Valid
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Valid
Private pCod, pGru
Local codcor,xobj,rec,Codigo,loLista,lnRefCmp

lnOldSel = Select()
ThisForm.Podatamgr.cursorquery('SigCdGrp','TmpGru','Cgrus',crSigCdPro.Cgrus,[PrdRefCmp])
lnRefCmp = TmpGru.PrdRefCmp
Select(lnOldSel)

If Not ThisForm.habilitacompo 
	Return .t.
EndIf

lcArq = [crMtPrima]
If ThisForm.TemTipos And ThisForm.TempTipos
	lcArq = [crMtPrimaT]
EndIf

oPagC = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgComposicao
pCod  = crSigCdPro.Cpros

If (This.Tag <> This.Value)
	If (This.Value = pCod)
		=MessageBox('Composiçăo Inválida!!!', 0+48, '')
		This.Value = ''
		Return 0
	Else
		Select &lcArq.
		Set Filter To Custos = 1 In &lcArq.
		Select crSigCdPro
		If Not Empty(This.Value)
			Keyboard Chr(32) Plain
			lnInkey = Inkey()
			If Not Seek(Padr(This.Value, 14), lcArq, [CPros]) And Not Seek(This.Value, lcArq, [Reffs])
						
*!*					loBusca = CreateObject([frmprod], this.Value, [CPROS], 1000)
*!*					If Type('loBusca')<>'O'
*!*						This.Value = ''
*!*						Return 0
*!*					ENDIF
*!*					loBusca.Show()
*!*					*** move atributos do objeto para arquivo ***
*!*					SELECT &lcArq
*!*					ZAP
*!*					APPEND BLANK
*!*					replace cpros with loBusca.cPros

				If Not Seek(Padr(This.Value, 14), lcArq, [CPros]) And Not Seek(This.Value, lcArq, [Reffs])
					*--Rafael - 08/07/2016 - Busca de produto pela descriçăo, descritivo, referencia, Codigo	
					If lnRefCmp = 1
						lcProduto = Space(14)
						DO form SigOpBus With .f. TO lcProduto
						This.Value = lcProduto
						If Empty(This.Value)
							Return 0
						Else
							If Not Seek(Padr(This.Value, 14), lcArq, [CPros])
								=MessageBox([Composiçăo Informada năo está configurado como Matéria-Prima ou está Inativo.],0+64,[Atençăo])	
								This.Value = []
								Return 0
							EndIf 	
						Endif
					Else
						loBrowse = CreateObject([fwBuscaSel], lcArq, [CPros], Padr(This.Value, 14), [Matéria-Prima])
						loBrowse.AddColuna([CPros], [], [Código], .t., [CPros])
						loBrowse.AddColuna([DPros], [], [Descriçăo], .t., [DPros])
						loBrowse.AddColuna([Reffs], [], [Referencia], .t., [Reffs])
						loBrowse.AddColuna([CGrus], [xxxxxx], [Grupo])
						loBrowse.Show
					EndIf 
				EndIf
			EndIf
			ThisForm.LockScreen = .t.
			If LastKey() <> 27
				If (&lcArq..CPros = pCod)
					ThisForm.LockScreen = .f.
					MessageBox('Composiçăo Inválida !!',0+48,'')
					This.Value = ''
					Select &lcArq.
					Set Filter To
					Return 0
				Else
					lStrQuery = [Select * ] + ;
								[From SigCdPro ] + ;
								[Where CPros = ']+&lcArq..CPros+[' ]
					If ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lStrQuery,'CrListaRemota') < 1
						ThisForm.LockScreen = .f.
						=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (GrdCompo - 1)')
						Select &lcArq.
						Set Filter To
						Return 0
					EndIf
					Go Top In CrListaRemota
				
					With oPagC.grdcompo.Column1.text1
						.Value = CrListaRemota.CPros
						.Refresh
					EndWith
					With oPagC.grdcompo.Column2.text1
						.Value = CrListaRemota.DPros
						.Refresh
					EndWith
					With oPagC.grdcompo.Column3.text1
						If (This.Tag <> CrListaRemota.CPros)
							.Value = CrListaRemota.CUnis
							.Refresh
						EndIf
					EndWith

					Replace CGrus     With CrListaRemota.CGrus, ;
							Dtmovs    With DateTime(), ;
							cUniPs    With CrListaRemota.CUniPs,;
							cIdChaves With fUniqueIds() In crSigPrCpo

					If (This.Tag <> This.Value)
						With oPagC.grdcompo.Column4.text1
							.Value = CrListaRemota.CustoFs
							.Refresh
						EndWith
						With oPagC.grdcompo.Column7.text1
							.Value = CrListaRemota.Moecusfs
							.Refresh
						EndWith
						With oPagC.grdcompo.Column8.Text1
							lcObs = CrSigPrCpo.ObsCompos &&.Value
							If Not Empty(CrListaRemota.ObsPeds)
								lcObs = CrListaRemota.ObsPeds
							EndIf
							If Not Empty(CrListaRemota.ObsPes)
								lcObs = CrListaRemota.ObsPes
							EndIf
							
							.Value = lcObs
							.Refresh
						EndWith
						ThisForm.AlterouCompo = .t.

						pGru = CrListaRemota.CGrus
						ThisForm.poDataMgr.Requery('crSigCdGrp')
						Go Top In crSigCdGrp
						ThisForm.OrdGrade = Int(Val(Substr(crSigCdGrp.CfgGerGprs, 6, 1)))

						If CrSigCdGrp.ServPrds = 1
							Replace Cats With Left(This.Value,6) In CrSigPrCpo
						Endif
						Replace Etiqs with CrSigCdGrp.Etipads In CrSigPrCpo

						If !Empty(CrSigCdGrp.PadFase)
							Select CrSigCdPrf
							Go top
							Locate for Grupos = CrSigCdGrp.PadFase
							replace Grupos with CrSigCdGrp.PadFase in crSigPrCpo
							replace Ordems with CrSigCdPrf.Ordems in crSigPrCpo
						EndIf
						
						Select CrSigPrCpo
						=ThisForm.Atuapreco()
					EndIf

					Replace Compos    With CrListaRemota.Compos, ;
							DtMovs    With DateTime(), ;
							cUniPs    With CrListaRemota.CUniPs,;
							OrdCompos With CrListaRemota.OrdCompos In crSigPrCpo

					If (CrListaRemota.Varias = 1)
						With oPagC.Get_MatP
							.Value = Iif(Not Empty(CrListaRemota.Cproeqs),CrListaRemota.Cproeqs,CrListaRemota.Cpros)
							.Refresh
						EndWith
					EndIf 
				EndIf 
				&&Use In CrListaRemota
			Else
				ThisForm.LockScreen = .f.
				*This.Value = ''
				With oPagC.grdcompo.Column2.text1
					.Value = ''
					.Refresh
				EndWith
				Select &lcArq.
				Set Filter To
				Return 0
			EndIf	
			This.Refresh
		EndIf
	EndIf
	Select &lcArq.
	Set Filter To

	Select crSigPrCpo
	ThisForm.CalcFornec(crSigPrCpo.Mats)

	If Not ThisForm.CarregaInstal(crSigPrCpo.Mats)
		Return .f.
	EndIf
EndIf
ThisForm.LockScreen = .f.
ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgComposicao.grdCompo.Refresh
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE When
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE When
Return Inlist(ThisForm.pcEscolha, 'INSERIR', 'ALTERAR') and thisform.habilitacompo 

ENDPROC


================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGCDPRO.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgComposicao.grdCompo.Column2.Text1
* Classe: textbox (Base: textbox)
* Registro: 236
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE When
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE When
Return Inlist(ThisForm.pcEscolha, 'INSERIR', 'ALTERAR') And thisform.habilitacompo AND Empty(crSigPrCpo.Mats)

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Valid
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Valid
Private pCod, pGru, pDes
Local loLista

If Not ThisForm.HabilitaCompo 
	Return .t.
EndIf

lcArq = [crMtPrima]
If ThisForm.TemTipos And ThisForm.TempTipos
	lcArq = [crMtPrimaT]
EndIf

oPagC = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgComposicao
pCod = crSigCdPro.Cpros
pDes = crSigCdPro.Dpros

If (This.Tag <> This.Value)
	If (This.Value = pDes)
		=MessageBox('Composiçăo Inválida !!',0+48,'')
		This.Value = ''
		Return 0
	Else
		Select &lcArq.
		Set Filter To Custos = 1 In &lcArq.
		Select crSigCdPro
		If Not Empty(This.Value)
			Keyboard Chr(32) Plain
			Inkey()
			Select &lcArq.
		    Set Near On
			If Not Seek(Padr(This.Value, 65), lcArq, [DPros])
				loLista = CreateObject([fwBuscaSel], lcArq, [DPros], Padr(This.Value, 65), [Matéria Prima])
				loLista.AddColuna([DPros], [], 	     [Descriçăo], .t., [DPros])
				loLista.AddColuna([CPros], [], 	     [Código], .t., [CPros])
				loLista.AddColuna([CGrus], [xxxxxx], [Grupo])
				loLista.Show()
			EndIf
			Set Near Off

			If (Lastkey() <> 27)
				If (&lcArq..DPros = pDes)
					=MessageBox([Composiçăo Inválida!!!], 0+48, [])
					This.Value = []
					Select &lcArq.
					Set Filter To
					Return 0
				Else
					lStrQuery = [Select * ] + ;
								  [From SigCdPro ] + ;
								 [Where CPros = '] + &lcArq..CPros + [']

					If ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lStrQuery, [crListaRemota]) < 1
						MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (GrdCompo - 2)')
						Select &lcArq.
						Set Filter To
						Return 0
					EndIf
					Go Top In CrListaRemota

					With oPagC.grdcompo.Column1.text1
						.Value = CrListaRemota.Cpros
						.refresh
					EndWith
					With oPagC.grdcompo.Column2.text1
						.Value = CrListaRemota.Dpros
						.refresh
					EndWith
					With oPagC.grdcompo.Column3.text1
						If (This.Tag <> CrListaRemota.Cpros)
							.Value = CrListaRemota.Cunis
							.refresh
						EndIf
					EndWith
					Replace CGrus     With CrListaRemota.CGrus, ;
							Dtmovs    With DateTime(), ;
							cUniPs    With CrListaRemota.CUniPs,;
							cIdChaves With fUniqueIds() In crSigPrCpo

					If (This.Tag <> This.Value)
						With oPagC.grdcompo.Column4.text1
							.Value = CrListaRemota.CustoFs
							.Refresh
						EndWith
						With oPagC.grdcompo.Column7.text1
							.Value = CrListaRemota.Moecusfs
							.Refresh
						EndWith
						With oPagC.grdcompo.Column8.Text1
							lcObs = CrSigPrCpo.ObsCompos &&.Value
							If Not Empty(CrListaRemota.ObsPeds)
								lcObs = CrListaRemota.ObsPeds
							EndIf
							If Not Empty(CrListaRemota.ObsPes)
								lcObs = CrListaRemota.ObsPes
							EndIf
							
							.Value = lcObs
							.Refresh
						EndWith
						ThisForm.AlterouCompo = .t.

						pGru = CrListaRemota.CGrus
						ThisForm.poDataMgr.Requery('crSigCdGrp')
						Go Top In crSigCdGrp
						ThisForm.OrdGrade = Int(Val(Substr(crSigCdGrp.CfgGerGprs, 6, 1)))

						If !Empty(CrSigCdGrp.PadFase)
							Select CrSigCdPrf
							Go top
							Locate for Grupos = CrSigCdGrp.PadFase
							replace Grupos with CrSigCdGrp.PadFase in crSigPrCpo
							replace Ordems with CrSigCdPrf.Ordems in crSigPrCpo
						EndIf

						Replace Etiqs with CrSigCdGrp.Etipads In CrSigPrCpo
						
						Select CrSigPrCpo
						=ThisForm.Atuapreco()
					EndIf
		
					Replace Compos    With CrListaRemota.Compos, ;
							DtMovs    With DateTime(), ;
							cUniPs    With CrListaRemota.CUniPs,;
							OrdCompos With CrListaRemota.OrdCompos In crSigPrCpo

					If (CrListaRemota.Varias = 1)
						With oPagC.Get_MatP
							.Value = Iif(Not Empty(CrListaRemota.Cproeqs),CrListaRemota.Cproeqs,CrListaRemota.Cpros)
							.Refresh
						EndWith
					EndIf 
				EndIf 
&&				Use In CrListaRemota
			Else
				This.Value = ''
				Select &lcArq.
				Set Filter To
				Return 0
			EndIf	
			This.Refresh
		EndIf
	EndIf
	Select &lcArq.
	Set Filter To

	Select crSigPrCpo
	ThisForm.CalcFornec(crSigPrCpo.Mats)

	If Not ThisForm.CarregaInstal(crSigPrCpo.Mats)
		Return .f.
	EndIf
EndIf
ENDPROC

Go Bottom In crSigPrCpo

	Return .t.

	lcQuery = [Select b.pCustVens ] + ;
			    [From SigCdPro a, SigCdGrp b ] + ;
			   [Where a.CPros = '] + crSigPrCpo.Mats + [' And ] + ;
			   		 [a.CGrus = b.CGrus ]

	If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'crTmp') < 1)
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (GrdCompo - 3)')
		Return 0
	EndIf
	Go Top In crTmp

	Select crSigPrCpo	
	ThisForm.CalcFornec(crSigPrCpo.Mats)
	This.Tag = Str(This.Value, 12, 2)
EndIf


* Fim *********************************************************************************
ENDPROC

If (Val(This.Tag) <> This.Value) And (This.Value <> 0)
	lcQuery = [Select b.pCustVens,b.Fators,qtequalps, a.PesoMs, a.cGrus ] + ;
			    [From SigCdPro a, SigCdUni b ] + ;
			   [Where a.CPros = '] + crSigPrCpo.Mats + [' And ] + ;
			   		 [a.CUnis = b.CUnis]

	If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'crTmp') < 1)
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (GrdCompo - 4)')
		Return 0
	EndIf
	Go Top In crTmp
	
	If CrTmp.Fators = 1 And CrTmp.QtEqualps <> [S]
		Replace Qtscons With This.Value In CrSigPrCpo
		*** Tiago - 20/03/2012 - Vianna - Se a flag Calcula Peso Composiçăo = 1, calcula o peso total do componente através peso médio do seu cadastro
		pGru = crTmp.CGrus
		ThisForm.poDataMgr.Requery('crSigCdGrp')
		Go Top In crSigCdGrp
		ThisForm.OrdGrade = Int(Val(Substr(crSigCdGrp.CfgGerGprs, 6, 1)))

		If crSigCdGrp.respcads = 1		
			replace Pesos With This.Value * crTmp.PesoMs In CrSigPrCpo
			this.Parent.Parent.column11.Refresh()
		Endif
		***		
	EndIf
	Select crSigPrCpo
	=ThisForm.Atuapreco()
	ThisForm.CalcFornec(crSigPrCpo.Mats)
EndIf
* Fim *********************************************************************************
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Valid
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Valid
If Not Empty(This.Value)
	ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdGrp', 'crGrupo', 'cGrus', crSigCdPro.cGrus)
	ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdPro', 'LocalPro', 'Cpros', crSigCdPro.Cpros)
	PFalhb   = crGrupo.varpesos
	PesoReal = This.Value
	xPesagem = PesoReal
	
	If Type([crGrupo.VldVarPeso])=[N] And InList(crGrupo.VldVarPeso,0,1,3)
		If ( xPesagem <> LocalPro.Pesoms) And Not Empty(PFalhb)
			xDif = (((xPesagem / LocalPro.Pesoms) -1) * 100 )
			If ( xDif < ( PFalhb * -1 ) ) Or ( xDif > PFalhb And crSigCdPam.Sinals <> 2 )
				lcMsg = 'Peso Diferente do Peso da Tabela e fora do Limite de '+Transf(PFalhb,"@Z 999.99%")+Chr(13)+;
					'Tabela: '+Alltrim(Transf(LocalPro.Pesoms,"@Z 9999.999"))+' Real:'+Alltrim(Transform(xPesagem,"@Z 9999.999"))+' Dif. '+Transf(xDif,"@Z 999.99%")
				Messagebox( lcMsg, 32, '' )
				If Not fChecaAcesso('SIGCDPRO','LIBPESO')
					This.Value = LocalPro.Pesoms
				Else
					This.Value = PesoReal
				Endif
			Endif
		EndIf
	EndIf 
EndIf 
ENDPROC

================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGCDPRO.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgComposicao.Chk_Pvenda
* Classe: checkbox (Base: checkbox)
* Registro: 292
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Click
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Click
Go Top In crSigCdPam
With ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgComposicao

*** mena 06/10/2015 - retirado para fazer o calculo baseado nas moedas ***	
*!*		.GetPven.Value = (.GetPvIdeal.Value / Iif(.Get_Encarg.Value<>0,.Get_Encarg.Value,1))
*!*		.GetPven.Refresh
*!*		.GetMoev.Value = .GetMoeda.Value
*!*		.GetMoev.SetFocus
*!*		.GetMoev.Refresh

	*** mena 06/10/2015 - calcula preco de venda levando em conta as moedas envolvidas ***
	lnCotId = fBuscarCotacao(.GetMoeda.Value, DateTime(), ThisForm.poDataMgr)
	lnCotVd = fBuscarCotacao(.GetMoev.Value, DateTime(), ThisForm.poDataMgr)
	lnPven  = .GetPvIdeal.Value*IIF(thisform.tpcalcp = 7, 1, lnCotId/lnCotVd)
	
	.GetPven.Value = (lnPven / Iif(.Get_Encarg.Value<>0,.Get_Encarg.Value,1))
	.GetPven.Refresh

EndWith
Set Step On 
ThisForm.CalcPreco
This.Value = .f.

ENDPROC

* PROCEDURE When
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE When
Return (ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgComposicao.chkLiberaVenda.Value = 1) And ;
		InList(ThisForm.pcEscolha, 'INSERIR', 'ALTERAR') And This.Parent.getPvideal.Value >= 0 And ThisForm.Libprecovenda 
		
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Valid
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Valid
Private pPro
Local loBrowse, opagc, opagd, loLista

pPro = Iif(Empty(crSigCdPro.CPros), Replicate(Chr(254), 14), crSigCdPro.CPros)

oPagC = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgComposicao
oPagd = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgDados
Set Step On 
If Not Empty(This.Value)
	lcSql = [Select Cods, Descs, Moedas, Acrescs From SigPrFti Where Tipos <> 1]
	ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcSql,'TmpFtio')
	Select TmpFtio
	Index On Descs Tag Descs
	Index On cods Tag Cods
	If Not Seek(This.Value,'TmpFtio','Cods')
		loLista = CreateObject('fwBuscaInt','TmpFtio','Cods',This.Value,'Feitios', .t.)
		loLista.mAddColuna('Cods','','Cod')
		loLista.mAddColuna('Descs','','Descriçăo')
		loLista.Show()
		This.Value = TmpFtio.Cods
		This.Refresh
	Endif
	oPagc.getFtio.Value   = TmpFtio.Cods
	oPagc.Get_mftio.Value = TmpFtio.Moedas
	
	If Not Empty(TmpFtio.Acrescs)
		If (crSigCdPaC.chkMarkups = 2)
			oPagc.getMarkupA.Value = TmpFtio.Acrescs
		Else
			oPagc.getMargem.Value = TmpFtio.Acrescs
		EndIf
	EndIf
	
	If Empty(oPagC.GetMoeda.Value)
		oPagC.GetMoeda.Value = Tmpftio.Moedas
	Endif

	oPagc.Get_mftio.Refresh
	oPagc.getftio.Refresh
	oPagc.getMargem.Refresh
	oPagc.getMarkupA.Refresh
	oPagC.GetMoeda.Refresh

	Go Top In crSigPrPmi
	If Not Eof('crSigPrPmi')
		If (MessageBox('O Produto Encontra-se Em Promoçăo!!! Deseja Conferir ?', 4+32+256, '') = 6)
			Do Form SigOpPrm With ThisForm
		EndIf
	EndIf
Else
	oPagc.getFtio.Value   = ''
	oPagc.Get_mftio.Value = ''
EndIf
oPagc.getFtio.Refresh
oPagc.Get_mftio.Refresh
oPagc.getMargem.Refresh

If (ThisForm.Tpcalcp = 6)
	ThisForm.Calcpreco
EndIf

ENDPROC

Return (ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgComposicao.chkLiberaVenda.Value = 1) ;

If Not Empty(This.Parent.Getftio.Value) And This.Value <> 0
	MarkVd = This.Parent.GetFtio.Value
	lcSql = [Select * From SigPrFti Where Cods = ']+MarkVd+[']
	ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcSql,'TmpFtio')
	If (crSigCdPac.chkMarkups <> 2) And (TmpFtio.FaixaFs > 0) And Not Between(This.Value, TmpFtio.FaixaIs, TmpFtio.FaixaFs)
		MessageBox('Markup fora da Faixa definida pelo Cadastro de Feitio!!!',0+48,'')
		This.Value = 0
		Return 0
	Endif
Endif
ThisForm.CalcPreco

================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGCDPRO.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgComposicao.Get_MatP
* Classe: fwget (Base: textbox)
* Registro: 308
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Valid
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Valid
If !Empty(This.Value)
	m.loLista = CreateObject('fwBuscaExt',ThisForm.poDataMgr.pnIdConn,'SigCdPro','CrProds','CPros',This.Value,'Produtos',1000)
	If !(m.loLista.plAchouRegistro)
		m.loLista.mAddColuna('CPros','','Código')
		m.loLista.mAddColuna('DPros','','Descriçăo')
		m.loLista.Show()
	EndIf
	If CrProds.Varias <> 1
		MessageBox('Codigo Inválido!!! somente material com peso variável.',0+16,'')
		This.Value = ' '
		Return .F.
	Else
		This.Value = Evaluate('CrProds.CPros')
	Endif
EndIf
This.Refresh
Return(.T.)
ENDPROC


================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGCDPRO.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgComposicao.getPvideal
* Classe: fwget (Base: textbox)
* Registro: 311
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Valid
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Valid
Local Moecf, Moeda, lnMarkup

If This.Value < 0
	MessageBox('Valor Invalido!!!',16,'')
	Return .f.
EndIf

ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdMoe', 'crMoe', 'CMoes', crSigCdPro.MoeCusfs)
Go Top In crMoe
If Not Empty(crMoe.Moeqs)
	m.Moedas = crMoe.Moeqs
	_Qtdeqs = Iif(crMoe.Qtdeqs=0, 1, crMoe.Qtdeqs)
Else
	m.Moedas = crSigCdPro.Moecusfs
	_Qtdeqs = 1
EndIf
lnMoecf = fBuscarCotacao(m.Moedas, DateTime(), ThisForm.poDataMgr) * _qtdeqs

ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdMoe', 'crMoe', 'CMoes', crSigCdPro.Moedas)
Go Top In crMoe
If Not Empty(crMoe.Moeqs)
	m.Moedas = crMoe.Moeqs
	_Qtdeqs = Iif(crMoe.Qtdeqs=0, 1, crMoe.Qtdeqs)
Else
	m.Moedas = crSigCdPro.Moedas
	_Qtdeqs = 1
EndIf
lnMoeda = fBuscarCotacao(m.Moedas,DateTime(), ThisForm.poDataMgr) * _qtdeqs

lnMarkup = IIF(EMPTY(This.Parent.getCustof.value),0,This.Value/This.Parent.getCustof.Value)

If (crSigCdPro.MoeCusfs <> crSigCdPro.Moedas) && Tiago - 26/08/2015 - Mudei para checar Moecusfs, pois estava checando errado o campo Moecs
	lnMarkup = lnMarkup / lnMoecf * lnMoeda 
ENDIF

If Not ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgComposicao.cmdCalcVals.Visible 
	This.Parent.getMargem.Value = lnMarkup
	This.Parent.getMargem.Refresh
	ThisForm.CalcPreco
EndIf

RETURN .T.
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE When
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE When

       InList(ThisForm.pcEscolha, 'INSERIR', 'ALTERAR') And ;
       (This.Parent.getMargem.Value = 00 Or ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgComposicao.cmdCalcVals.Visible) And ;
       ThisForm.Tpcalcp <> 2 And (ThisForm.TpCalcp <> 6)
ENDPROC


================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGCDPRO.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgComposicao.chkLiberaCusto
* Classe: checkbox (Base: checkbox)
* Registro: 312
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Valid
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Valid
If (This.Value = 1)
	Do Form SigSnSen With [], [SigCdPro], [ALTCUSTO], [USUARIO] To loObj

	If (Type('loObj')='O') And Not Empty(loObj.Usuario)
		If loObj.Acesso
			=fGravarLog('T', 'PRODUTOS', Usuar, 'Houve Uma Tentativa de Liberaçăo de Alteraçăo de Custo do Produto [' + ;
						  Alltrim(crSigCdPro.CPros) + ' Pelo Usuário ' + loObj.Usuario)
		Else
			=fGravarLog('T', 'PRODUTOS', Usuar, 'Foi Liberada a Alteraçăo de Custo do Produto [' + ;
						  Alltrim(crSigCdPro.CPros) + ' Pelo Usuário ' + loObj.Usuario)
		EndIf
	EndIf

	This.Value = Iif(loObj.Acesso, 1, 0)
	This.Refresh
	Release loObj
EndIf
* Fim **************************************************************************************
ENDPROC

================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGCDPRO.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgComposicao.Get_cmkpc
* Classe: fwget (Base: textbox)
* Registro: 317
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Valid
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Valid
Local loLista
oPagC = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgComposicao
If Not Empty(This.Value)
	lcSql = [Select Cods, Descs, Moedas, Valors, TpFtios From SigPrFti Where Tipos = 1]
	ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcSql,'TmpFtio')
	Select TmpFtio
	Index On cods Tag Cods
	If Not Seek(This.Value,'TmpFtio','Cods')
		m.loLista = CreateObject('fwBuscaInt','TmpFtio','Cods',This.Value,'Feitios', .t.)
		m.loLista.mAddColuna('Cods','','Cod')
		m.loLista.mAddColuna('Descs','','Descriçăo')
		m.loLista.Show()
	EndIf
	This.Value = TmpFtio.Cods
	oPagc.GetMoePc.Value = TmpFtio.Moedas
	If TmpFtio.tpFtios = 2 And TmpFtio.Valors <> 0
		oPagc.Get_pftioc.Value = TmpFtio.Valors
	EndIf
	This.Refresh
	oPagc.GetMoepc.Refresh
	oPagc.Get_pfTioc.Refresh
Else
	This.Parent.get_pftioc.Value = 0
	This.Parent.get_pftioc.Refresh
EndIf
This.Refresh
Return(.T.)

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE LostFocus
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE LostFocus
Local opagc
Set Step On 
Go Top In crSigCdPam
If (crSigCdPam.AutComps = 1)
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgComposicao.cmdgCompo.cmdCompoAtualiza.Click
Else
	ThisForm.Calcpreco
EndIf
* Fim *********************************************************************************

ENDPROC

================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGCDPRO.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgComposicao.grdsubcp.Column1.Text1
* Classe: textbox (Base: textbox)
* Registro: 331
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE When
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE When
Return Inlist(ThisForm.pcEscolha, 'INSERIR', 'ALTERAR') and thisform.habilitacompo 

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Valid
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Valid
Private pCod, pGru
Local codcor,xobj,rec,Codigo,loLista

If Not ThisForm.habilitacompo 
	Return .t.
EndIf

lcArq = [crMtPrima]
If ThisForm.TemTipos And ThisForm.TempTipos
	lcArq = [crMtPrimaT]
EndIf

oPagC = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgComposicao
pCod  = crSigCdPro.Cpros

If (This.Tag <> This.Value)
	If (This.Value = pCod)
		=MessageBox('Composiçăo Inválida!!!', 0+48, '')
		This.Value = ''
		Return 0
	Else
		Select &lcArq.
		Set Filter To Custos = 1 In &lcArq.
		Select crSigCdPro
		If Not Empty(This.Value)
			Keyboard Chr(32) Plain
			lnInkey = Inkey()
			If Not Seek(Padr(This.Value, 14), lcArq, [CPros])
				loBrowse = CreateObject([fwBuscaSel], lcArq, [CPros], Padr(This.Value, 14), [Matéria-Prima])
				loBrowse.AddColuna([CPros], [], [Código], .t., [CPros])
				loBrowse.AddColuna([DPros], [], [Descriçăo], .t., [DPros])
				loBrowse.AddColuna([CGrus], [xxxxxx], [Grupo])
				loBrowse.Show
			EndIf
		
			ThisForm.LockScreen = .t.
			If LastKey() <> 27
				If (&lcArq..CPros = pCod)
					ThisForm.LockScreen = .f.
					MessageBox('Composiçăo Inválida !!',0+48,'')
					This.Value = ''
					Select &lcArq.
					Set Filter To
					Return 0
				Else
					lStrQuery = [Select * ] + ;
								[From SigCdPro ] + ;
								[Where CPros = ']+&lcArq..CPros+[' ]
					If ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lStrQuery,'CrListaRemota') < 1
						ThisForm.LockScreen = .f.
						=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (grdSubCp - 1)')
						Select &lcArq.
						Set Filter To
						Return 0
					EndIf
					Go Top In CrListaRemota
				
					With oPagC.grdSubCp.Column1.text1
						.Value = CrListaRemota.CPros
						.Refresh
					EndWith
					With oPagC.grdSubCp.Column2.text1
						.Value = CrListaRemota.DPros
						.Refresh
					EndWith
					With oPagC.grdSubCp.Column3.text1
						If (This.Tag <> CrListaRemota.CPros)
							.Value = CrListaRemota.CUnis
							.Refresh
						EndIf
					EndWith

					Replace CGrus     With CrListaRemota.CGrus, ;
							Dtmovs    With DateTime(), ;
							cUniPs    With CrListaRemota.CUniPs,;
							cIdChaves With fUniqueIds() In crSigSubCp

					If (This.Tag <> This.Value)
						With oPagC.grdSubCp.Column4.text1
							.Value = CrListaRemota.CustoFs
							.Refresh
						EndWith
						With oPagC.grdSubCp.Column7.text1
							.Value = CrListaRemota.Moecusfs
							.Refresh
						EndWith
						With oPagC.grdSubCp.Column8.Text1
							lcObs = CrSigSubCp.ObsCompos &&.Value
							If Not Empty(CrListaRemota.ObsPeds)
								lcObs = CrListaRemota.ObsPeds
							EndIf
							If Not Empty(CrListaRemota.ObsPes)
								lcObs = CrListaRemota.ObsPes
							EndIf
							
							.Value = lcObs
							.Refresh
						EndWith
						ThisForm.AlterouCompo = .t.

						pGru = CrListaRemota.CGrus
						ThisForm.poDataMgr.Requery('crSigCdGrp')
						Go Top In crSigCdGrp
						ThisForm.OrdGrade = Int(Val(Substr(crSigCdGrp.CfgGerGprs, 6, 1)))

						If CrSigCdGrp.ServPrds = 1
							Replace Cats With Left(This.Value,6) In CrSigSubCp
						Endif
						Replace Etiqs with CrSigCdGrp.Etipads In CrSigSubCp

						Select CrSigSubCp
						=ThisForm.Atuapreco()
					EndIf

					Replace Compos    With CrListaRemota.Compos, ;
							DtMovs    With DateTime(), ;
							cUniPs    With CrListaRemota.CUniPs,;
							OrdCompos With CrListaRemota.OrdCompos In crSigSubCp

					If (CrListaRemota.Varias = 1)
						With oPagC.Get_MatP
							.Value = Iif(Not Empty(CrListaRemota.Cproeqs),CrListaRemota.Cproeqs,CrListaRemota.Cpros)
							.Refresh
						EndWith
					EndIf 
				EndIf 
				Use In CrListaRemota
			Else
				ThisForm.LockScreen = .f.
				This.Value = ''
				Select &lcArq.
				Set Filter To
				Return 0
			EndIf	
			This.Refresh
		EndIf
	EndIf
	Select &lcArq.
	Set Filter To

	Select crSigSubCp
	ThisForm.CalcFornec(crSigSubCp.Mats)
EndIf
ThisForm.LockScreen = .f.
ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgComposicao.grdSubCp.Refresh
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE GotFocus
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE GotFocus
This.Tag = This.Value
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE LostFocus
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE LostFocus
If ThisForm.habilitacompo 
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgComposicao.grdSubCp.SetFocus
EndIf
ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgComposicao.grdSubCp.Refresh
ENDPROC


================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGCDPRO.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgComposicao.grdsubcp.Column2.Text1
* Classe: textbox (Base: textbox)
* Registro: 333
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE LostFocus
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE LostFocus
Go Bottom In crSIGPRCPO

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE GotFocus
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE GotFocus
This.Tag = This.Value
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Valid
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Valid
Private pCod, pGru, pDes
Local loLista

If Not ThisForm.HabilitaCompo 
	Return .t.
EndIf

lcArq = [crMtPrima]
If ThisForm.TemTipos And ThisForm.TempTipos
	lcArq = [crMtPrimaT]
EndIf

oPagC = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgComposicao
pCod = crSigCdPro.Cpros
pDes = crSigCdPro.Dpros

If (This.Tag <> This.Value)
	If (This.Value = pDes)
		=MessageBox('Composiçăo Inválida !!',0+48,'')
		This.Value = ''
		Return 0
	Else
		Select &lcArq.
		Set Filter To Custos = 1 In &lcArq.
		Select crSigCdPro
		If Not Empty(This.Value)
			Keyboard Chr(32) Plain
			Inkey()
			Select &lcArq.
		    Set Near On
			If Not Seek(Padr(This.Value, 40), lcArq, [DPros])
				loLista = CreateObject([fwBuscaSel], lcArq, [DPros], Padr(This.Value, 65), [Matéria Prima])
				loLista.AddColuna([DPros], [], 	     [Descriçăo], .t., [DPros])
				loLista.AddColuna([CPros], [], 	     [Código], .t., [CPros])
				loLista.AddColuna([CGrus], [xxxxxx], [Grupo])
				loLista.Show()
			EndIf
			Set Near Off

			If (Lastkey() <> 27)
				If (&lcArq..DPros = pDes)
					=MessageBox([Composiçăo Inválida!!!], 0+48, [])
					This.Value = []
					Select &lcArq.
					Set Filter To
					Return 0
				Else
					lStrQuery = [Select * ] + ;
								  [From SigCdPro ] + ;
								 [Where CPros = '] + &lcArq..CPros + [']

					If ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lStrQuery, [crListaRemota]) < 1
						MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (GrdCompo - 2)')
						Select &lcArq.
						Set Filter To
						Return 0
					EndIf
					Go Top In CrListaRemota
					With oPagC.grdcompo.Column1.text1
						.Value = CrListaRemota.Cpros
						.refresh
					EndWith
					With oPagC.grdcompo.Column2.text1
						.Value = CrListaRemota.Dpros
						.refresh
					EndWith
					With oPagC.grdcompo.Column3.text1
						If (This.Tag <> CrListaRemota.Cpros)
							.Value = CrListaRemota.Cunis
							.refresh
						EndIf
					EndWith

					Replace CGrus     With CrListaRemota.CGrus, ;
							Dtmovs    With DateTime(), ;
							cUniPs    With CrListaRemota.CUniPs,;
							cIdChaves With fUniqueIds() In CrSigSubCp

					If (This.Tag <> This.Value)
						With oPagC.grdcompo.Column4.text1
							.Value = CrListaRemota.CustoFs
							.Refresh
						EndWith
						With oPagC.grdcompo.Column7.text1
							.Value = CrListaRemota.Moecusfs
							.Refresh
						EndWith
						With oPagC.grdcompo.Column8.Text1
							lcObs = CrSigSubCp.ObsCompos &&.Value
							If Not Empty(CrListaRemota.ObsPeds)
								lcObs = CrListaRemota.ObsPeds
							EndIf
							If Not Empty(CrListaRemota.ObsPes)
								lcObs = CrListaRemota.ObsPes
							EndIf
							
							.Value = lcObs
							.Refresh
						EndWith
						ThisForm.AlterouCompo = .t.

						pGru = CrListaRemota.CGrus
						ThisForm.poDataMgr.Requery('crSigCdGrp')
						Go Top In crSigCdGrp
						ThisForm.OrdGrade = Int(Val(Substr(crSigCdGrp.CfgGerGprs, 6, 1)))
						
						Select CrSigSubCp
						=ThisForm.Atuapreco()
					EndIf
		
					Replace Compos    With CrListaRemota.Compos, ;
							DtMovs    With DateTime(), ;
							cUniPs    With CrListaRemota.CUniPs,;
							OrdCompos With CrListaRemota.OrdCompos In CrSigSubCp

					If (CrListaRemota.Varias = 1)
						With oPagC.Get_MatP
							.Value = Iif(Not Empty(CrListaRemota.Cproeqs),CrListaRemota.Cproeqs,CrListaRemota.Cpros)
							.Refresh
						EndWith
					EndIf 
				EndIf 
				Use In CrListaRemota
			Else
				This.Value = ''
				Select &lcArq.
				Set Filter To
				Return 0
			EndIf	
			This.Refresh
		EndIf
	EndIf
	Select &lcArq.
	Set Filter To
	
	Select crSigSubCp
	ThisForm.CalcFornec(CrSigSubCp.Mats)
EndIf

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------

ENDPROC

================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGCDPRO.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgComposicao.grdsubcp.Column4.Text1

* PROCEDURE Valid
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Valid
If Not ThisForm.habilitacompo 
	Return .t.
endif

If (Val(This.Tag) <> This.Value) And (This.Value <> 0)
	lcQuery = [Select b.pCustVens ] + ;
			    [From SigCdPro a, SigCdGrp b ] + ;
			   [Where a.CPros = '] + crSigSubCp.Mats + [' And ] + ;
			   		 [a.CGrus = b.CGrus ]

	If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'crTmp') < 1)
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (GrdSubCp - 3)')
		Return 0
	EndIf
	Go Top In crTmp

	Select crSigSubCp	
	ThisForm.CalcFornec(crSigSubCp.Mats)
	This.Tag = Str(This.Value, 12, 2)
EndIf


* Fim *********************************************************************************
ENDPROC

If Not Empty(crSigSubCp.Bloqueio) AND (Val(This.Tag) <> This.Value)
	Select crSigSubCp
	ThisForm.CalcFornec(crSigSubCp.Mats)
EndIf
* Fim *********************************************************************************
ENDPROC

	And ThisForm.habilitacompo And ThisForm.Tpcalcp <> 2

ENDPROC


================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGCDPRO.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgComposicao.grdsubcp.Column5.Text1
* Classe: textbox (Base: textbox)
* Registro: 339
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Valid
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Valid
If Not Thisform.habilitacompo 
	Return .t.
endif

If (Val(This.Tag) <> This.Value) And (This.Value <> 0)
	lcQuery = [Select b.pCustVens,b.Fators,qtequalps ] + ;
			    [From SigCdPro a, SigCduni b ] + ;
			   [Where a.CPros = '] + crSigSubCp.Mats + [' And ] + ;
			   		 [a.CUnis = b.CUnis]

	If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'crTmp') < 1)
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (grdSubCp - 4)')
		Return 0
	EndIf
	Go Top In crTmp
	
	If CrTmp.Fators = 1 And CrTmp.QtEqualps <> [S]
		Replace Qtscons With This.Value In CrSigSubCp
	EndIf
	Select CrSigSubCp
	=ThisForm.Atuapreco()
	ThisForm.CalcFornec(crSigSubCp.Mats)
EndIf
* Fim *********************************************************************************
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE When

================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGCDPRO.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgComposicao.grdsubcp.Column11.Text1
* Classe: textbox (Base: textbox)
* Registro: 351
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE When
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE When
Local m.retorno
m.Retorno = .f.
If Not IsEmpty(crSIGPRCPO.UniCompos)
	lcSql = [Select cEstos From SigCduni Where cunis = ']+crSIGPRCPO.UniCompos+[']
	ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcsql,'TmpUni')
	If TmpUni.cEstos = '3' And Not IsEmpty(crSIGPRCPO.cUniPs)
		m.Retorno = .t.
	EndIf
EndIf
Return Inlist(ThisForm.pcEscolha, 'INSERIR', 'ALTERAR') and thisform.habilitacompo And m.retorno

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Valid
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Valid
If Not Thisform.habilitacompo 
	Return .t.
EndIf
If (Val(This.Tag) <> This.Value) And (This.Value <> 0)
	lcQuery = [Select b.pCustVens,b.Fators ] + ;
			    [From SigCdPro a, SigCduni b ] + ;
			   [Where a.CPros = '] + crSIGPRCPO.Mats + [' And ] + ;
			   		 [a.CUnips = b.CUnis]

	If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'crTmp') < 1)
		=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (GrdSubCp - 4)')
		Return 0
	EndIf
	Go Top In crTmp
	
	If CrTmp.Fators = 1
		Replace Qtscons With This.Value In CrSigSubCp
	Endif
	Select CrSigSubCp
	=ThisForm.Atuapreco()
	ThisForm.CalcFornec(CrSigSubCp.Mats)
EndIf
* Fim *********************************************************************************
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE LostFocus
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE LostFocus
This.Tag = Str(This.Value, 12, 2)

ENDPROC

================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGCDPRO.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgComposicao.cmdgSubCp
* Classe: commandgroup (Base: commandgroup)
* Registro: 360
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE cmdCompoInserir.Click
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE cmdCompoInserir.Click
Local obrow, mater

oPagC = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgComposicao

If InList(ThisForm.pcEscolha, 'INSERIR', 'ALTERAR')
	Select crSIGPRCPO
	If Empty(crSIGPRCPO.mats)
		MessageBox('Composiçăo inválida.',48,'Aviso')
		Return .f.
	EndIf

	Select crSigSubCp
	Go Top In crSigSubCp
	Locate For Empty(Mats)
	If Eof([crSigSubCp])
		Insert Into crSigSubCp (Cpros, DtMovs, cIdChaves, TpCalcCus, matsubs) Values (crSigCdPro.Cpros, DateTime(), fUniqueIds(), 1, crSIGPRCPO.mats)
	EndIf
	obrow = oPagC.grdSubCp
	obrow.Refresh
	obrow.SetFocus 
	obrow.Column1.SetFocus
	obrow.Column1.Text1.SetFocus
EndIf

If ThisForm.TemTipos And ThisForm.TempTipos
	ThisForm.FiltrarCompo(1)
EndIf
* Fim *********************************************************************************
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE cmdCompoIexcluir.Click
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE cmdCompoIexcluir.Click
If InList(ThisForm.pcEscolha, 'INSERIR', 'ALTERAR')
	Select crSigSubCp
	If Not Eof([crSigSubCp])
		Delete
	EndIf
	
	If Not Eof()
		Skip 
		Skip - 1
	EndIf 
	
	If ThisForm.TemTipos And ThisForm.TempTipos
		ThisForm.FiltrarCompo(1)
	EndIf

	ThisForm.TotalGrupocv
	ThisForm.TotalGrupo
	ThisForm.TotalPlan
	
	Goto Bottom
	
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgComposicao.grdSubCp.SetFocus
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgComposicao.grdSubCp.Refresh
EndIf
* Fim *********************************************************************************
ENDPROC

================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGCDPRO.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDadosFiscais.getClfiscal
* Classe: fwget (Base: textbox)
* Registro: 374
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Valid
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Valid
Local loLista

If Not Empty(This.Value)
	loLista = CreateObject('fwBuscaExt', ThisForm.poDataMgr.pnIdConn, 'SigCdClf', ;
						   'CrListaRemota', 'Codigos', This.Value, 'Seleçăo', .t.)

	If Not loLista.plAchouRegistro
		loLista.mAddColuna('Codigos',    '', 'Código')
		loLista.mAddColuna('Descricaos', '', 'Descriçăo')
		loLista.Show()
	EndIf
	
	If (Lastkey() <> 27)
		This.Parent.getClfiscal.Value  = CrListaRemota.Codigos
		This.Parent.getDclfiscal.Value = CrListaRemota.Descricaos

		This.parent.Say_AliqIPI.Enabled = ( CrListaRemota.IpiProds = [S] )
		This.parent.Get_AliqIPI.Enabled = ( CrListaRemota.IpiProds = [S] )
	Else
		This.Parent.getClfiscal.Value  = ''
		This.Parent.getDclfiscal.Value = ''
		This.parent.Say_AliqIPI.Enabled = (.f.)
		This.parent.Get_AliqIPI.Enabled = (.f.)
	EndIf

	Use In CrListaRemota
Else
	This.Parent.getClfiscal.Value  = ''
	This.Parent.getDclfiscal.Value = ''
	This.parent.Say_AliqIPI.Enabled = (.f.)
	This.parent.Get_AliqIPI.Enabled = (.f.)
EndIf
This.Parent.getClfiscal.Refresh
This.Parent.getDclfiscal.Refresh
* Fim *********************************************************************************

ENDPROC

	Endif

	This.parent.Get_dcontaccus.Refresh
	return(.t.)

	StrToFile(crSigCdPrf.FigProcs, lcArquivo)

================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGCDPRO.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.PgDadosFaseP.cmdgFigura
* Classe: commandgroup (Base: commandgroup)
* Registro: 430
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Click
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Click
Local lnConfirma,lcFigura,lcDiretorio,lcArquivo,lcFigJpg,llJpg,lcArquivo1

Select crSigCdPrf
If Eof() Or Bof()
	Return 0
EndIf

ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgDadosFaseP.GradFase.SetFocus

If InList(ThisForm.pcEscolha, 'INSERIR', 'ALTERAR')
	lcAntPath = Sys(5) + Sys(2003)
	lcDir = goSistema.DirImagens
	If Directory(lcDir)
		Set Default To &lcDir.
	EndIf
	
	lcFigura = Alltrim(GetPict('Formato Jpeg:JPG;Formato Bitmap:BMP', 'Nome do Arquivo:', 'Selecionar'))

	Set Default To &lcAntPath.

	If Not Empty(lcFigura) And File(lcFigura)
		If Not fTamanhoImagem(lcFigura, ThisForm.poDataMgr, .t.)
			Return 0
		EndIf

		If (MessageBox('Confirma a Transferęncia da Imagem ?', 4+32+256, '') <> 6)
			ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.Grupo_Salva.Cancelar.SetFocus
			Return .t.
		EndIf

		Wait Window 'Aguarde!!! Transferindo a Imagem...' NoWait

		Replace FigProcs With FileToStr(lcFigura) IN CrSigCdPrf
				
		Wait Clear

		lcArquivo = Sys(2023) + [\] + goSistema.Sys2015Tmp + Sys(2015) + [.jpg]

		With ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgDadosFaseP
			Clear Resources
			.ImgFigJpg.Picture = ''
			.ImgFigJpg.Visible = .f.

			* Figura no Campo Memo
			If Not Empty(crSigCdPrf.FigProcs) And Not IsNull(crSigCdPrf.FigProcs)
				If (StrToFile(crSigCdPrf.FigProcs, lcArquivo) > 0)
					.ImgFigJpg.Visible = .t.
					.ImgFigJpg.Picture = (lcArquivo)
				EndIf
			EndIf
		EndWith

		If (MessageBox('Deseja Excluir a Imagem Original ?', 4+32+256, '') = 6)
			Delete File (lcFigura)
		EndIf
	EndIf

	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgDadosFaseP.GradFase.Column1.SetFocus
EndIf
* Fim *********************************************************************************

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE cmdFigura.When
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE cmdFigura.When
Return InList(ThisForm.pcEscolha, 'INSERIR', 'ALTERAR')
ENDPROC

	Clear Resources
	.ImgFigJpg.Picture = ''
	.ImgFigJpg.Visible = .f.

	* Figura no Campo Memo
	If Not Empty(crSigCdPrf.FigProcs) And Not IsNull(crSigCdPrf.FigProcs)
		If (StrToFile(crSigCdPrf.FigProcs, lcArquivo) > 0)
			.ImgFigJpg.Visible = .t.

		EndIf

=Seek(CrSigCdPrf.Grupos,'CrSigCdGcr')

================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGCDPRO.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.PgDadosFaseP.GradFase.Column1.Text1
* Classe: textbox (Base: textbox)
* Registro: 436
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE When
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE When
Return .f.
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE LostFocus
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE LostFocus
Local lnCont

ThisForm.LockScreen = .t.
If (This.Value > 0) And (This.Value <> ThisForm.AntOrd)
	Ponteiro = Recno('crSigCdPrf')
	
	Select crSigCdPrf
	Set Order To '' In crSigCdPrf && desativa o set key ...
	Set Relation Off Into crSigCdGcr
	Scan
 		If (Recno() <> Ponteiro)
	 		Replace Ordem2 With crSigCdPrf.Ordems * 10 In crSigCdPrf
	 	Else
			If (This.Value < ThisForm.AntOrd)
				Replace Ordem2 With (This.Value * 10 - 1) In crSigCdPrf
			Else
				Replace Ordem2 With (This.Value * 10 + 1) In crSigCdPrf
			EndIf
	 	EndIf
	EndScan

	Select crSigCdPrf
	Set Order to Linhas
	lnCont = 1
 	Scan
 		Replace Ordems With lnCont, ;
 				Ordem2 With lnCont In crSigCdPrf
 		lnCont = lnCont + 1
	EndScan
Else
	This.Value = ThisForm.AntOrd
EndIf

Select crSigCdPrf
Set Order To Linhas In crSigCdPrf
Set Order To Codigos In crSigCdGcr
Set Relation To crSigCdPrf.Grupos Into crSigCdGcr

ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.PgFrameDados.PgDadosFaseP.GradFase.Refresh
ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.PgFrameDados.PgDadosFaseP.GradFase.SetFocus
ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.PgFrameDados.PgDadosFaseP.GradFase.Column2.SetFocus
ThisForm.LockScreen = .f.
* Fim *********************************************************************************

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE GotFocus
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE GotFocus
ThisForm.AntOrd = This.Value
ENDPROC

================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGCDPRO.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.PgDadosFaseP.inserir
* Classe: fwbtnp (Base: commandbutton)
* Registro: 445
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Click
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Click
ThisForm.LockScreen = .t.

ProdutoAux = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.PgFrameDados.PgDados.getCPro.Value

Select crSigCdPrf
Set Order To Linhas In crSigCdPrf

Select crSigCdPrf
If Not Eof('crSigCdPrf')
	If Empty(crSigCdPrf.Grupos)
		ThisForm.LockScreen = .f.
		ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.PgFrameDados.PgDadosFAseP.GradFase.SetFocus
		Return 0
	EndIf
	OrdemAux = crSigCdPrf.Ordems
Else
	OrdemAux = 0
EndIf
lcGrupo = CrSigCdPrf.Grupos

Set Order To
Go Top
Scan For Ordems > OrdemAux
	Select CrSigCdPrf
	lnOrdem = Ordems
	lcgrupo = Grupos
	Replace Ordems With Ordems + 1,;
			Ordem2 With Ordems * 10 in CrSigCdPrf

	Select CrSigPrCpo
	If ThisForm.TemTipos And ThisForm.TempTipos
		Set Filter To (TpCalcCus < 2) Or Empty(Mats) In crSigPrCpo
	EndIf
	Replace Ordems With CrSigCdPrf.Ordems For Ordems = lnOrdem And Grupos = lcGrupo in CrSigPrCpo

	Select CrSigCdPrf
EndScan

Select CrSigCdPrf
Set Order To Linhas
Locate For Ordems = OrdemAux

Insert Into crSigCdPrf (Produtos, Ordems, Ordem2, cIdChaves) ;
			   Values (ProdutoAux, OrdemAux+1, (OrdemAux+1) * 10, fUniqueIds())

With ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgDadosFaseP.GradFase
	.Refresh
	.SetFocus
	.Column2.SetFocus
	.Column2.Text1.SetFocus
EndWith	
ThisForm.LockScreen = .f.

ENDPROC


================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGCDPRO.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.PgDadosFaseP.excluir
* Classe: fwbtnp (Base: commandbutton)
* Registro: 446
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Click
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Click
If Eof() Or Bof()
	Return
EndIf

ThisForm.LockScreen = .t.

Select crSigCdPrf
Set Order To Linhas In crSigCdPrf

With ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.PgFrameDados.PgDadosFaseP
	.SetFocus
	.GradFase.Column2.SetFocus
EndWith	

Delete
If Not Eof() And Not Bof()
	Skip
Endif
If Eof()
	Go Bott
Endif
Ponteiro = Recno()
Go top
Locate For Recno() = Ponteiro
llInicio = .f.
If ! Bof()
	Skip -1
	If Bof()
		llInicio = .t.
	EndIf
EndIf 
If Bof()
	Go Top
Endif

If Not Eof('crSigCdPrf')

	If Not llInicio
		ContAux  = Ordems
		Skip
	Else
		ContAux  = 0
	Endif

	DO While Not EOF()
		ContAux = ContAux + 1
		Select CrSigCdPrf
		lnOrdem = Ordems
		lcGrupo = Grupos
		Replace Ordems With ContAux While Ordems = lnOrdem In crSigCdPrf

		Select CrSigPrCpo
		If ThisForm.TemTipos And ThisForm.TempTipos
			Set Filter To (TpCalcCus < 2) Or Empty(Mats) In crSigPrCpo
		EndIf
		Replace Ordems With ContAux For Ordems = lnOrdem And Grupos = lcGrupo
		
		Select CrSigCdPrf
		
	EndDo
EndIf
Locate for Recno() = Ponteiro

Select crSigCdPrf

With ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgDadosFaseP.GradFase
	.Refresh
	.Column2.SetFocus
EndWith
	
ThisForm.LockScreen = .f.

ENDPROC


================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGCDPRO.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.PgDadosFaseP.Alternativa
* Classe: fwbtnp (Base: commandbutton)
* Registro: 447
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Click
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Click
ThisForm.LockScreen = .t.

ProdutoAux = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.PgFrameDados.PgDados.getCPro.Value

Select crSigCdPrf
Set Order To Linhas In crSigCdPrf

Select crSigCdPrf
If Not Eof('crSigCdPrf')
	If Empty(crSigCdPrf.Grupos)
		ThisForm.LockScreen = .f.
		ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.PgFrameDados.PgDadosFAseP.GradFase.SetFocus
		Return 0
	EndIf
	OrdemAux = crSigCdPrf.Ordems
Else
	ThisForm.LockScreen = .f.
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.PgFrameDados.PgDadosFAseP.GradFase.SetFocus
	Return 0
EndIf

Count to OrdemAux2 For Ordems = OrdemAux

Insert Into crSigCdPrf (Produtos, Ordems, Ordem2, cIdChaves) ;
			   Values (ProdutoAux, OrdemAux, (OrdemAux * 10) + OrdemAux2 + 1 , fUniqueIds())

Ponteiro = Recno()
ContAux = OrdemAux
skip
If Not Eof('crSigCdPrf')
	DO While Not EOF()
		ContAux = ContAux + 1
		Replace Ordems With ContAux In crSigCdPrf
		Skip
	EndDo
EndIf
Go Ponteiro

If Not Eof()
	Skip -1
	If Not Eof()
		Skip
	EndIf
EndIf

With ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgDadosFaseP.GradFase
	.Refresh
	.SetFocus
	.Column2.SetFocus
	.Column2.Text1.SetFocus
EndWith	
ThisForm.LockScreen = .f.

ENDPROC


================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGCDPRO.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.PgDadosFaseP.CmdFicha
* Classe: fwbtnp (Base: commandbutton)
* Registro: 448
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Click
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Click
Local lcOldOrd

Create Cursor CsCabecalho ( _NmEmp C(80), _NmTit C(99), _cPros C(14), _dPros C(65), _cGrus C(03), _dGrus C(20), ;
							_sGrus C(06), _sDesc C(20), _cLinh C(10), _dLinh C(40), _cGVen C(10), _dGVen C(40), ; 
							_nPeso N(9,2), _DtIni D(08), _DtFin D(08), _TExec C(15), _cMode C(10), _dMode C(50))

_NmEmp = ''
If ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery('SigCdEmp', 'crTmp', 'Cemps', _Empr)
	Go Top In crTmp
	_NmEmp = crTmp.Razas
EndIf
Use In crTmp

_NmTit = 'Ficha Técnica de Produto'
With ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados
	m._nPeso = .PgComposicao.getPesom.Value
	With .pgDados
		m._cPros = .getCpro.Value
		m._dPros = .getDpro.Value
		m._cGrus = .getCgru.Value
		m._dGrus = .getDgru.Value
		m._sGrus = .GetCSGru.Value
		m._sDesc = .GetDsGru.Value
		m._cLinh = .GetLin.Value
		m._dLinh = .GetDLin.Value
		m._cGVen = .GetCol.Value
		m._dGVen = .GetDCol.Value
	EndWith
EndWith

Insert Into csCabecalho From Memvar

Select crSigCdPrf

If ThisForm.Tipo2
	Select f.produtos, f.ordems, f.grupos, f.figProcs, f.Descrs, f.Ordem2, ;
		   f.Obs, 'TP'+PADL(allt(str(f.Ordems)),3,'0') as ident ;
	  From crSigCdPrf f ;
	 Order By Ordems ;
	  Into Cursor CsDetalhes ReadWrite
Else
	Select f.produtos, f.ordems, f.grupos, f.figProcs, f.Descrs, f.Ordem2, ;
		f.Obs, 'TP'+PADL(allt(str(f.Ordems)),3,'0') as ident ;
	From crSigCdPrf f ;
	Order By Ordems ;
	Into Cursor CsDetalhes ReadWrite
EndIf

Select CsDetalhes

Update CsDetalhes Set Ordem2 = Recno()
Update CsDetalhes Set Ident  = 'TP'+PADL(allt(str(Ordem2)),3,'0') 
 
lcFigJpg = Addbs(JustPath(ThisForm.poDataMgr.GetDatabase())) + 'BrJpg.JPG'
Create Cursor CrBranco (Branco M)
Select CrBranco
Append Blank
Append Memo Branco From (lcFigJpg) Overwrite
Select CsDetalhes
Scan
	xImg = Alltrim(Ident)
	lcArquivo = Sys(2023) + '\' + xImg + '.JPG'
	Clear Resources
	If Not Empty(CsDetalhes.FigProcs) And Not IsNull(CsDetalhes.FigProcs)
		=StrToFile(csDetalhes.FigProcs, lcArquivo)
	Else
		=StrToFile(crBranco.Branco, lcArquivo)
	EndIf
EndScan

Do Form SigReFtp With m._cPros, m._dPros
* Fim *********************************************************************************

ENDPROC

						   'CrListaRemota', 'Cods', This.Value, 'Seleçăo', .t.)

	If Not loLista.plAchouRegistro

		This.Parent.Get_dacb.Value = ''

	Use In CrListaRemota

	This.Parent.Get_dacb.Value = ''
EndIf

This.Parent.Get_dacb.Refresh
