------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Valid
Local loLista, lcQuery
*** Mostra lista de conquilhas ***
lcQuery = [Select conquilhas From SigCdCnq group by conquilhas]
IF (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, [crLocal])) >0

	If Not Empty(This.Value)
		Select crLocal
		Index On conquilhas tag CON
		If Not Seek(Padr(This.Value, 10), [crLocal], [con])
			loLista = CreateObject([fwBuscaInt], [crLocal], [conquilhas], This.Value, [Conquilhas], .t.)
			loLista.mAddColuna([conquilhas], [], [Conquilhas], 	 .t.)
			loLista.Show()
		EndIf
		This.Value = Iif(Lastkey()=27, [], crLocal.conquilhas)
	EndIf
ELSE

ENDIF

This.Refresh
* Fim *********************************************************************************

ENDPROC

PROCEDURE AfterRowColChange
Lparameters nColIndex

Local lcArquivo

lcArquivo = Sys(2023) + [\] + goSistema.Sys2015Tmp + Sys(2015) + [.jpg]

With ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgDadosFaseP
	Clear Resources
	.ImgBorracha.Picture = []
	.ImgBorracha.Visible = .f.

	lcQuery = [Select * ] + ;
			    [From SigCdPro ] + ;
			   [Where CPros = '] + crSigPrMtz.CMats + [']

	If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, [LocalImgPro]) < 1)
		=MessageBox([Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!], 16, [Falha na Conexăo (LocalImgPro)])
		Return 0
	EndIf

	If Not Eof([LocalImgPro]) And Not Empty(LocalImgPro.FigJpgs) And Not IsNull(LocalImgPro.FigJpgs)
		lcFoto=Strconv(Strtran(Strtran(Strtran(LocalImgPro.FigJpgs,[data:image/png;base64,],[]),[data:image/jpeg;base64,],[]),[data:image/jpg;base64,],[]),14)
		If (StrToFile(lcFoto, lcArquivo) > 0)
			.ImgBorracha.Visible = .t.
			.ImgBorracha.Picture = (lcArquivo)
		EndIf
	EndIf
EndWith
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Valid
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Valid

	Select crMatrizes
	If Not Seek(Padr(This.Value, 14), [crMatrizes], [CPros])
		loLista = CreateObject([fwBuscaInt], [crMatrizes], [CPros], This.Value, [Matriz], .t.)
		loLista.mAddColuna([CPros],  [], [Matriz], 	  .t.)
		loLista.mAddColuna([DPros],  [], [Descriçăo], .t.)
		loLista.mAddColuna([Locals], [], [Local],     .t.)
		loLista.Show()
	EndIf
	If (Lastkey() <> 27)
		ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDadosFaseP.grdMAtrizes.Column1.Text1.Value = crMatrizes.CPros
		ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDadosFaseP.grdMAtrizes.Column3.Text1.Value = crMatrizes.Locals
	Else
		ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDadosFaseP.grdMAtrizes.Column1.Text1.Value = []
		ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDadosFaseP.grdMAtrizes.Column3.Text1.Value = []
	EndIf
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDadosFaseP.grdMAtrizes.Column1.Text1.Refresh 
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDadosFaseP.grdMAtrizes.Column3.Text1.Refresh 
EndIf

================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGCDPRO.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.PgDadosFaseP.cmdgFigCam
* Classe: commandgroup (Base: commandgroup)
* Registro: 481
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Click
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Click
Local lnConfirma,lcFigura,lcDiretorio,lcArquivo,lcFigJpg,llJpg,lcArquivo1

Select crSigCdPrf
If Eof() Or Bof()
	Return 0
EndIf

ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgDadosFaseP.GradFase.SetFocus

If InList(ThisForm.pcEscolha, 'INSERIR', 'ALTERAR')
	lcAntPath = Sys(5) + Sys(2003)
	lcDir = goSistema.DirImagens
	If Directory(lcDir)
		Set Default To &lcDir.
	EndIf
	
	lcFigura = []
	DO form SigImage TO lcFigura
	Set Default To &lcAntPath.
	If Not Empty(lcFigura) And File(lcFigura)
		llMudaImg = .F.
		If Not fTamanhoImagem(lcFigura, Thisform.poDataMgr, .F.)
			Local lcStrImg1 As String, lcStrImg2 As String, lnRetTamImg1 As Integer, ImgCam as String 
			m.ImgCam = Filetostr(lcFigura)
			If crSigCdPac.nLargImgs > 0 And Not IsEmpty(m.ImgCam)
				m.lcStrImg1 = m.ImgCam
				m.lcStrImg2 = ''
				m.lnRetTamImg1 = fAjustarImg(m.lcStrImg1, @m.lcStrImg2, crSigCdPac.nLargImgs)

				If m.lnRetTamImg1 > 0
					llMudaImg = .T.
					= Messagebox('Largura / Altura da Imagem do Produto Alterada ' + Alltrim(Str(crSigCdPac.nLargImgs, 20, 0)) + ' para Pixels.', 64, [Atençâo !],100)
				Endif
			Endif
		Endif

		If (Messagebox('Confirma a Transferęncia da Imagem ?', 4+32+256, '') <> 6)
			Thisform.Pagina.Dados.Grupo_Salva.Cancelar.SetFocus
			Return .T.
		Endif

		Wait Window 'Aguarde!!! Transferindo a Imagem...' Nowait
		
		If llMudaImg
			Replace FigProcs With m.lcStrImg2 In CrSigCdPrf
		Else
			Replace FigProcs With Filetostr(lcFigura) In CrSigCdPrf
		EndIf 
		
		Wait Clear

		lcArquivo = Sys(2023) + [\] + goSistema.Sys2015Tmp + Sys(2015) + [.jpg]

		With ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgDadosFaseP
			Clear Resources
			.ImgFigJpg.Picture = ''
			.ImgFigJpg.Visible = .f.

			* Figura no Campo Memo
			If Not Empty(crSigCdPrf.FigProcs) And Not IsNull(crSigCdPrf.FigProcs)
				If (StrToFile(crSigCdPrf.FigProcs, lcArquivo) > 0)
					.ImgFigJpg.Visible = .t.
					.ImgFigJpg.Picture = (lcArquivo)
				EndIf
			EndIf
		EndWith

		If (MessageBox('Deseja Excluir a Imagem Original ?', 4+32+256, '') = 6)
			Delete File (lcFigura)
		EndIf
	EndIf

	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgDadosFaseP.GradFase.Column1.SetFocus
EndIf
* Fim *********************************************************************************

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE cmdFigura.When
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE cmdFigura.When
Return InList(ThisForm.pcEscolha, 'INSERIR', 'ALTERAR')
ENDPROC

================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGCDPRO.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.PgDadosConsP.GrdCons.Column1.Text1
* Classe: textbox (Base: textbox)
* Registro: 487
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Valid
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Valid
Private pCod

Local loBrowse,codcor,xobj,rec,Codigo

oPagC = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgComposicao
pCod = crSigCdPro.Cpros

If (This.Value = pCod)
	=MessageBox('Composiçăo Inválida!!!', 0+48, '')
	This.Value = ''
	Return 0
Else
	If Not Empty(This.Value)
		loLista = CreateObject('fwBuscaExt', ThisForm.poDataMgr.pnIdConn, 'SigCdPro', ;
							   'CrListaRemota', 'CPros', This.Value, 'Seleçăo', .t.)

		If Not loLista.plAchouRegistro
			loLista.mAddColuna('CPros', '', 'Código')
			loLista.mAddColuna('DPros', '', 'Descriçăo')
			loLista.Show()
		EndIf

		If (CrListaRemota.CPros = pCod)
			=MessageBox('Composiçăo Inválida !!',0+48,'')
			Use In CrListaRemota
			This.Value = ''
			Return 0
		Else
			lcQuery = [Select * ] + ;
					    [From SigCdPro ] + ;
					   [Where CPros = '] + CrListaRemota.CPros + [']

			If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'CrListaRemota') < 1)
				=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (GrdCons - 2)')
				Return 0
			EndIf
			Go Top In CrListaRemota

			If (CrListaRemota.Varias = 1)
				With oPagC.Get_MatP
					.Value = Iif(Not Empty(CrListaRemota.Cproeqs),CrListaRemota.Cproeqs,CrListaRemota.Cpros)
					.Refresh
				EndWith
			EndIf
		EndIf
	EndIf
	This.Parent.Parent.Refresh
EndIf
* Fim *********************************************************************************

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE When
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE When
Return .f.

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE GotFocus
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE GotFocus
This.Tag = This.Value
ENDPROC


================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGCDPRO.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.PgDadosConsP.GrdCons.Column2.Text1
* Classe: textbox (Base: textbox)
* Registro: 489
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE GotFocus
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE GotFocus
This.Tag = This.Value
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE When
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE When
Return .f.

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Valid
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Valid
Local loBrowse, CodCor, xObj, Rec

oPagC = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgComposicao

pDes = crSigCdPro.Dpros

If (This.Value = pDes)
	=MessageBox('Composiçăo Inválida!!!', 0+48, '')
	This.Value = ''
	Return 0
Else
	If Not Empty(This.Value)
		loLista = CreateObject('fwBuscaExt', ThisForm.poDataMgr.pnIdConn, 'SigCdPro', ;
							   'CrListaRemota', 'DPros', This.Value, 'Seleçăo', .t.)

		If Not loLista.plAchouRegistro
			loLista.mAddColuna('DPros', '', 'Descriçăo')
			loLista.mAddColuna('CPros', '', 'Código')
			loLista.Show()
		EndIf
		
		If (CrListaRemota.DPros = pDes)
			=MessageBox('Composiçăo Inválida !!',0+48,'')
			Use In CrListaRemota
			This.Value = ''
			Return 0
		Else
			lcQuery = [Select * ] + ;
					    [From SigCdPro ] + ;
					   [Where CPros = '] + CrListaRemota.CPros + [']

			If (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, 'CrListaRemota') < 1)
				=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (GrdCons - 1)')
				Return 0
			EndIf
			Go Top In CrListaRemota

			ThisForm.AlterouCompo = .t.
		EndIf
		
		Replace Cgrus  	  With CrListaRemota.Cgrus,;
				Compos    With CrListaRemota.Compos, ;
				OrdCompos With CrListaRemota.OrdCompos, ;
				Dtmovs 	  With DateTime() In crSigPrCpo

		If (CrListaRemota.Varias = 1)
			With oPagC.Get_MatP
				.Value = Iif(Not Empty(CrListaRemota.Cproeqs),CrListaRemota.Cproeqs,CrListaRemota.Cpros)
				.Refresh
			EndWith
		EndIf
	EndIf
	This.Parent.Parent.Refresh
EndIf
* Fim *********************************************************************************

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE When
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE When
This.Tag = This.Value
Return(Inlist(ThisForm.pcEscolha, 'INSERIR', 'ALTERAR'))
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Valid
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Valid
Local xBrow, lCod, lFan, xObj
Private lcDopes, lcDopeSTrfs

Select CrSigCdPrf
Locate For Grupos = This.Value And Ordems = CrSigPrCpo.Ordems
If (Not IsEmpty(This.Value) And This.Value <> This.Tag) &&Or Eof('CrSigCdPrf')

	Select crSigCdPrf
	LOCATE FOR Grupos = This.Value
	lnOrdem = Ordems
	This.Value = This.Value + Str(lnOrdem,2)
	
	xBrow = CreateObject('fwBuscaInt','crSigCdPrf','GrpOrdem',This.Value,'Seleçăo',.t.)
	xBrow.mAddColuna('Grupos','','Código',.t.)
	xBrow.mAddColuna('Descrs','','Descriçăo',.t.)
	xBrow.mAddColuna('Ordems','99','O',.t.)
	xBrow.Show

	Select crSigPrCpo
	Replace crSigPrCpo.Dscgrp With crSigCdPrf.Descrs
	Replace crSigPrCpo.Ordems With crSigCdPrf.Ordems

	This.Value                             = Evaluate('crSigCdPrf.Grupos')
	This.Parent.Parent.Column5.Text1.Value = Evaluate('crSigCdPrf.Descrs')
	This.Parent.Parent.Column6.Text1.Value = Evaluate('crSigCdPrf.Ordems')
	
	This.Refresh
	This.Parent.Parent.Column5.Text1.Refresh
	This.Parent.Parent.Column6.Text1.Refresh
EndIf

ENDPROC


================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGCDPRO.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.PgDadosConsP.GrdCons.Column5.Text1
* Classe: textbox (Base: textbox)
* Registro: 495

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Valid
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Valid
Local xBrow, lCod, lFan, xObj
Private lcDopes, lcDopeSTrfs

If Not IsEmpty(This.Value) And Lastkey() <> 27

	Select crSigCdPrf
	LOCATE FOR Descrs = This.Value
	
	If EOF()
		xBrow = CreateObject('fwBuscaInt','crSigCdPrf','Descrs',This.Value,'Seleçăo',.t.)
		xBrow.mAddColuna('Descrs','','Descriçăo',.t.)
		xBrow.mAddColuna('Grupos','','Código',.t.)
		xBrow.mAddColuna('Ordems','99','O',.t.)
		xBrow.Show		
	EndIf
	
	Select crSigPrCpo

	Replace crSigPrCpo.Grupos With crSigCdPrf.Grupos
	Replace crSigPrCpo.Ordems With crSigCdPrf.Ordems

	This.Value                             = Iif( LastKey() # 27, Evaluate('crSigCdPrf.Descrs'), '')
	This.Parent.Parent.Column4.Text1.Value = Iif( LastKey() # 27, Evaluate('crSigCdPrf.Grupos'), '')
	This.Parent.Parent.Column6.Text1.Value = Iif( LastKey() # 27, Evaluate('crSigCdPrf.Ordems'), '')
	
	This.Refresh
	This.Parent.Parent.Column4.Text1.Refresh
	This.Parent.Parent.Column6.Text1.Refresh

EndIf

ENDPROC

ENDPROC

PROCEDURE LostFocus
Select crSigPrCpo

If (crSigCdPam.AutComps = 1)
	If Not Empty(crSigPrCpo.Mats)
		ThisForm.TotalGrupoCv
		ThisForm.TotalGrupo
		ThisForm.Totalplan
	EndIf
	
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgComposicao.cmdgCompo.cmdCompoAtualiza.Click

	If (This.Tag <> This.Value)
		ThisForm.AlterouCompo = .t.
	EndIf
	Return
EndIf
* Fim *********************************************************************************

ENDPROC

* OBJETO: SIGCDPRO.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgCusto.grdCompo
* Classe: fwgrade (Base: grid)
* Registro: 510

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE AfterRowColChange
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE AfterRowColChange
Lparameters nColIndex

If ThisForm.TemTipos And ThisForm.TempTipos
	ThisForm.Composiciona = crSigPrCpo.Mats
	ThisForm.FiltrarCompo(2)
EndIf

ThisForm.poDataMgr.CursorQuery([SigCdGrp], [LocalGru], [CGrus], crSigPrCpo.CGrus, [DGrus])
If Not Used([LocalGru])
	=MessageBox([Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!], 16, [Falha na Conexăo (grdCompo - CursorQuery - LocalGru)])
	Return 0
EndIf
ThisForm.Pagina.dados.pgframeDados.pgCusto.getDGruCompos.Value = LocalGru.DGrus
ThisForm.Pagina.dados.pgframeDados.pgCusto.getDGruCompos.Refresh
This.Parent.Get_Desc.Refresh
ENDPROC


================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGCDPRO.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgCusto.grdCompo.Column1.Text1
* Classe: textbox (Base: textbox)
* Registro: 512
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE When
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE When
Return Inlist(ThisForm.pcEscolha, 'INSERIR', 'ALTERAR') and thisform.habilitacompo 

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Valid
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Valid
Private pCod, pGru
Local codcor,xobj,rec,Codigo,loLista

If Not ThisForm.habilitacompo 
	Return .t.
EndIf

lcArq = [crMtPrima]
If ThisForm.TemTipos
	lcArq = [crMtPrimaT]
EndIf

oPagC = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgCusto
pCod  = crSigCdPro.Cpros
lcTip = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgCusto.cmbTipos.Value 
ThisForm.Composiciona = []

If (This.Tag <> This.Value)
	If (This.Value = pCod)
		=MessageBox('Composiçăo Inválida!!!', 0+48, '')
		This.Value = ''
		Return 0
	Else
		Select &lcArq.
		Set Filter To Tipos = lcTip In &lcArq.
		Select crSigCdPro
		If Not Empty(This.Value)
			Keyboard Chr(32) Plain
			lnInkey = Inkey()
			If Not Seek(Padr(This.Value, 14), lcArq, [CPros])
				loBrowse = CreateObject([fwBuscaSel], lcArq, [CPros], Padr(This.Value, 14), [Matéria-Prima])
				loBrowse.AddColuna([CPros], [], [Código], .t., [CPros])
				loBrowse.AddColuna([DPros], [], [Descriçăo], .t., [DPros])
				loBrowse.AddColuna([CGrus], [xxxxxx], [Grupo])
				loBrowse.Show
			EndIf
		
			If LastKey() <> 27
				If (&lcArq..CPros = pCod)
					MessageBox('Composiçăo Inválida !!',0+48,'')
					This.Value = ''
					Select &lcArq.
					Set Filter To
					Return 0
				Else
					ThisForm.Composiciona = &lcArq..CPros
					
					lStrQuery = [Select * ] + ;
								[From SigCdPro ] + ;
								[Where CPros = ']+&lcArq..CPros+[' ]
					If ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lStrQuery,'CrListaRemota') < 1
						=MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (GrdCompo - 1)')
						Select &lcArq.
						Set Filter To
						Return 0
					EndIf
					Go Top In CrListaRemota
				
					With oPagC.grdcompo.Column1.text1
						.Value = CrListaRemota.CPros
						.Refresh
					EndWith
					With oPagC.grdcompo.Column2.text1
						.Value = CrListaRemota.DPros
						.Refresh
					EndWith
					With oPagC.grdcompo.Column3.text1
						If (This.Tag <> CrListaRemota.CPros)
							.Value = CrListaRemota.CUnis
							.Refresh
						EndIf
					EndWith

					Replace CGrus     With CrListaRemota.CGrus, ;
							Dtmovs    With DateTime(), ;
							cUniPs    With CrListaRemota.CUniPs,;
							cIdChaves With fUniqueIds(), ;
							Tipos	  With lcTip In crSigPrCpo

					If (This.Tag <> This.Value)
						With oPagC.grdcompo.Column4.text1
							.Value = CrListaRemota.CustoFs
							.Refresh
						EndWith
						With oPagC.grdcompo.Column7.text1
							.Value = CrListaRemota.Moecusfs
							.Refresh
						EndWith
						With oPagC.grdcompo.Column8.Text1
							lcObs = CrSigPrCpo.ObsCompos &&.Value
							If Not Empty(CrListaRemota.ObsPeds)
								lcObs = CrListaRemota.ObsPeds
							EndIf
							If Not Empty(CrListaRemota.ObsPes)
								lcObs = CrListaRemota.ObsPes
							EndIf
							
							.Value = lcObs
							.Refresh
						EndWith
						ThisForm.AlterouCompo = .t.

						pGru = CrListaRemota.CGrus
						ThisForm.poDataMgr.Requery('crSigCdGrp')
						Go Top In crSigCdGrp
						ThisForm.OrdGrade = Int(Val(Substr(crSigCdGrp.CfgGerGprs, 6, 1)))
						Select CrSigPrCpo
					EndIf

					Replace Compos    With CrListaRemota.Compos, ;
							DtMovs    With DateTime(), ;
							cUniPs    With CrListaRemota.CUniPs,;
							OrdCompos With CrListaRemota.OrdCompos, ;
							Tipos	  With lcTip In crSigPrCpo

					If (CrListaRemota.Varias = 1)
						With oPagC.Get_MatP
							.Value = Iif(Not Empty(CrListaRemota.Cproeqs),CrListaRemota.Cproeqs,CrListaRemota.Cpros)
							.Refresh
						EndWith
					EndIf 
				EndIf 
				Use In CrListaRemota
			Else
				This.Value = ''
				Select &lcArq.
				Set Filter To
				Return 0
			EndIf	
			This.Refresh
		EndIf
	EndIf
	Select &lcArq.
	Set Filter To

	Select crSigPrCpo
	ThisForm.CalcFornec(crSigPrCpo.Mats)
EndIf

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE GotFocus
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE GotFocus
This.Tag = This.Value
ENDPROC


================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGCDPRO.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgCusto.grdCompo.Column2.Text1
* Classe: textbox (Base: textbox)
* Registro: 514

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE GotFocus
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE GotFocus
This.Tag = This.Value

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Valid
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Valid
Private pCod, pGru, pDes
Local loLista

If Not ThisForm.HabilitaCompo 
	Return .t.
EndIf

lcArq = [crMtPrima]
If ThisForm.TemTipos
	lcArq = [crMtPrimaT]
EndIf

oPagC = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgCusto
lcTip = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgCusto.cmbTipos.Value 
ThisForm.Composiciona = []

pCod = crSigCdPro.Cpros
pDes = crSigCdPro.Dpros

If (This.Tag <> This.Value)
	If (This.Value = pDes)
		=MessageBox('Composiçăo Inválida !!',0+48,'')
		This.Value = ''
		Return 0
	Else
		Select &lcArq.
		Set Filter To Tipos = lcTip In &lcArq.
		Select crSigCdPro
		If Not Empty(This.Value)
			Keyboard Chr(32) Plain
			Inkey()
			Select &lcArq.
		    Set Near On
			If Not Seek(Padr(This.Value, 40), lcArq, [DPros])
				loLista = CreateObject([fwBuscaSel], lcArq, [DPros], Padr(This.Value, 65), [Matéria Prima])
				loLista.AddColuna([DPros], [], 	     [Descriçăo], .t., [DPros])
				loLista.AddColuna([CPros], [], 	     [Código], .t., [CPros])
				loLista.AddColuna([CGrus], [xxxxxx], [Grupo])
				loLista.Show()
			EndIf
			Set Near Off

			If (Lastkey() <> 27)
				If (&lcArq..DPros = pDes)
					=MessageBox([Composiçăo Inválida!!!], 0+48, [])
					This.Value = []
					Select &lcArq.
					Set Filter To
					Return 0
				Else
					ThisForm.Composiciona = &lcArq..CPros 
					
					lStrQuery = [Select * ] + ;
								  [From SigCdPro ] + ;
								 [Where CPros = '] + &lcArq..CPros + [']

					If ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lStrQuery, [crListaRemota]) < 1
						MessageBox('Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!', 16, 'Falha na Conexăo (GrdCompo - 2)')
						Select &lcArq.
						Set Filter To
						Return 0
					EndIf
					Go Top In CrListaRemota
					With oPagC.grdcompo.Column1.text1
						.Value = CrListaRemota.Cpros
						.refresh
					EndWith
					With oPagC.grdcompo.Column2.text1
						.Value = CrListaRemota.Dpros
						.refresh
					EndWith
					With oPagC.grdcompo.Column3.text1
						If (This.Tag <> CrListaRemota.Cpros)
							.Value = CrListaRemota.Cunis
							.refresh
						EndIf
					EndWith

					Replace CGrus     With CrListaRemota.CGrus, ;
							Dtmovs    With DateTime(), ;
							cUniPs    With CrListaRemota.CUniPs,;
							cIdChaves With fUniqueIds(), ;
							Tipos	  With lcTip In crSigPrCpo

					If (This.Tag <> This.Value)
						With oPagC.grdcompo.Column4.text1
							.Value = CrListaRemota.CustoFs
							.Refresh
						EndWith
						With oPagC.grdcompo.Column7.text1
							.Value = CrListaRemota.Moecusfs
							.Refresh
						EndWith
						With oPagC.grdcompo.Column8.Text1
							lcObs = CrSigPrCpo.ObsCompos &&.Value
							If Not Empty(CrListaRemota.ObsPeds)
								lcObs = CrListaRemota.ObsPeds
							EndIf
							If Not Empty(CrListaRemota.ObsPes)
								lcObs = CrListaRemota.ObsPes
							EndIf
							
							.Value = lcObs
							.Refresh
						EndWith
						ThisForm.AlterouCompo = .t.

						pGru = CrListaRemota.CGrus
						ThisForm.poDataMgr.Requery('crSigCdGrp')
						Go Top In crSigCdGrp
						ThisForm.OrdGrade = Int(Val(Substr(crSigCdGrp.CfgGerGprs, 6, 1)))
						Select CrSigPrCpo
					EndIf
		
					Replace Compos    With CrListaRemota.Compos, ;
							DtMovs    With DateTime(), ;
							cUniPs    With CrListaRemota.CUniPs,;
							OrdCompos With CrListaRemota.OrdCompos, ;
							Tipos	  With lcTip In crSigPrCpo

					If (CrListaRemota.Varias = 1)
						With oPagC.Get_MatP
							.Value = Iif(Not Empty(CrListaRemota.Cproeqs),CrListaRemota.Cproeqs,CrListaRemota.Cpros)
							.Refresh
						EndWith
					EndIf 
				EndIf 
				Use In CrListaRemota
			Else
				This.Value = ''
				Select &lcArq.
				Set Filter To
				Return 0
			EndIf	
			This.Refresh
		EndIf
	EndIf
	Select &lcArq.
	Set Filter To

	Select crSigPrCpo
	ThisForm.CalcFornec(crSigPrCpo.Mats)
EndIf
* Fim **************************************************************************************
ENDPROC

PROCEDURE When

================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGCDPRO.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgCusto.grdCompo.Column11.Text1
* Classe: textbox (Base: textbox)
* Registro: 532
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE When
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE When
Local m.retorno
m.Retorno = .f.
If Not IsEmpty(CrSigPrCpo.UniCompos)
	lcSql = [Select cEstos From SigCdUni Where cunis = ']+CrSigPrCpo.UniCompos+[']
	ThisForm.Podatamgr.Sqlexecute(lcsql,'TmpUni')
	If TmpUni.cEstos = '3' And Not IsEmpty(CrSigPrCpo.cUniPs)
		m.Retorno = .t.
	EndIf
EndIf
Return Inlist(ThisForm.pcEscolha, 'INSERIR', 'ALTERAR') and thisform.habilitacompo And m.retorno

ENDPROC

* Classe: commandgroup (Base: commandgroup)
* Registro: 539

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE cmdCompoInserir.Click
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE cmdCompoInserir.Click
Local obrow, mater

oPagC = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgCusto

If InList(ThisForm.pcEscolha, 'INSERIR', 'ALTERAR')
	lcTip = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgCusto.cmbTipos.Value 

	Select crSigPrCpo
	Go Top In crSigPrCpo
	Locate For Empty(Mats)
	If Eof([crSigPrCpo])
		Insert Into crSigPrCpo (Cpros, DtMovs, cIdChaves, Tipos) Values (crSigCdPro.Cpros, DateTime(), fUniqueIds(), lcTip)
	EndIf

	obrow = oPagC.grdCompo
	obrow.Refresh
	obrow.Column1.SetFocus
EndIf
If ThisForm.TemTipos And ThisForm.TempTipos
	ThisForm.FiltrarCompo(2)
EndIf
* Fim *********************************************************************************
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE cmdCompoIexcluir.Click
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE cmdCompoIexcluir.Click
If InList(ThisForm.pcEscolha, 'INSERIR', 'ALTERAR')
	Select crSigPrCpo
	If Not Eof()
		Delete
	EndIf
	
	If Not Eof()
		Skip 
		Skip - 1
	EndIf 
	Go Bottom
	
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgCusto.grdCompo.SetFocus
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgFrameDados.pgCusto.grdCompo.Refresh

	If ThisForm.TemTipos And ThisForm.TempTipos
		ThisForm.FiltrarCompo(2)
	EndIf
EndIf
* Fim *********************************************************************************

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE LostFocus
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE LostFocus
If Not Empty(This.Value) And (Lastkey()=13)
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDesigner.getObsTarefas.SetFocus
EndIf
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE When
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE When
Return InList(ThisForm.pcEscolha, [INSERIR], [ALTERAR]) And (crSigPrTar.Usuars = Usuar) And IsEmpty(crSigPrTar.DtFims)
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Valid
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Valid
Local loLista

If Not Empty(This.Value)
	Select crTarefas
	Go Top In crTarefas
	Locate For CodCads = Padr(This.Value, 10)
	If Eof([crTarefas])
		loLista = CreateObject([fwBuscaInt], [crTarefas], [CodCads], This.Value, [Tarefas], .t.)
		loLista.mAddColuna([CodCads], [], [Tarefas],   .t.)
		loLista.mAddColuna([DesCads], [], [Descriçăo], .t.)
		loLista.Show()
	EndIf
	This.Value 		 = Iif(Lastkey()=27, [], crTarefas.CodCads)
	This.ToolTipText = Iif(Lastkey()=27, [], crTarefas.DesCads)
EndIf
* Fim **************************************************************************************
ENDPROC

================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGCDPRO.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDesigner.btnIniTarefa
* Classe: fwbtng (Base: commandbutton)
* Registro: 563
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE When
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE When
Return InList(ThisForm.pcEscolha, [INSERIR], [ALTERAR])
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Click
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Click
Select crSigPrTar
Go Top In crSigPrTar
Locate For Usuars = Usuar And IsEmpty(DtFims)
If Not Eof([crSigPrTar])
	=MessageBox([Existe Uma Tarefa Năo Encerrada Para Esse Usuário!!!], 0+16, [Atençăo!!!])
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDesigner.grdDesigner.Column4.SetFocus
	Return .f.
EndIf

Select crSigPrTar
Go Top In crSigPrTar
Locate For Usuars = Usuar And Empty(Tarefas)
If Not Eof([crSigPrTar])
	=MessageBox([Existe Uma Tarefa Ainda Năo Informada!!!], 0+16, [Atençăo!!!])
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDesigner.grdDesigner.Column4.SetFocus
	Return .f.
EndIf

ltDat = ThisForm.poDataMgr.GetDatetime()

Insert Into crSigPrTar (CPros, pkChaves, DtInis, Usuars) ;
				Values (crSigCdPro.CPros, fUniqueIds(), ltDat, Usuar)

ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDesigner.grdDesigner.Column4.SetFocus
* Fim **************************************************************************************
ENDPROC


================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGCDPRO.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDesigner.btnFimTarefa
* Classe: fwbtng (Base: commandbutton)
* Registro: 564
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE When
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE When
Return InList(ThisForm.pcEscolha, [INSERIR], [ALTERAR])
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Click
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Click
If (crSigPrTar.Usuars <> Usuar)
	=MessageBox([Essa Tarefa Năo Pertence a Esse Usuário!!!], 0+16, [Atençăo!!!])
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDesigner.grdDesigner.Column4.SetFocus
	Return .f.
EndIf

If Not IsEmpty(crSigPrTar.DtFims)
	=MessageBox([Essa Tarefa Já Se Encontra Finalizada!!!], 0+16, [Atençăo!!!])
	ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDesigner.grdDesigner.Column4.SetFocus
	Return .f.
EndIf

ltDat = ThisForm.poDataMgr.GetDatetime()

Replace DtFims With ltDat In crSigPrTar

ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDesigner.grdDesigner.Column4.SetFocus
* Fim **************************************************************************************
ENDPROC


================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGCDPRO.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDesigner.grdArquivos
* Classe: fwgrade (Base: grid)
* Registro: 565
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE AfterRowColChange
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE AfterRowColChange
Lparameters nColIndex

Local lcArq

lcArq = Alltrim(crSigPrArq.Arquivos)

With ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.pgframeDados.pgDesigner
	Clear Resources
	.imgArqJpg.Picture = []
	.imgArqJpg.Visible = .f.

	If Not Empty(lcArq) And InList(Alltrim(Upper(Substr(lcArq, At([.],lcArq), 5))), [.JPG], [.ICO], [.BMP], [.JPEG])
		.imgArqJpg.Picture = (lcArq)
		.imgArqJpg.Visible = .t.
	EndIf
EndWith
* Fim ********************************************************************************* 

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Click
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Click
Local lcArq

lcArq = Alltrim(crSigPrArq.Arquivos)

If Not Empty(lcArq) And File(lcArq)
	loApp = CreateObject([Shell.Application])
	loApp.Open(lcArq)
Else
	=MessageBox([Arquivo Năo Encontrado!!!], 0+16, [Atençăo!!!])
	Return .f.
EndIf
* Fim **************************************************************************************
ENDPROC

PROCEDURE DblClick
Local lcArq

lcArq = Alltrim(crSigPrArq.Arquivos)

If Not Empty(lcArq) And File(lcArq) And InList(Alltrim(Upper(Substr(lcArq, At([.],lcArq), 5))), [.JPG], [.ICO], [.BMP], [.JPEG])
	Do Form SigOpZom With lcArq, [Arquivo : ] + lcArq
EndIf
* Fim *********************************************************************************

ENDPROC


================================================================================
* OBJETO: SIGCDPRO.Pagina.Dados.Optiongroup1
* Classe: optiongroup (Base: optiongroup)
* Registro: 572
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE InteractiveChange
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE InteractiveChange
Do Case
	Case ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.optiongroup1.Value = 1 && Principal
		ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.PgFrameDados.ActivePage = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.PgFrameDados.pgDados.PageOrder

	Case ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.optiongroup1.Value = 2 && Componente
		ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.PgFrameDados.ActivePage = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.PgFrameDados.pgComposicao.PageOrder

	Case ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.optiongroup1.Value = 3 && Custos
		ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.PgFrameDados.ActivePage = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.PgFrameDados.pgCusto.PageOrder
		
	Case ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.optiongroup1.Value = 4 && Fiscal
		ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.PgFrameDados.ActivePage = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.PgFrameDados.pgDadosFiscais.PageOrder

	Case ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.optiongroup1.Value = 5 && Processos
		ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.PgFrameDados.ActivePage = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.PgFrameDados.pgDadosFaseP.PageOrder

	Case ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.optiongroup1.Value = 6 && Consumo
		ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.PgFrameDados.ActivePage = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.PgFrameDados.pgDadosConsP.PageOrder

	Case ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.optiongroup1.Value = 7 && Designer
		ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.PgFrameDados.ActivePage = ThisForm.Pagina.Dados.PgFrameDados.pgDesigner.PageOrder
EndCase

ENDPROC
